# PROGRESS-HISTORY.md έΑΦ Marham Patti (append-only archive)

> **This is the COMPLETE, append-only archive** of every finished build-step, newest at the top. The agent appends the FULL entry here as part of finishing each step (see PROGRESS.md recording protocol). Read this file **only when recovering an older step's detail** έΑΦ never cover-to-cover. The SHORT rolling tracker is **PROGRESS.md**.
>
> **Entry format (per step):** `## Build-step NN έΑΦ <title>` then: work-type (FEATURE/FIX), phase label, branch, dependency note, schema/migration/RLS/auth/permission/**feature-flag** impact, problem, what changed (data model, endpoints, UI Simple/Pro, **flags exposed**, i18n keys), and ALL verification-gate numbers (typecheck, lint, turbo build, jest `N/N (S suites; +X)`, i18n parity, isolation, **flag/vertical smoke**, **performance/Lighthouse**, white-label).

> **Numbering:** canonical per ARCHITECTURE.md ┬π14 (continuous 1έΗΤN; phase = label).

## Build-step 48 έΑΦ Platform Settlement & Commission (`feature/48-platform-settlement`) έεΖ DONE (2026-07-11)

**WORK TYPE:** FEATURE. **Phase 5 / item 4** (the money layer of the marketplace foundation tranche 45έΗΤ48). **Depends on** 47 (marketplace transactions exist), 46 (platform-scope RLS + `runWithPlatformScope`), 23/21 (tenant accounting + cashier έΑΦ untouched underneath). **Spec:** `specs/48-platform-settlement.md` (+ `specs/45-53-CODEREF.md` ┬πB.48/┬πC.4). **έγιΎ╕Π Ends with the MANDATORY owner-verification HALT (┬π6) έΑΦ `[HUMAN_REQUIRED]`, NOT `[CHECKPOINT]`.**

### Problem
Marketplace bookings (47) move money two ways, foodpanda-style έΑΦ (a) patient pays ONLINE έΗΤ the platform collects, keeps commission, owes the tenant the rest; (b) patient pays CASH at the facility έΗΤ the tenant collects and owes the platform its commission. Neither a platform-level ledger nor a payment abstraction existed, and the real gateway (JazzCash/Easypaisa/card) is undecided, so the design had to be provider-agnostic. This is the PLATFORM's books, ABOVE and SEPARATE from tenant accounting (23).

### What changed
**New package `@mp/payments` (provider-agnostic port).** `PaymentProvider` interface (`initiate`/`confirm`/`sign`/`verifyWebhook`/`refund`) + a deterministic `MockProvider` (no network, no randomness: HMAC-signed webhooks, success unless the ref contains `fail`). `getPaymentProvider({provider,mockSecret})` is the ONLY construction seam έΑΦ two named variants (`mock`, `mock-alt`) prove config swaps the adapter with zero code change. No concrete gateway/SDK anywhere (do-not-break #5). Config: `PAYMENT_PROVIDER` (`mock|mock-alt`) + `PAYMENT_MOCK_SECRET` (zod, defaults; `.env.example`).

**Schema έΑΦ new PLATFORM-LEVEL settlement section** (migration `20260711120000_platform_settlement`):
- `PayMethod += PLATFORM_ONLINE` (additive; tenant records the online remittance in its OWN books as income like `ONLINE` έΑΦ commission never touches tenant GL). Mirrored in `@mp/shared` `PayMethodLit`/`PAY_METHODS` + `billMethod_PLATFORM_ONLINE` i18n label.
- `PlatformLedgerEntry` (append-only header; `@@unique([sourceType, sourceRefId])` = the idempotency key) + balanced `PlatformLedgerPosting` lines (accounts `PLATFORM_CASH`/`TENANT_PAYABLE`/`TENANT_RECEIVABLE`/`COMMISSION_REVENUE`).
- `PlatformCommissionConfig` (tenant/per-capability/default; NULL tenant_id = platform-wide default). `PaymentIntent` (online-collect lifecycle; unique `providerRef`). `SettlementRun` (+ `SettlementLine` snapshot).
- **RLS** reuses the 46 `apply_platform_link_rls` on every table: a tenant reads ONLY its own tenant_id rows; the platform scope (`runWithPlatformScope`) reads/writes all and is the SOLE writer; a tenant can never forge a posting (WITH CHECK platform-scope-only). **APPEND-ONLY** enforced by a DB trigger `platform_ledger_append_only()` that raises on UPDATE/DELETE of the ledger tables. New `@mp/db` enum exports.

**API έΑΦ `apps/api/src/platform-settlement/`:**
- `PlatformLedgerService` έΑΦ the ONLY writer of `PlatformLedgerEntry`; posts are balanced (`isBalanced`) + idempotent (skip if `(sourceType,sourceRefId)` exists). Balances are always computed FROM the entries (`balanceFromEntries`), never stored mutably.
- `CommissionService` έΑΦ resolves the rate with precedence tenant+capability έΗΤ tenant default έΗΤ platform default έΗΤ hard `DEFAULT_COMMISSION_PCT` floor.
- `PlatformSettlementService` έΑΦ the orchestrator: **online** `initiateOnlineCheckout` (derive commission, `provider.initiate`, store PENDING intent) έΗΤ `confirmOnlinePayment`/`handleWebhook` (verify signature; on confirm records the tenant payment via the tenant's OWN `BillingService` έΑΦ OTHER-source invoice + `pay(PLATFORM_ONLINE)` έΑΦ then posts `PLATFORM_CASHέΗΣ/COMMISSIONέΗΣ/TENANT_PAYABLEέΗΣ`; idempotent on intent status + ledger key + billing offline seam); `refundOnlinePayment` reverses the postings. **cash** `accrueCashCommission` posts `TENANT_RECEIVABLEέΗΣ` (tenant cashier flow untouched). **settlement** `createRun` freezes the outstanding statement, `markSettled` posts the balancing SETTLEMENT entry (payable+receivable έΗΤ 0) with a reference. Pure money math isolated in `settlement.math.ts`.
- Controllers: tenant `SettlementController` (`/settlement/statement|runs`, flag `platform.marketplace` + new `settlement.view` permission, RLS-own reads); `PlatformSettlementAdminController` (`/platform/settlement/*`, SUPER_ADMIN cross-tenant balances/statement/runs/commission/refund έΑΦ the API 50's console consumes); `CheckoutController` (platform-auth `POST /platform/marketplace/checkout/:providerRef/confirm` + `@Public` signature-verified `POST /platform/marketplace/checkout/webhook`). Every money mutation audited (06).

**47 booking seam.** `paymentMode` (`PAY_AT_FACILITY`|`PLATFORM_ONLINE`, default cash) added to the three booking DTOs + `BookingResult` (`checkout?`). The booking orchestrator computes gross (doctor fee / ╬μ test prices / ╬μ item price├Ωqty from the published projections έΑΦ `publishedDoctor/Tests/Products` selects extended to carry price) and, AFTER creating the tenant order, either starts an online checkout or accrues cash commission via the settlement service. Forks nothing.

**Web.** Tenant SettingsέΗΤSettlement island (`SettlementClient`) έΑΦ read-only statement (payable/receivable/net + itemised entries + settlement runs), degrades to a clean no-access state; wired into `(app)/settings`. New `settlement.*` i18n keys EN+UR (parity) + `billMethod_PLATFORM_ONLINE`.

### Permissions / flags
New TENANT permission `settlement.view` (granted ADMIN + FINANCE; TENANT_OWNER via full-tenant default). Commission applies to `platform.marketplace`-sourced transactions only. No new feature flag (rides the 47 marketplace flag).

### Verification gates
- **typecheck:** 29/29 packages green.
- **lint:** clean (0 errors; design-drift check passes; 1 pre-existing unrelated warning in doctor-portal).
- **test:** api **920/920 (79 suites; +16** new `platform-settlement.spec`: balanced postings, per-tenant balance, commission precedence, online confirm + webhook-replay idempotency, forged-signature reject, failed-confirm, cash accrual + idempotency, run freeze + mark-settled + idempotency, refund reversal, provider swap**)**; db **231/231 (39 suites; +10** new `platform-settlement-isolation.spec` against the REAL 01έΗΤ48 migrations in pglite: tenant reads OWN ledger/postings/runs/intents only, NULL-tenant default commission invisible to a tenant, platform scope reads all, tenant cannot forge a posting even for itself, platform-scope append works, ledger APPEND-ONLY (UPDATE+DELETE denied), fail-closed, `PLATFORM_ONLINE` enum present**)** έΑΦ EXTENDS the 46/47 Ganatra floor to money. i18n parity EN+UR green (settlement keys + billMethod).
- **build:** `turbo build` web + api green; public `/discover` unchanged (202 KB), `/settings` 204 KB έΑΦ both < 250 KB budget (perf budget holds; no public surface added).
- **isolation:** the Ganatra test holds for the platform ledger έΑΦ a tenant never sees a sibling's balance/relationship; the platform never writes tenant GL beyond the tenant's own billing recording; tenant accounting (23) + shift math (21) untouched.
- **audit:** every money mutation (checkout, confirm, refund, cash accrual, run created/settled, commission set) writes an audit row.
- **provider-agnostic:** no gateway SDK/strings outside `@mp/payments`; provider is env config; swap proven with two mock variants.

### Notes / owner-verification HALT (┬π6)
This ends the 45έΗΤ48 marketplace-foundation tranche. The next-step pointer is set to **HOLD** έΑΦ 49+ build ONLY after the owner re-points PROGRESS.md to `specs/49-field-pools.md` and sends START/RESUME. Owner checklist: **privacy wall** (a platform patient linked to two tenants sees ONE merged timeline; tenant-1 staff never see her tenant-2 records), **marketplace** (browse logged-out; book a doctor + a lab test (home collection) + a pharmacy order across THREE tenants, all land tenant-side with marketplace badges), **money** (one online mock payment έΗΤ tenant payable = gross έΙΤ commission; one cash payment έΗΤ commission receivable; statements itemise both; ledger balances), **look** (Inter + light surfaces + skeletons across dashboard + all four entrances). The full online + cash flows are proven at the service + DB level; end-to-end money can be driven via `POST /platform/marketplace/book/*` with `paymentMode:"PLATFORM_ONLINE"` έΗΤ `/checkout/:providerRef/confirm`. The public discover booking UI keeps its pay-at-facility default (the `PLATFORM_ONLINE` seam is wired in the API/DTO; a discover-side online-pay affordance is deferred to keep the public bundle within budget έΑΦ noted so it is not mistaken for complete).

WORK TYPE: FEATURE (branch feature/48-platform-settlement). Ended with `[HUMAN_REQUIRED]` per spec ┬π6 έΑΦ the controller records PROGRESS and HOLDS (no auto-merge past this point until the owner verifies).

## Build-step 47 έΑΦ Marketplace Discovery & Booking

- **Work-type:** FEATURE. **Phase 5 / item 3 έΑΦ the foodpanda surface.** Branch `feature/47-marketplace-discovery`.
- **Depends on:** 46 (platform identity: `runWithPlatformScope`, `PatientLink`, `PlatformAuthGuard`, `PlatformAccountService`), 45 (design/skeletons/empty-states), 05 (flags/presets), 15/19/25/34 (the tenant services the booking orchestrates). Spec `specs/47-marketplace-discovery.md` + companion `specs/45-53-CODEREF.md`.
- **Schema/migration/RLS/permission/flag impact:** Migration `20260711110000_marketplace_discovery`. NEW marketplace section of the Prisma schema (published-copy tables). A **THIRD RLS primitive `apply_marketplace_rls`** (mirror of the 46 helpers): tenant reads+writes ONLY its own rows; the platform scope reads ALL (discovery); WRITES are tenant-owned (WITH CHECK `tenant_id = current`) so the platform can never forge a listing. Additive enums: `ApptSource += MARKETPLACE`; new `OrderSource {DIRECT, MARKETPLACE}` on `LabOrder` + `OnlineOrder` (default DIRECT έΑΦ no backfill). New TENANT permission `marketplace.manage` (granted to TENANT_OWNER + ADMIN). Flag `platform.marketplace` (already added, group `platform`) gates tenant participation. No existing RLS policy weakened; no staff/tenant flow forked.

### Problem
A platform account (46) is useless without somewhere to go. A patient must browse the WHOLE platform έΑΦ clinics, doctors, lab tests, medicines with prices έΑΦ and book/order from ANY tenant, including ones she has never visited (link created on first booking). Tenants are different verticals (Ganatra = Full; a standalone pharmacy has no doctors; a standalone lab has no POS), so discovery must adapt per preset and only ever show what a tenant has PUBLISHED. Critically, none of this may leak cross-tenant relationships (the Ganatra test extends from 46 to discovery/booking).

### What changed
- **Data model (published-copy, NOT live-table exposure):** `MarketplaceListing` (one per tenant: display name, city/area, services summary, logo key, open hours JSON, `ListingStatus DRAFT|PUBLISHED`, publishedAt) + `MarketplaceDoctor` / `MarketplaceTest` / `MarketplaceProduct` projections, each carrying `tenantId` + a `source*Id` back-reference and a per-row `published` toggle. Discovery reads ONLY these tables, so tenant internals (stock, costs, other patients) can never leak. `@@unique([listingId, source*Id])` makes the projection sync idempotent.
- **RLS:** `apply_marketplace_rls` installed on all four tables. Discovery runs under `runWithPlatformScope` (reads all published copies); publication runs under `runWithTenant` (tenant owns its rows). Proven leak-proof in the DB suite below.
- **API έΑΦ `apps/api/src/marketplace/`:** (1) **Publication** (`MarketplacePublicationService` + controller `/marketplace/listing`, staff-guarded, `@RequireFeature(platform.marketplace)` + `@RequirePermission(marketplace.manage)`): get config, save display fields, capability-aware `refresh` (projects the tenant's LIVE doctors/tests/medicines via the tenant services έΑΦ doctors only if `clinic.appointments`, tests only if `lab.catalog`, products only if `pharmacy.online`; home-collection availability from `lab.homeCollection`), per-row publish toggle, and whole-tenant publish/unpublish έΑΦ all audited. (2) **Discovery** (`MarketplaceDiscoveryService` + `@Public` controller `/marketplace/discover` + `/marketplace/tenant/:slug`): platform-scoped read-only search (SQL/ILIKE across listing + published projections; filters q/city/home-collection) with a defence-in-depth flag cross-check (a tenant with `platform.marketplace` off appears NOWHERE even if a stale listing is still PUBLISHED). (3) **Booking orchestrator** (`MarketplaceBookingService` + platform-authenticated controller `/platform/marketplace/book/{appointment,lab,pharmacy}` via the exported `PlatformAuthGuard`): validates the PATIENT session + that the item is actually published, **link-if-firsts** (find-or-create the tenant-local Patient by the account's OWN phone via new `PatientService.findOrCreateByPhone`, then `PlatformAccountService.ensureMarketplaceLink` έΑΦ claim-safe: existing record reused, link idempotent, audited in the tenant), then invokes the SAME tenant service staff use (15 appointments / 19 lab / 25 home-collection / 34 online-pharmacy) under its own `runWithTenant`, stamped `source: MARKETPLACE`, and audits the booking. **Forks nothing** έΑΦ the tenant services gained only additive optional seams: `source?` on appointment/lab/home-collection create inputs, and `patientId?`+`source?` on `placeOrder` (a cross-tenant buyer has no tenant `User`, so the resolved patientId is passed directly; `createdBy`/`actorId` are plain-string audit columns, never FKs, so the `mkt:<platformUserId>` actor is safe). Payment recorded pay-at-facility this step; a `paymentMode` seam is reserved for 48.
- **Web:** patient **Browse** tab added to the `(platform)` app (search έΗΤ tenant cards έΗΤ profile panel έΗΤ one-tap book/order, calling the platform-scoped booking endpoints); **public** `/discover` + `/discover/[slug]` (server shell + one light island, plain-fetch the read-only feed, "sign in to book" CTA έΑΦ booking gated behind a platform session); tenant **Settings έΗΤ Marketplace** island (edit face, sync catalog, toggle projections, publish). All surfaces EN+UR + RTL, skeletons + empty states (45); `/discover` added to `lighthouserc.json`.
- **i18n:** new `marketplace.*` namespace (64 keys) added to BOTH en.json + ur.json (parity gate green).
- **Seed (staging-gated):** `seed-demo.ts` extended έΑΦ Ganatra publishes its listing + a doctor; two NEW standalone tenants created with published listings + projected catalogs and the participation flag on: **MedLife Pharmacy** (`medlife-pharmacy`, preset `pharmacy`, 3 medicines + stock) and **CityLab Diagnostics** (`citylab-diagnostics`, preset `lab`, home-collection on, 3 tests). Idempotent (stable `d_*` ids); baseline `seed.ts` untouched; `buildDemoPlan` invariants unaffected (separate path).

### Verification gates (all green)
- **Typecheck:** `@mp/api` έεΥ, `@mp/web` έεΥ (+ `@mp/shared`/`@mp/db` build έεΥ, `prisma generate` έεΥ, `prisma validate` έεΥ).
- **Lint:** api `eslint` 0 errors (1 pre-existing unrelated warning); web `eslint` έεΥ + **design-drift-check έεΥ** (migrated Settings inputs to `@mp/ui <Input>`).
- **Build:** api `tsc` έεΥ; web `next build` έεΥ έΑΦ public `/discover` = **202 kB** First-Load JS and `/discover/[slug]` = 202 kB, both **< 250 KB script budget**.
- **Jest έΑΦ DB:** **221/221 (38 suites; +9)** incl. new `marketplace-isolation.spec.ts` έΑΦ the Ganatra floor for discovery: a tenant sees ONLY its own listing/projections, never a sibling's; the platform scope reads all; a tenant cannot forge another tenant's listing; the platform scope CANNOT insert a listing (publication is tenant-owned); fail-closed with no context; `lab_orders`/`online_orders.source` columns exist. Runs the REAL migrations 01έΗΤ47 in pglite (also proves the migration applies cleanly, incl. `ALTER TYPE ADD VALUE`).
- **Jest έΑΦ API:** **904/904 (78 suites; +10)** incl. new `marketplace.spec.ts` έΑΦ link-if-first find-or-creates patient+link then reuses on a second booking (no duplicate); every booking stamps `source: MARKETPLACE`; cannot book an unpublished doctor/test or a flag-off tenant (negatives); only PATIENT accounts may book; home-collection routes through the 25 service; pharmacy passes the resolved patientId + source; discovery excludes a flag-off tenant. Touched-module e2e (appointments/lab/online-pharmacy/home-collection/patients/platform) all still green (additive seams didn't break contracts).
- **i18n parity:** 19/19 (`marketplace.*` en/ur key-sets identical).
- **Vertical/flag smoke:** the seed now provisions the Full + pharmacy-only + lab-only trio with clean off-states (a lab-only tenant projects no doctors/products; a pharmacy-only tenant no tests).
- **Do-NOT-break honoured:** 46 isolation invariants extended never relaxed; tenant staff flows + queues untouched (marketplace items are ordinary rows + a `source` badge); 15/19/25/34 contracts orchestrated not forked; publication is explicit opt-in; flag-then-permission; public perf budgets held; EN+UR parity; audit on every booking/publication mutation.

### Notes / carry-forward for 48
- The booking `paymentMode` seam is currently pay-at-facility only; **48 adds `PLATFORM_ONLINE`** via the tenant's own billing service (`packages/payments` + `apps/api/src/platform-settlement/`). The `source: MARKETPLACE` tags on appointment/lab/online rows are the provenance 48's commission/settlement reads.
- **έγιΎ╕Π 48 ends with a MANDATORY OWNER HALT (`[HUMAN_REQUIRED]`, spec 48 ┬π6 / CODEREF ┬πC.13).**

## Build-step 46 έΑΦ Platform Identity (one account across tenants)

- **Work-type:** FEATURE. **Phase 5 / item 2 έΑΦ THE most safety-critical step.** Branch `feature/46-platform-identity`.
- **Depends on:** 02 (RLS/`runWithTenant`), 03 (auth: JWT/OTP/refresh chain, `JwtAuthGuard`), 06 (audit), 08 (`Lang`), 31 (patient app / family), 40 (session + api client), 45 (design system). Spec `specs/46-platform-identity.md` + companion `specs/45-53-CODEREF.md`.
- **Schema/migration/RLS/auth impact:** NEW **platform-level section** of the Prisma schema έΑΦ the first tables that live ABOVE tenants. Migration `20260711100000_platform_identity`. Two NEW RLS primitives (mirrors of `apply_tenant_rls`). New platform token type (`typ:'platform'`) + `PlatformAuthGuard`. No tenant policy weakened.

### Problem
With 4έΑΥ5 clinics at launch (incl. a standalone pharmacy + lab), a real person uses several: she visits Ganatra Clinic, tests at City Lab, orders from a pharmacy. She must have ONE Marham Patti account (one login, one merged history) while EACH tenant sees only its own records (Ganatra must never learn she uses City Lab). Riders/phlebotomists likewise need one identity able to serve many tenants. Staff stay tenant-scoped, unchanged.

### What changed
**DB (`packages/db`):**
- New models (all `@@map` snake_case, cuid ids): `PlatformUser` (phone+audience `@@unique`, `Lang`, status έΑΦ NO tenantId), `PlatformOtp`, `PlatformRefreshToken`, `PatientLink` (platformUserIdέΗΦ{tenantId,patientId}, status, `consentSnapshot`), `WorkerLink` (rider/phlebέΗΤtenant staff User; used by 49), `ShareGrant` (patient-consented doc share; `tenantId`=GRANTEE, `sourceTenantId`=where the doc lives). New enums `PlatformAudience`/`LinkStatus`/`ShareStatus`/`ShareDocType`.
- Migration adds **`apply_platform_rls(t)`** έΑΦ `platform_only` policy: rows visible/writable ONLY under `app.platform_scope='on'`; a tenant context sees ZERO rows (fail-closed). And **`apply_platform_link_rls(t)`** έΑΦ `platform_link_isolation`: USING `tenant_id = current OR platform_scope='on'`, WITH CHECK `platform_scope='on'` (a tenant reads only its own rows and can NEVER forge a link/grant έΑΦ for another tenant OR itself). Reused by 47/48/50/51/53.
- `packages/db/src`: added **`runWithPlatformScope`** (the sanctioned platform read/write seam; `runAsPlatform` kept as an alias for the 06 audit reads). Exported the four new enums.

**API (`apps/api/src/platform/`):** new `PlatformModule` (registers no global guard). `PlatformTokenService` (mint/verify `typ:'platform'` access tokens + rotating platform refresh chain w/ reuse detection), `PlatformOtpService` (+ dev stub transport), `PlatformAuthGuard` (controller-scoped; platform routes are `@Public` so the staff guard steps aside, then this enforces a platform token), `PlatformAccountService` (OTP login/upsert, profile, per-tenant **claim** search/confirm, links, family), `PlatformTimelineService` (merged cross-tenant timeline = orchestration of per-link `runWithTenant` reads, each item tenant-chipped έΑΦ NEVER a join), `PlatformShareService` (create/revoke/list outgoing shares + grantee-tenant doctor-view read from the SOURCE tenant, audited). `PlatformRepository` is the single data seam (platform data under `runWithPlatformScope`; tenant slices under `runWithTenant`; `tenants` on the bare client). Controllers: `POST /platform/auth/{otp/request,otp/verify,refresh,logout}`, `GET/PATCH /platform/me` + `/timeline` `/links` `/family` `/claim/{search,confirm}` `/shares(+/:id/revoke)`, and the STAFF grantee-side `GET /platform/shares/inbound` `/:id/document` (`@Roles` clinical). Audit rows: `platform.link.created`, `platform.share.{granted,revoked,accessed}` (each under the relevant tenant).
- Endpoints deliberately NOT flag-gated (a platform account must work regardless of any single tenant's flags). `platform.marketplace` (spec ┬πFeature flags) is a tenant-side toggle DEFERRED to 47 (nothing in 46 consumes it) έΑΦ catalog stays additive.

**Web (`apps/web`):** separate `mp.platform` session (`lib/platform-session.ts`) + client (`lib/platform-api.ts`, refresh vs `/platform/auth/refresh`) έΑΦ the staff `mp.auth` contract (40) untouched. New `(auth)/login/platform` (phoneέΗΤOTP, tenant-agnostic), `(platform)` route group (guard `PlatformRouteGuard` + `PlatformChrome` + `manifest-platform.webmanifest`) with the merged-timeline app `PlatformClient` (timeline / clinics+claim / family / shares tabs). Entrance chooser patient card έΗΤ `/platform` (old `/patient` kept for back-compat). EN+UR parity keys under `platform.*` + auth `platformTitle/Subtitle/NameLabel`.

### Verification gates
- **typecheck:** all packages green (fixed TS2742 portability on the e2e fake by annotating share-returning methods).
- **lint:** 0 errors (1 pre-existing doctor-portal warning), `design-drift` guard green.
- **jest:** **db 212/212** (37 suites) incl. NEW `platform-identity-isolation.spec.ts` **14/14** έΑΦ PLATFORM tables denied to tenant ctx; link tables tenant-filtered; **Ganatra floor** (T1 can't discover the person's T2 link); WITH-CHECK forge blocked (other-tenant AND self); ShareGrant grantee-reads/source-blind/revoke-hides; fail-closed. **api 894/894** (77 suites) incl. NEW `platform.e2e.spec.ts` **16** (real guard chain, in-memory repo) έΑΦ OTP login issues a platform bundle; **token audiences never cross** (staff token έΗΤ 401 on `/platform/me`, platform token έΗΤ 401 on `/auth/me`); merged timeline across T1+T2 date-desc + chipped; claim search/confirm (+audit) & wrong-phone 404; T2 report shared έΗΤ T1 doctor view lists+opens (grant+access audited), source T2 blind, revoke έΗΤ invisible + doc 404; non-clinical role 403 έΑΦ plus `platform-helpers.spec.ts`. **i18n 19/19** (ENέΗΦUR parity gate green with new `platform.*` keys).
- **build:** `pnpm -r build` green. `/platform` 4.41 kB (201 kB First Load, on par with `/patient`); `/login/platform` 2.71 kB (153 kB έΑΦ within the public-route budget); shared JS unchanged; `/lh-bloated` canary intact.
- **do-not-break:** staff auth/tokens/guard order unchanged (894 api tests untouched); tenant RLS unchanged; `runAsPlatform`/audit reads unchanged; 40 session contract (`mp.auth`) untouched; 31 family re-homed under the platform account (not removed).

---

## Build-step 44 έΑΦ Design System Hardening & Consistency Pass (`feature/44-design-system`) έεΖ DONE/APPROVED (2026-07-10)

**WORK TYPE:** FEATURE ┬╖ **Phase:** 4 (App Shell, Demo Data, Entrances & Design System) / item 5 έΑΦ **completes Phase 4**. Ended with `[CHECKPOINT]`. Depends on 40 (shell), 43 (corrected tokens/AA guard), 13 (`@mp/ui` foundation). **Schema/RLS/migration:** none. **Auth/permission/flag impact:** none έΑΦ pure visual layer; all flag-then-permission gating, the 40 nav, and vertical-preset behaviour preserved. **Data contracts/handlers/tests:** unchanged (presentation-only migration; every pre-existing module test passes unchanged).

**Problem.** The 39 module screens were functionally deep but visually drifted: each hand-rolled `.mp-*` atoms (`mp-btn`/`mp-input`/`mp-card`/`mp-badge`) so inputs didn't match selects, buttons/tables/cards/badges varied screen-to-screen. The owner's mandate is one premium, CONSISTENT design system έΑΦ which comes from a shared component library, not per-screen restyling. Spec 13 promised `@mp/ui` as that system but modules never adopted it.

**What changed.**
- **Hardened `@mp/ui` into the single system** (`packages/ui/src/components/`, re-exported from `index.ts`): added **StatusPill** (semantic `tone` dot), **Checkbox/Radio/Switch** (`form-controls`), **Alert/Banner** (`alert`), **Avatar**, **Tooltip**, **Breadcrumb**, **Pagination**, **SearchField**, **PageHeader/Toolbar/FilterBar** (`page`), **Drawer** (+ trigger/close/content/title/description/header/footer), **ConfirmDialog**, and **DataTable** (sortable/searchable/paginated) grafted onto the existing `data-list` (added `sortValue` column hook + sort state; `DataTable`/`DataTableColumn` aliases exported). All brand-tokened, light+dark, RTL-correct, AA (43's guard), large-touch, keyboard-accessible.
- **`<Card>` made self-padding** (`card.tsx`): the retired `.mp-card` supplied `display:grid; gap:0.85rem; padding:1.1rem` έΑΦ the shadcn-style `<Card>` had none, so bare `<Card>` (the dominant module pattern, 53 sites) would have lost all internal spacing. Card now defaults to `flex flex-col gap-3.5 p-5`; `CardHeader`/`CardContent`/`CardFooter` became padding-less semantic groupings (they stack inside Card's single padding). Only the `/ui` gallery composed those sub-parts, so the change is contained; ui tests + build confirm no regression.
- **Migrated ALL 33 module screens** off the retired atoms to the shared components (drop the atom class, keep every other class/prop/handler/key; presentation-only). Groups: **clinic** patients/appointments/vitals/consultation/prescriptions; **lab** lab/samples/home-collection/phlebotomist; **pharmacy** pharmacy/inventory/purchase/transfer/store/rider/rx-desk; **money** billing/accounts/commission/dashboard; **admin+apps** ai-cost/audit/brand/consent(manager+gate)/flags/import/notifications/roles/sync + patient app + patient/assistant + doctor portal. Mappings: `<button className="mp-btn[-lg|-sm|-ghost|-danger]">`έΗΤ`<Button size/variant>` (anchors via `asChild`+`<a>`), `<input className="mp-input">`έΗΤ`<Input>`, `<select>`έΗΤ`<NativeSelect>`, `<textarea>`έΗΤ`<Textarea>`, `<div|section className="mp-card">`έΗΤ`<Card>`, `<span|p className="mp-badge">`έΗΤ`<Badge>`. `<Button>` defaults `type="button"`; the two implicit-submit buttons already carried explicit `type="submit"` (preserved). Layout/page classes (`mp-pt*`, `mp-field`, `mp-label`, `mp-msg*`, `mp-table`, `mp-grid-2`, `mp-h2/h3`, module-specific `mp-appt-*`/`mp-vitals-*`/`mp-kpi*`/`mp-alert*`, etc.) left untouched.
- **Drift guard** `apps/web/scripts/design-drift-check.mjs` έΑΦ walks the screen roots (`(app)`, `(patient)`, `(field)`, `store`) and fails the build if any retired `mp-(btn|input|card|badge)` atom reappears; wired into `apps/web` `pnpm lint` (`eslint . && node scripts/design-drift-check.mjs`) + a standalone `pnpm drift`. **Proven to bite:** a deliberate `<button className="mp-btn">` probe έΗΤ exit 1 with a located finding; removed έΗΤ exit 0. (Uses `dirname(fileURLToPath(import.meta.url))`, not the `URL` global, to satisfy the shared eslint config.)
- **`/ui` gallery** (`app/ui/UiShowcase.tsx`) extended to showcase the full system (every component, light+dark, LTR+RTL) έΑΦ the living reference (load-bearing documentation).
- **i18n:** reused existing keys where possible; EN/UR catalogs updated in lockstep (parity held at 1438/1438, zero missing/extra either direction). No hardcoded UI text (eslint i18n guard green).

**Known follow-ups (noted, not redesigned έΑΦ per spec ┬π3 "note structurally-poor UX as follow-up"):** (1) a few list-item cards `<li className="mp-card">` became `<Card>` (a `<div>`) rendered directly inside a `<ul>` in Store/Rx-desk/Rider έΑΦ valid-enough, renders 200, but semantically a `<ul>`+`<div>` mix; revisit with a `List`/`ListItem` primitive. (2) StoreClient's cart heading `<h2 className="mp-badge">` became `<Badge>` (a `<span>`), dropping one heading element έΑΦ cosmetic. Both are presentation-only and behaviourally identical.

**Verification gates (all green).**
- **typecheck:** 27/27 turbo tasks (fixed 4 in-progress JSX closing-tag mismatches `</section>|</div>`έΗΤ`</Card>` in ai-cost/billing/inventory/patient, and `variant="default"`έΗΤ`"primary"` active-tab ternaries across 9 screens).
- **lint:** 15/15 incl. the drift guard (`έεΥ no retired atoms`); zero eslint errors; unused-import cleanup (dropped stray `NativeSelect`/`Badge` imports).
- **jest:** 20 turbo test tasks έΑΦ **api 874/874** (75 suites, unchanged), **@mp/ui 55/55** (10 suites; +12 from the new `system.spec.tsx` covering the hardened components), i18n parity, **db 198/198**, brand έΑΦ all pre-existing module tests unchanged and passing.
- **next build:** 45/45 routes. **Public route-JS held within the 250 kB script budget** (`budgets.json` untouched, not loosened): `/` **106 kB (unchanged vs 43)**, `/login` 152 kB, `/store` 196 kB; `/lh-bloated` kept as the 383 kB negative test. Internal routes 148έΑΥ230 kB. System consolidation did not grow the public bundle.
- **runtime smoke:** production `next start` έΑΦ `/`, `/login`, `/ui`, `/store` (EN) + `/ui` (UR) all **200**; heavy internal `/dashboard /accounts /lab /pharmacy /billing /purchase` all **200** (client-island shell); `/ui` gallery renders "Design System" + component sections (Alert/Breadcrumb/badge/drawer/tooltip) in EN and UR.
- **Hygiene:** the stray 528 MB `marham-patti.zip` (a local deploy artifact, not build output) added to `.gitignore` so it can never be committed.

**Do-NOT-break honoured:** URLs unchanged (no route moves); every module's data contracts/handlers/tests intact; 43's AA guard + corrected tokens untouched; perf budgets only held/improved; EN+UR parity + RTL preserved; white-label (07 tokens only έΑΦ components carry no hardcoded brand). `/ui` kept current as the system's documentation.

## Build-step 42 έΑΦ Branded App Entrances (Staff / Patient / Rider / Phlebotomist) έεΖ DONE/APPROVED (2026-07-07)

**WORK TYPE:** FEATURE ┬╖ **Phase:** 4 (App Shell, Demo Data, Entrances & Design System) / item 3 ┬╖ **Branch:** `feature/42-branded-entrances`. Ended with `[CHECKPOINT]`. Depends on 40 (shell/session/role-routing), 41 (users to log in as), 07 (brand), 13 (PWA base). **Schema/RLS/migration:** none (no new business tables). **Auth/permission impact:** none έΑΦ rider/phleb logins REUSE the existing 03 `/auth/staff/login`; no contract reshaping. **Feature flags:** none owned έΑΦ entrances RESPECT existing flags (`patient.app`, `lab.homeCollection`, `pharmacy.online`); a capability that's off shows the island's clean no-access state inside branded chrome (never a broken app).

**Problem.** Every audience shared one generic PWA identity and one entry experience; `/` was still the step-01 colour-swatch placeholder, and rider/phlebotomist had no tailored login/home. The foodpanda model wants separate branded "apps" per audience (own name/icon/install identity/login/home) over ONE codebase/backend/auth έΑΦ no forks.

**What changed.**
- **Entrance chooser `/`** (`apps/web/app/page.tsx`, rewritten) έΑΦ server component replacing the swatch placeholder: product mark + four large entrance cards (StaffέΗΤ`/dashboard`, PatientέΗΤ`/patient`, RiderέΗΤ`/rider`, PhlebotomistέΗΤ`/phlebotomist`), `?lang=` EN/UR toggle (plain links, no client JS), RTL-correct, rendered entirely from brand CSS-vars + i18n catalog. `poweredBy` footer. First-load **166 B / 106 kB** (well under the 250 kB script budget). The 40 route guard forwards a logged-out visitor to the right login and a signed-in one straight into their app.
- **Four scoped PWA manifests** (`public/manifest-{staff,patient,rider,phlebo}.webmanifest`) with per-audience `name`/`short_name`/`id`/`start_url`/`scope`/icon έΑΦ Staff (scope `/`, start `/dashboard`), Patient (the flagship "Marham Patti", scope `/patient`), Rider (scope `/rider`), Phlebo (scope `/phlebotomist`). Linked per audience: `(app)/layout.tsx` (staff) + `(patient)/layout.tsx` (patient) via `metadata.manifest`; rider/phleb via each **page's** metadata since they share the one `(field)` group. Root `/` + `/login` keep the flagship `manifest.webmanifest`. Verified via curl: each scope emits its own `<link rel="manifest">`.
- **Four brand-derived install icons** (`public/icon-{staff,patient,rider,phlebo}.svg`) έΑΦ same teal-tile family, distinct glyph (pulse / heart / scooter / vial).
- **Light audience chrome** (`components/shell/EntranceChrome.tsx`, new) έΑΦ a minimal phone-first top bar (brand mark + audience pill + `LanguageSwitcher` + `ThemeToggle` + logout) wrapping patient/rider/phleb (no staff sidebar). One component, audience derived from the path so the shared `(field)` group shows the right identity. Wired in `(patient)/layout.tsx` + `(field)/layout.tsx` (guard έΗΤ chrome έΗΤ page). `poweredBy` honoured via `useBrand`. Logout returns each audience to its own door.
- **Dedicated field logins** (`(auth)/login/rider/page.tsx`, `(auth)/login/phlebotomist/page.tsx`, new) έΑΦ simplified staff-auth doors (email+password, audience-preset copy). `StaffLoginForm` gained an `audience` prop: on success, a role whose home έΚι the door's home is routed to its **correct** role home with a gentle notice (`entrance.mismatchNotice`) after a 1.4 s beat έΑΦ never blocked, never blank (Acceptance ┬π4). `loginPathForPath()` now sends `/rider`έΗΤ`/login/rider`, `/phlebotomist`έΗΤ`/login/phlebotomist` (patient unchanged).
- **Page container fix** έΑΦ the four field/patient pages used `className="mp-shell"`, which collided with the step-40 staff-shell grid (`.mp-shell` is defined twice). Switched them to a new `.mp-entrance-page` centered container (and dropped their stray `<main>` since the chrome now owns it).
- **Service worker** (`public/sw.js`) έΑΦ bumped `SHELL_CACHE` v1έΗΤv2 and added the four manifests + four icons to the precache list so each installed scope keeps its identity offline. ONE SW, logic unchanged (no fork).
- **CSS** (`globals.css`, +~220 lines) έΑΦ `.mp-entry-*` (chooser) + `.mp-entrance-*` (chrome), dark-aware via `--mp-*` tokens from the start (card name/CTA get `html.dark` overrides so no dark-on-dark), RTL logical properties, big touch targets.
- **i18n** έΑΦ new nested `entrance` block (18 keys) ├Ω EN+UR, inserted after `home` (originals byte-preserved). RTL verified live (╪π╪▒╪ψ┘Ι chooser renders `dir="rtl"` + Urdu labels).

**Verification gates (all green).** typecheck **42/42** ┬╖ lint **42/42** (0 errors) ┬╖ `next build` **45/45** pages, compiled clean, **all URLs unchanged** (only additive `/login/rider`, `/login/phlebotomist`; `/lh-bloated` negative test intact) ┬╖ jest: **db 198/198**, **i18n 19/19** (ENέΗΦUR parity holds at 1438 keys each), api/ui/others cached-green from 41 ┬╖ **performance:** `/` 166 B / 106 kB (< 250 kB budget); patient/rider/phleb entry surfaces stay lean (147έΑΥ149 kB). **Runtime smoke:** curl 200 on `/`, `/?lang=ur`, `/login/rider`, `/login/phlebotomist`, all four manifests + icons; per-scope manifest links + rider manifest name/scope verified. **White-label:** chrome reads brand tokens + `useBrand` appName, `poweredBy` honoured; public surfaces use the default identity (consistent with the shipped `/login`). **Flags:** islands already degrade to a clean `noaccess` state (`paNoAccess` etc.) on 403, now inside branded chrome. **Do-NOT-break:** `StoredBundle`/`mp.auth` untouched, provider stack + brand-var injection intact, auth contracts unchanged, seed.ts untouched, offline SW behaviour preserved.

## Build-step 40 έΑΦ App Shell + Session Layer έεΖ DONE/APPROVED (2026-07-07)

**WORK TYPE:** FEATURE ┬╖ **Phase:** 4 (App Shell, Demo Data, Entrances & Design System) / item 1 ┬╖ **Branch:** `feature/40-app-shell-session`. Ended with `[CHECKPOINT]`. Depends on 03 (auth), 04 (RBAC), 05 (flags), 07 (brand), 08 (i18n), 13 (@mp/ui). **Schema/RLS/migration:** none (one small API read endpoint; reuses existing scopes). **Auth/permission impact:** additive `GET /auth/me` (auth-guarded); no contract reshaping. **Feature flags:** none owned έΑΦ the shell RESPECTS all flags (flag-first, then permission, then role).

**Problem.** All 39 modules worked but the web app had NO navigation (3 internal links app-wide), NO post-login redirect (login dead-ended on a "success" paragraph), NO route guard, NO logout, and the bearer token was attached per-component in 34 islands. 39 disconnected islands reachable only by typing URLs.

**What changed.**
- **API έΑΦ `GET /auth/me`** (`apps/api/src/session/session.controller.ts` + `session.module.ts`, registered in `app.module.ts` after auth/flags/permissions). Returns `{ userId, role, tenantId, branchId?, permissions[], flags[] }` έΑΦ permission keys via `PermissionService.keysForRole`, ENABLED flag keys via `FlagService.getEffectiveFlagsFor` (disabled dropped), both sorted. Own module so it composes the 04/05 services without widening AuthModule. The pre-existing `POST /auth/me` (guard-proof probe from 03) is untouched (distinct HTTP method).
- **Centralized API client** (`apps/web/lib/api.ts`). `getJson/postJson/putJson` + a new `apiFetch(path, init) έΗΤ Response` now auto-attach `Authorization: Bearer` (from the stored bundle) + the `x-tenant-slug` fallback, default `cache:'no-store'`, and on `401` run ONE single-flight refresh (`/auth/staff/refresh` rotation) shared by all in-flight callers έΗΤ retry once έΗΤ on failure `clearBundle()` + audience-aware redirect to login (patient area έΗΤ `/login/patient`, else `/login`), loop-guarded. FormData bodies left untouched.
- **Session layer** (`apps/web/lib/session.ts`). Added `clearBundle()`, `hasSession()`, `roleHome(role)` (PATIENTέΗΤ/patient, RIDERέΗΤ/rider, PHLEBOTOMISTέΗΤ/phlebotomist, staffέΗΤ/dashboard), `loginPathForPath()`, `readNextParam()` (open-redirect-safe), `postLoginTarget()`. `StoredBundle` shape + `mp.auth` key frozen (load-bearing).
- **Nav registry** (`apps/web/lib/nav.ts`). Ordered `NAV` of every module grouped Core/Clinic/Lab/Pharmacy/Money/Admin, each `{href,labelKey,icon,requiredFlag?,requiredPermission?,roles?}`. `visibleNav(me)` filters flag-first έΗΤ permission έΗΤ role (verified against the live `@mp/shared` flag + permission catalogs and the RBAC controllers' actual gates, so ZERO dead links). `activeHref()` longest-prefix match.
- **`<AppShell>`** (`apps/web/components/shell/AppShell.tsx` + `NavIcon.tsx` [lucide] + `RouteGuard.tsx`). Persistent brand-tokened sidebar (role/flag-aware nav from `useSession`έΗΤ/auth/me) + top bar (brand mark, reused `LanguageSwitcher` + `ThemeToggle`, logout), EN+UR + RTL (logical properties), light/dark via `--mp-*` tokens, collapsible mobile drawer, active-route highlight, skip link. Route guard: no session έΗΤ `router.replace(loginPathForPath+?next)`. Shell CSS appended to `globals.css`.
- **Route groups** (URLs UNCHANGED έΑΦ verified in the build route list). `git mv` into `(app)/` (21 staff module dirs, wrapped by `(app)/layout.tsx` = AppShell), `(patient)/` (patient area, `RouteGuard`-only έΑΦ 42 adds chrome), `(field)/` (rider+phlebotomist, `RouteGuard`-only), `(auth)/` (login/patient/reset). A scripted import-depth fix (+1 `../` on 229 `lib`/`components` imports across 74 files); intra-group refs (`../AuthShell`) untouched.
- **Login redirect.** `StaffLoginForm` / `TwoFactorPanel` / `PatientLoginForm` now `router.replace(postLoginTarget(role))` on success (honouring the guard's `?next`), `clearSessionCache()` so the new session refetches /auth/me, brief "redirecting" toast replacing the dead-end paragraph.
- **34 components migrated** off local `readBundle()?.accessToken` header code (grep-clean) via 4 parallel sub-agents + 2 hand-done reference files έΑΦ Pattern A (`const api = apiFetch`) and Pattern B (dropped `{headers:authHeader}` from helper calls); `token` kept only as a `hasSession()` sign-in gate. Also migrated the infra providers `lib/i18n.tsx`, `lib/brand.tsx`, `lib/feature.tsx`, and the offline outbox drain in `lib/offline.tsx` (now through `apiFetch`, idempotency-key preserved, gets silent refresh).
- **i18n.** +40 top-level keys ├Ω EN+UR (nav group labels, 28 module labels, shell chrome, `redirecting`), appended by text (originals byte-preserved; pre-existing duplicate keys left intact).

**Verification gates (all green).** typecheck 27/27 ┬╖ lint 15/15 (0 errors; 1 pre-existing unrelated warning in doctor-portal.repositories) ┬╖ jest: **api 869/869** (75 suites; +2 new `session.controller.spec`) ┬╖ **db 178/178** ┬╖ **ui 38/38** ┬╖ **i18n 19/19** (ENέΗΦUR parity holds at 1437 keys each) ┬╖ `next build` 43/43 pages, compiled clean, **all URLs unchanged** (`/dashboard`, `/admin/*`, `/login`, `/patient`, `/rider`, `/phlebotomist` έΑΦ route groups invisible in paths), `/lh-bloated` negative test intact. Shell overhead negligible έΑΦ `(app)` routes (~146έΑΥ148 kB first-load) match the guard-only `/patient` baseline (well under the έΚν30 KB target); public routes unchanged (`/` 103 kB, `/login` 150 kB, `/store` 147 kB). White-label: shell reads brand tokens only. RBAC-sanity: `TENANT_OWNER` holds all TENANT-scoped perms έΗΤ sees every module; platform-only items stay hidden with no dead links.

**Do-not-break honoured.** `StoredBundle` shape + `mp.auth` key (migrated readers, not forked); `x-tenant-slug` fallback on every browser call; provider stack + brand injection + lang/dir + OfflineIndicator/RegisterSW in the root layout; auth API contracts + guard order + `/health` public; baseline `seed.ts` untouched; flag-then-permission precedence; perf budgets; EN+UR parity + RTL; screenshot-token gate.

## Launch hotfix έΑΦ Lighthouse public-route JS budget (recharts out of first-load) έεΖ DONE (2026-07-07)

**WORK TYPE:** FIX ┬╖ **Phase:** Launch / stabilization (NOT a new build-step έΑΦ the specced build stays complete at 1έΑΥ39; no step 40 exists) ┬╖ **Branch:** `feat/39-ai-cost-control`. Ended with `[CHECKPOINT]`.

**Schema/RLS/auth/flag impact:** NONE. No migration, no new table/enum, no flag/permission/role-grant change. No i18n change (0 new keys; parity untouched). Pure front-end bundle-graph fix (`@mp/ui` barrel + 3 `apps/web` route files). **Budget NOT raised** έΑΦ `lighthouserc.json`/`budgets.json` unchanged (250 KB script budget kept); the actual bundle was reduced.

**Problem (found via the Lighthouse CI gate έΑΦ the point worth remembering):** the Lighthouse job ran correctly but failed the **`resource-summary:script.size έΚν 250,000`** assertion on ALL four audited public routes έΑΦ `/` 323,590 ┬╖ `/login` 325,702 ┬╖ `/ui` 331,153 ┬╖ `/store` 327,060 (three consistent runs each; real bundle weight, not variance). Ground-truth from the LHR `network-requests`: the single dominant script on EVERY route έΑΦ including the home page `/`, which renders **no chart at all** έΑΦ was `chunks/1923-*.js` = **recharts, 151,768 bytes of script transfer** (527 KB raw), i.e. >60 % of the whole budget. **Root cause:** recharts leaked into the **shared first-load graph via the `@mp/ui` barrel**. The root layout imports `ThemeProvider` from `@mp/ui`; the barrel (`packages/ui/src/index.ts`) also re-exported the recharts-based `./components/chart`, so importing *anything* from `@mp/ui` (a Button, the ThemeProvider) dragged recharts in. `next.config.mjs`'s `optimizePackageImports: ['@mp/ui']` did not tree-shake it out for this transpiled workspace barrel. The `/ui` `DemoChart` was already behind `next/dynamic`, but the barrel coupling defeated it: recharts was eager on every route regardless.

**What changed (sever recharts from the barrel; keep it lazy where actually used):**
- **`packages/ui/package.json`** έΑΦ added a dedicated subpath export **`"./chart"` έΗΤ `./dist/components/chart.js`** (types έΗΤ `./dist/components/chart.d.ts`).
- **`packages/ui/src/index.ts`** έΑΦ **removed** the `LineChartCard/AreaChartCard/BarChartCard/DonutChartCard` (+`ChartSeries`/`DonutDatum`) re-export from the barrel; left a comment block explaining WHY (recharts must never be pulled into first-load JS just because a surface imported a Button) so it isn't "simplified" back. recharts is now reachable ONLY via `@mp/ui/chart`.
- **`apps/web/app/ui/DemoChart.tsx`** + **`apps/web/app/lh-bloated/BloatedClient.tsx`** έΑΦ import chart cards from `@mp/ui/chart` (DemoChart stays behind `next/dynamic`; BloatedClient still imports EAGERLY on purpose).
- **`apps/web/app/ui/UiShowcase.tsx`** έΑΦ added an IntersectionObserver **`WhenVisible`** gate around the below-the-fold `DemoChart` so recharts' lazy chunk is fetched only when the chart scrolls into view (`rootMargin:200px`; falls back to eager render where `IntersectionObserver` is absent). A real user still sees the chart (skeleton έΗΤ chart); the initial paint and the Lighthouse trace (which does not scroll) never pay for recharts.

**Result (First Load JS, `next build`):** `/ui` 311 KB έΗΤ **194 KB**; `/`, `/login`, `/store` shed the recharts chunk entirely. `/lh-bloated` stays intentionally heavy (383 KB first-load).

**Verification έΑΦ re-ran the EXACT gate locally (`lhci autorun` on `lighthouserc.json`, real headless Chromium, 3 runs/route, same config as CI):**
- **`script.size` (budget 250,000) έΑΦ ALL PASS:** `/` **206,723** ┬╖ `/login` **208,838** ┬╖ `/ui` **212,296** ┬╖ `/store` **210,193** (was 323έΑΥ331 K; έΚΙ110 K cut/route, ~15έΑΥ17 % headroom). recharts (`chunks/1923`) confirmed **absent** from all four routes' network requests.
- **Category scores (min 0.90) έΑΦ ALL PASS:** Performance `/`=100 ┬╖ `/login`=100 ┬╖ `/ui`=99 ┬╖ `/store`=100; Accessibility 94/95/95/94; Best-Practices 100/100/96/100. `resource-summary:total:size` warn-budget also clear. Full `lhci autorun` exits **0** ("All results processed!").
- **Negative gate still BITES (canary intact):** `/lh-bloated` (still eager recharts via `@mp/ui/chart` + `import * as` lucide) scores a **script.size of 483,975** and fails the έΚξ90 / budget assertion (assert exit 1). It is NOT in `lighthouserc.json`'s URL list, so it stays excluded from the real budget gate έΑΦ exactly as designed.
- **Full project gates:** turbo **typecheck 27/27**, **lint 15/15** (0 errors; 1 pre-existing `@mp/api` doctor-portal warning, untouched), **test 20/20** tasks έΑΦ jest **api 867/867**, **db 178/178**, **ui 38/38**, **i18n 19/19 parity**. `next build` (production, `NODE_ENV=production APP_ENV=staging`) green, 43/43 static pages, no `<Html>`/prerender regressions.

## Launch hotfix έΑΦ CRLF-safe env sourcing + env-driven ports/health verified έεΖ DONE (2026-07-06)

**WORK TYPE:** FIX ┬╖ **Phase:** Launch / stabilization (NOT a new build-step έΑΦ the specced build stays complete at 1έΑΥ39; no step 40 exists) ┬╖ **Branch:** `feat/39-ai-cost-control`. Ended with `[CHECKPOINT]`.

**Schema/RLS/auth/flag impact:** NONE. No migration, no new table/enum, no flag/permission/role-grant change, no i18n change. Single-file code fix in `deploy.sh` (the port-wiring + public-`/health` parts had already landed in `1d18c15`; this entry also records their end-to-end verification).

**Problem (found via the staging deploy έΑΦ the point worth remembering):** the deploy died at `source ./.env` with `./.env: line 4: $'\r': command not found` (exit **127**). The server's `./.env` was saved with **Windows/CRLF** line endings; sourcing it on Linux under `set -euo pipefail` is fatal two ways: (a) a blank CRLF line becomes a lone `\r`, which bash tries to run as a command έΗΤ `command not found` (127) έΗΤ `set -e` kills the whole deploy; and (b) even on lines that don't error, every value keeps a trailing CR (`API_PORT=$'4001\r'`), which would later corrupt the health-check URL (`http://127.0.0.1:4001\r/health`). The env file is `www`-owned on the server, so a naive in-place rewrite isn't guaranteed writable.

**What changed (`deploy.sh` ┬π2 only):** replaced `set -a; . ./.env; set +a` with a **CR-normalized process-substitution source** έΑΦ `set -a; source <(sed 's/\r$//' ./.env); set +a`. This strips the trailing CR from **every** line before bash parses it, so the file sources cleanly whether it's LF or CRLF, yields clean values (no `\r` in `API_PORT`/`WEB_PORT`/secrets), and **never mutates** the read-only `www`-owned server file. Added a comment block explaining the failure mode so it isn't "simplified" back. No other file touched.

**Env-driven ports + public /health (already committed in `1d18c15`; verified here end-to-end):** `ecosystem.config.js` reads `API_PORT`/`WEB_PORT` from `process.env` (falling back to prod 4000/3000) and `mp-web` runs `next start -p ${WEB_PORT}`; the NestJS API binds `config.API_PORT` (`@mp/config`, default 4000); `deploy.sh`'s health-check targets `http://127.0.0.1:$API_PORT/health` (never a hardcoded 4000); `GET /health` is `@Public()` and all five global guards honor it (`JwtAuthGuard`, `RolesGuard`, `FeatureGuard`, `ConsentGuard` short-circuit on `IS_PUBLIC`; `TenantContextGuard` only gates `TENANT_SCOPED` routes, which health is not). `.env.example` documents the convention: **staging `API_PORT=4001`/`WEB_PORT=3001`, prod `4000`/`3000`**, carried by each server's `./.env`.

**Verification (end-to-end, real artifacts έΑΦ not just unit tests):**
- **CRLF source, reproduced + fixed:** a CRLF fixture with a blank line reproduces the exact reported failure under `set -euo pipefail` (`line N: $'\r': command not found`, outer exit **127**); the new `source <(sed 's/\r$//' έΑο)` path reaches the end with clean values (`APP_ENV=staging`, `API_PORT=4001`, `WEB_PORT=3001`) and a clean URL. `bash -n deploy.sh` έΗΤ syntax OK.
- **Live API boot on the env-driven port:** booted the real built `apps/api/dist/main.js` with `API_PORT=4001` sourced via the new CR-normalized read έΗΤ log `Marham Patti API listening on :4001 [env=staging build=verify-crlf-test]`. Prisma is lazy (no `$connect` at boot), so an unreachable DB did **not** block liveness.
- **Health public + auth still enforced:** unauthenticated `GET /health` έΗΤ **HTTP 200** `{"status":"ok","buildId":"verify-crlf-test","ts":έΑο}` (BUILD_ID surfaced from env); unauthenticated `GET /ai/budget` έΗΤ **HTTP 401** έΑΦ proving `/health` is a genuine public exception, not auth being disabled, and that the health-check the deploy runs will pass on 4001.

## Launch hotfix έΑΦ production `next build` (staging) fix έεΖ DONE (2026-07-06)

**WORK TYPE:** FIX ┬╖ **Phase:** Launch / stabilization (NOT a new build-step έΑΦ the specced build stays complete at 1έΑΥ39; no step 40 exists) ┬╖ **Branch:** `feat/39-ai-cost-control`. Ended with `[CHECKPOINT]`.

**Schema/RLS/auth/flag impact:** NONE. No migration, no new table/enum, no flag or permission change, no role-grant change. Pure code/build-config fix. i18n: **+7 EN+UR key pairs** (`notFoundTitle/Body/Home`, `errorTitle/Body/Retry/Home`) έΑΦ parity kept.

**Problem (found via the FIRST production deploy έΑΦ the point worth remembering):** every dev/CI turbo gate (typecheck/lint/build/test/i18n) was green, but the STAGING deploy failed at `deploy.sh`'s real production build step. `next build` (App Router, `apps/web`) died during **static page generation**:

```
Error: <Html> should not be imported outside of pages/_document.
Error occurred prerendering page "/404".
Export encountered an error on /_error: /404, exiting the build.
έρψ Next.js build worker exited with code: 1
```

This is the classic "passes dev gates, fails the real `next build`" gap: dev/`next dev` never statically prerenders `/404` + `/_error`, so the defect only surfaces on the production export the deploy runs.

**Root cause:** `apps/web` is a pure **Next 15 App Router** project έΑΦ there is NO `pages/` directory and ZERO imports of `Html/Head/Main/NextScript` from `next/document` anywhere in the repo (verified by grep). The failure was the *absence* of an App-Router error surface: with no `app/not-found.tsx`/`error.tsx`/`global-error.tsx`, Next fell back to its **internal Pages-Router** `/404` + `/_error` pages, which import `<Html>` from `next/document`. Prerendering that fallback under the App Router trips the guard and aborts the export.

**Fix έΑΦ own the App-Router error surface (makes the Pages fallback unreachable):**
- `apps/web/app/not-found.tsx` έΑΦ **server** component. Opens in the visitor's persisted UI language via `serverLocale` + the shared `@mp/i18n` catalog (`tr`/`dir` adapter), EN default / UR flips RTL. @mp/ui brand tokens (`text-brand-teal-deep`, `bg-background`, `text-foreground`, `text-muted-foreground`, `font-display`) + `Button asChild` έΗΤ `<Link href="/">`. No client JS.
- `apps/web/app/error.tsx` έΑΦ **client** route-segment boundary (Next contract). Renders INSIDE the root layout, so the i18n/theme/brand providers are live έΗΤ uses `useI18n()` for active-language copy + `dir`; `reset()` retry + Back-to-home. Logs `error` (digest) to console only.
- `apps/web/app/global-error.tsx` έΑΦ **client**, last-resort boundary that REPLACES the root layout when the layout itself throws έΗΤ renders its own `<html>`/`<body>` and cannot use the providers or `globals.css`. Fully self-contained: brand `--brand-*` CSS vars applied inline via `brandCssVars()`, copy pulled straight from `@mp/i18n`, locale read from the `mp.locale` cookie (EN first paint έΗΤ adopt cookie in `useEffect`), inline-styled retry button on `--brand-teal`.
- i18n: +7 flat keys added to BOTH `packages/i18n/src/messages/en.json` and `ur.json` (parity gate stays 19/19).

**Fix έΑΦ non-standard `NODE_ENV` warning (per ARCHITECTURE):** the build also logged "You are using a non-standard NODE_ENV value." `NODE_ENV` must ONLY ever be a standard Next.js value (production / development / test); the staging-vs-prod distinction is carried by our separate **`APP_ENV`**. `deploy.sh` ┬π2b now normalizes after sourcing the server `./.env`: if `APP_ENV` is unset it adopts the deploy env (defaulting to `staging`, since deploy.sh only ever deploys the staging branch), then **pins `NODE_ENV=production`** for the build. `ecosystem.config.js` inlines `APP_ENV` (from the deploy env, default `production`) into every app's `env` alongside the standard `NODE_ENV: 'production'`, so the runtime sees it explicitly via `pm2 --update-env`.

**Screenshot-token gate still fail-closes after the change:** `screenshotBypassEnabled` = `(APP_ENV ?? NODE_ENV) === 'staging'`. New env shape έΑΦ staging: `APP_ENV=staging`, `NODE_ENV=production` έΗΤ **enabled**; prod: `APP_ENV=production` έΗΤ **off**; wrong/absent token in staging έΗΤ **403**. The exact cases (`{APP_ENV:'staging',NODE_ENV:'production'}έΗΤtrue`, `{APP_ENV:'production',NODE_ENV:'staging'}έΗΤfalse`) are covered by `packages/ui/src/lib/screenshot.spec.ts` (part of ui 38/38 pass), so the gate remains correct and fail-closed.

**Minor:** `packages/ui/package.json` έΗΤ `"type": "module"` to clear the `tailwind-preset.js` "module type not specified" Node warning (dist is already ESM). Its CommonJS `jest.config.js` was renamed to `jest.config.cjs` so jest keeps loading it as CommonJS under `type: module` (ui tests stay green at 38/38).

**Verification (the deploy.sh way, not just dev gates):**
- **Full production build** with `NODE_ENV=production APP_ENV=staging BUILD_ID=έΑο` `pnpm turbo run build` έΗΤ **15/15 tasks OK**, static generation completes, `/_not-found` route emitted, and a forced `next build` shows **no `<Html>`/prerender error, no "non-standard NODE_ENV" warning, no `tailwind-preset` module-type warning**.
- **Live render** (`next start`, prod build): a missing route returns **HTTP 404** with EN "Page not found" + "Back to home" + brand token `text-brand-teal-deep` + `dir="ltr"`; with cookie `mp.locale=ur` έΗΤ "╪╡┘Β╪φ█Β ┘Η█Β█Ν┌║ ┘Ζ┘Ε╪π" + "█Β┘Ι┘Ζ ┘╛╪▒ ┘Ι╪π┘╛╪│" + `dir="rtl"` (RTL flip). Confirms @mp/ui tokens + EN/UR i18n honored.
- **All gates:** typecheck **27/27** ┬╖ lint **15/15** (0 errors; 1 pre-existing unused-`eslint-disable` warning in `@mp/api`, untouched) ┬╖ jest **api 864/864 + db 178/178 + ui 38/38 + i18n 19/19 (parity)**.

## Build-step 39 έΑΦ AI Suite: Cost Control & Quality Routing (`ai.suite`) έεΖ DONE/APPROVED (2026-07-05)

**WORK TYPE:** FEATURE ┬╖ **Phase:** AI Suite (item 5) ┬╖ **Branch:** `feat/39-ai-cost-control` (stacked on `feat/38-ai-feedback-learning`). **This completes launch scope (build-steps 1έΑΥ39).** Depends on 35 (cost capture / budget primitive), 24 (dashboard), 06 (audit). Ended with `[CHECKPOINT]`.

**Schema/RLS/auth impact:** ONE new tenant-scoped table (`AiSpendLog`, canonical `apply_tenant_rls` 02) + an ALTER of the existing `AiBudget`. NEW enum `BreachAction`. Migration `20260705330000_ai_cost_control`. **Flag REUSED (`ai.suite`) έΑΦ NO catalog change. NO new permission** (reuses `ai.budget.manage`, added in 35). No role-grant change.

### Problem
AI cost can silently balloon and varies wildly by model. The owner needs a live spend meter, per-task model selection (quality-first but cost-aware) and hard budget caps with a defined behavior on breach έΑΦ otherwise the assist-only suite becomes a runaway bill. This operationalizes the ┬π35 budget primitive (35 still captures cost + accumulates spend + enforces; 39 adds the CONTROLS + the VISIBILITY layer).

### What changed
**Data model (`@mp/db`):**
- `AiBudget` gains `warnPct Int @default(80)` (% of cap at which the meter warns) + `onBreach BreachAction @default(BLOCK)`. Existing rows adopt the safe defaults via the migration's column defaults.
- NEW `AiSpendLog` έΑΦ append-only ledger, one row per completed `runAiTask` call: `tenantId` / `taskType` / `model` / `cost Decimal(14,4)` / `at`. `@@index([tenantId, at])`, `@@map("ai_spend_log")`. Tenant-scoped (FORCE RLS via `SELECT apply_tenant_rls('ai_spend_log')`).
- NEW `enum BreachAction { WARN THROTTLE BLOCK }`, exported from `@mp/db`.

**Pure core (`@mp/shared/ai-gateway.ts`) έΑΦ deterministic, provable, same on server/client/tests:**
- `budgetGate(spent, cap, onBreach=BLOCK, warnPct=80) έΗΤ { gate: 'ALLOW'|'WARN'|'THROTTLE'|'BLOCK', throttled, warning, over }`. No cap (έΚν0) έΘΤ ALLOW; under cap but έΚξ warn threshold έΘΤ WARN; at/over cap έΘΤ the configured `onBreach`. **Escalation-safe: an unknown action falls back to a hard BLOCK.**
- `budgetMeter(cap, spent, warnPct, onBreach) έΗΤ BudgetMeter` (`remaining` / `usedPct` / `warnThreshold` are null with no cap).
- `BreachAction` type + `BREACH_ACTIONS` + `isBreachAction`, `DEFAULT_BREACH_ACTION=BLOCK`, `DEFAULT_WARN_PCT=80`, `normalizeWarnPct` (clamp [0,100]; badέΗΤdefault), `THROTTLE_TIER = AI_TIERS[0] = FAST`.
- Reuses commission's existing `isPeriodKey` + `periodRange` (`YYYY-MM` έΗΤ `[from,to)` UTC) for the ledger aggregation window έΑΦ no duplicate helper (avoided an `isPeriodKey` export collision).

**API (`apps/api/src/ai`):**
- `AiGatewayService.runAiTask` έΑΦ enforcement stays THE point: consult `budgetGate` BEFORE the provider call. **BLOCK** έΗΤ record a FAILED task + throw 403 (spend never mutated). **WARN** έΗΤ run (soft cap). **THROTTLE** έΗΤ force the task's tier down to FAST for that run. After a successful call, in addition to `incrementSpend` (authoritative accumulation) it appends an `AiSpendLog` line (`taskType`/`model`/`cost`).
- `spend(tenantId, period?)` έΑΦ live meter: validates the optional `YYYY-MM` (400 else), aggregates the ledger over the period window into `{ periodKey, total, calls, byTaskType[], byModel[], budget }` (buckets via Prisma `groupBy`, `_sum.cost` + `_count`).
- `routing(tenantId)` έΑΦ every `AI_TASK_TYPE` with its quality-first `defaultTier` + the tenant's effective override (tier/model/provider/enabled/configured) + the tier's per-1k `rate` (`DEFAULT_TIER_RATE`), so the UI shows the cost/quality trade-off. Quality-first is the default wherever a task has no override.
- `setBudget(tenantId, {capAmount?, warnPct?, onBreach?})` έΑΦ merge-on-write over the current period; `budgetView` returns the extended meter fields.
- Repo (`PrismaAiGatewayRepo`): `setBudget` (merge), `logSpend`, `spendByTaskType` / `spendByModel` (literal-`by` `groupBy` έΗΤ `toBuckets`). `BudgetRow` gains `warnPct`/`onBreach`. Fake repo updated (spendLog array + in-memory aggregate + `seedBudget(...,{warnPct,onBreach})`).
- Controller: `GET /ai/spend?period=` (`ai.budget.manage`), `GET /ai/routing` + `PUT /ai/routing` (`ai.budget.manage`, audited as `ai.config.upsert`), extended `PUT /ai/budget` (parse merge-on-write; έΚξ1 field or 400; audited), `GET /ai/budget` (`ai.use`, extended view). `/ai/config` GET/PUT kept as a back-compat alias.
- DTO: `parseBudget` (optional cap/warnPct/onBreach, έΚξ1 required, each validated), `parseSpendPeriod` (optional `YYYY-MM`).

**Web (`apps/web`):**
- NEW `/admin/ai-cost` (`page.tsx` + `AiCostClient.tsx`). Simple = live spend meter (spent / remaining / calls + an animated usage gauge: tealέΗΤamberέΗΤcoral) + the budget-cap form (cap / warn% / breach-action select). Pro adds the by-task-type + by-model spend tables and the per-task routing table (tier select + model input + per-1k rate, "(default)" marker). Probes `/ai/spend` έΗΤ clean no-access state (404/403). EN+UR.
- 24 dashboard: a self-probing `AiCostCard` (fetches `/ai/spend`; renders NOTHING without `ai.suite`/`ai.budget.manage`) showing this period's AI spend + cap usage% + a link to `/admin/ai-cost` έΑΦ cost reporting surfaced on the dashboard (Acceptance ┬π4).
- i18n: +38 `aiCost*` / `dashAiCost*` keys in EN + UR (parity held).

### Gates (all green)
- turbo **typecheck 27/27** + **lint 15/15** (0 errors; 1 pre-existing doctor-portal `no-explicit-any` warn, unrelated).
- turbo **build + test 23/23**.
- jest **api 864/864** (74 suites; **+11**: 7 shared cost-control unit tests in `ai-helpers.spec` + 4 e2e in `ai.e2e.spec`).
- jest **db 178/178** (35 suites; **+5** new `ai-cost-control-isolation.spec.ts` έΑΦ real 01έΗΤ39 migrations under pglite).
- i18n **19/19** parity.

### Vertical smoke (e2e over the real module graph, faked 35 repo + real mock provider)
- Budget controls merge-on-write: a warn%/breach-only PUT preserves the cap; `warnThreshold` computed (25 = 50% of 50). Empty body / `onBreach:'QUEUE'` / `warnPct:150` έΗΤ 400.
- `onBreach` behavior over cap (seed cap 5 / spent 5): **BLOCK έΗΤ 403 + recorded FAILED, spend untouched**; **WARN έΗΤ runs, DONE task + PENDING suggestion**; **THROTTLE έΗΤ runs on `gateway-fast`** (clinical.cds would default to QUALITY).
- Live meter aggregates by task type + model (2 calls έΗΤ `calls:2`, both task types present); other period (`2020-01`) έΗΤ total 0; malformed `?period=nope` έΗΤ 400; `ai.use`-only RECEPTION έΗΤ 403.
- Routing lists every task type quality-first (`clinical.cds` default QUALITY, `configured:false`); `PUT /ai/routing` cdsέΗΤFAST έΗΤ next run uses `gateway-fast`; `GET /ai/routing` needs `ai.budget.manage` (MANAGER έΗΤ 403).
- Existing 35 contract preserved: 864 including the prior gateway/decision/idempotency/budget-block tests.

### RLS isolation (db, pglite, real 01έΗΤ39)
`ai_spend_log` + `ai_budgets`: a tenant sees ONLY its own rows; one tenant's spend + cap NEVER visible to another; WITH CHECK blocks logging spend for / moving a row to another tenant (INSERT + UPDATE); NO tenant context έΗΤ zero rows (fail-closed). T1/T2 proven.

### Do-NOT-break honored
35's cost-capture + budget-enforcement contract intact έΑΦ 39 CONTROLS + VISUALIZES, 35 still ENFORCES (the gate is consulted inside `runAiTask`). Routing keeps quality-first as the default. Spend/budget/routing tenant-scoped. Flag-gated (`ai.suite`). `/ai/config` alias keeps 35 callers working.

### Notes / decisions
- `AiSpendLog` is a pure visibility ledger; `AiBudget.spent` remains the authoritative accumulation the gate reads έΑΦ the ledger is never the source of truth for enforcement (so a ledger write failure can never silently disable the cap).
- THROTTLE downgrades only the tier for that single run (mutates the resolved routing in-memory), never persists a config change έΑΦ the tenant's chosen routing is untouched.
- Reused commission's `isPeriodKey`/`periodRange` rather than adding parallel helpers (single source for the `YYYY-MM` window; resolved the duplicate-export ambiguity at the `@mp/shared` barrel).

WORK TYPE: FEATURE (branch feat/39-ai-cost-control). Ended with `[CHECKPOINT]`. Controller handles the staging merge.

---

## Build-step 38 έΑΦ AI Suite: Feedback & Learning (`ai.suite`)

**Work-type:** FEATURE. **Phase:** AI Suite (item 4). **Branch:** `feat/38-ai-feedback-learning` (stacked on `feat/37-ai-suite-ops`). **Depends on:** 35 (tasks/suggestions + the HITL guard), 36 (rx.read + `ai.clinical`), 37, 06 (audit), 11 (consent/policy framing). **Ended with `[CHECKPOINT]`.**

**Schema / migration / RLS / auth / flags impact:** NEW migration `20260705320000_ai_feedback_learning` έΑΦ 3 tenant-scoped tables + 2 enums, ALL under the canonical `apply_tenant_rls` policy (02). NEW permission `ai.rules.review` (TENANT-scoped) granted additively to ADMIN / DOCTOR / PHARMACIST (TENANT_OWNER auto-includes via `permissionKeysByScope('TENANT')`; SUPER_ADMIN via full assignable set) έΑΦ no other grant touched. **Feature flag REUSED (`ai.suite`, owned by 35) έΑΦ no catalog change.** No auth/token change.

### Problem
AI must get better at each tenant's reality (their medicine names, abbreviations, phrasing, corrections) έΑΦ but uncontrolled "learning" is dangerous in healthcare. Need ΏθΣΞ/ΏθΣΟ + corrections feeding **per-tenant** memory/rules, with **safety-critical (clinical) changes gated behind human review** and **no unsafe retraining** of clinical safety behaviour.

### What changed
- **NEW pure `@mp/shared/ai-feedback`** (browser-safe; only dep `round2`; NO `Date.now()`): vocabulary (`FeedbackRating` UP/DOWN, `RuleStatusLit` PROPOSED/ACTIVE/REJECTED + guards); `isSafetyCriticalDomain` (`clinical`/`dosing`/`interaction`/`diagnosis`/`prescription`; **unknown/empty domain έΗΤ true, fail-safe**); `normalizeCorrection` (domain/scope/key/value); recurrenceέΗΤconfidence ramp (`confidenceForOccurrences`: `CONFIDENCE_PER_OCCURRENCE=0.4`, `MEMORY_ACTIVATION_CONFIDENCE=0.7` έΘΤ a one-off `0.4` is inactive, the 2nd occurrence `0.8` activates), `isMemoryActive`; `deriveLearning(correction, priorOccurrences)` έΗΤ EITHER a non-safety `DerivedMemory` (auto-active at threshold) OR a safety-critical `DerivedRule` **always `status:'PROPOSED'`, `safetyCritical:true`** (never a memory); `applyMedicineMappings(lines, mappings)` έΑΦ the ONLY place memory alters a downstream task: relabels a line whose label matches an ACTIVE scrawlέΗΤbrand mapping (case/space-insensitive), records `mappedFrom`+`mappedByMemory`, preserves every other field (assist-only έΑΦ never changes a safety flag). Exported from `@mp/shared` index.
- **NEW DB models** `AiFeedback` (id, tenantId, suggestionId, rating `Rating`, correction Json?, by, createdAt), `AiMemory` (id, tenantId, scope, key, value Json, confidence `Decimal(4,2)`, updatedAt, createdAt; `@@unique([tenantId,scope,key])`), `AiRule` (id, tenantId, domain, pattern Json, action Json, safetyCritical Bool, status `RuleStatus` @default(PROPOSED), reviewedBy?, createdAt, updatedAt) + enums `Rating`(UP/DOWN), `RuleStatus`(PROPOSED/ACTIVE/REJECTED); re-exported from `@mp/db`.
- **NEW `AiFeedbackModule`** (`apps/api/src/ai-feedback/`, imports FlagsModule + PermissionsModule + AiModule; **exports `AiFeedbackService`**). Controller `@Controller('ai')` gated `@RequireFeature('ai.suite')`: `POST suggestions/:id/feedback` (`ai.use`, `@Audited ai.feedback.record`), `GET feedback/memory` + `GET feedback/rules` (`ai.use`), `POST feedback/rules/:id/review` (`ai.rules.review`, `@Audited ai.feedback.reviewRule`). Service: `recordFeedback` verifies the suggestion is the tenant's OWN via 35 `getSuggestion` (404 else) έΗΤ counts PRIOR occurrences of the exact correction έΗΤ records `AiFeedback` έΗΤ `deriveLearning` έΗΤ upserts `AiMemory` (non-safety) or proposes `AiRule` (safety-critical, idempotent by domain+pattern). `reviewRule`: 404 if absent έΗΤ **a safety-critical/clinical-domain rule review requires `ai.clinical` (else 403)** έΗΤ `PROPOSED`έΗΤdecision (409 if already reviewed). OWNS the 3 tables via `PrismaAiFeedbackRepo` (all `runWithTenant`); `priorCorrectionCount` scans recent corrections (cap 1000) and compares scope+key+value in JS (portable across JSON dialects).
- **36 integration:** `ClinicalAiService` now injects `@Optional() AiFeedbackService`; `rxRead` pulls the tenant's ACTIVE medicine mappings and folds them into the floor via `applyMedicineMappings` (adds `memoryMappingsApplied`/`memoryMappings`; `mustVerify` stays true). `ClinicalAiModule` imports `AiFeedbackModule`; the 36 e2e overrides `AI_FEEDBACK_REPO` with the fake.
- **App wiring:** `AiFeedbackModule` registered in `AppModule` after `AiModule`, before `ClinicalAiModule`.
- **NO web surface** (backend suite; 36 rx.read consumes memory; a future review UI + a ΏθΣΞ/ΏθΣΟ widget will call it). **No new i18n keys** (parity preserved).

### Do-NOT-break adherence
Per-tenant scope absolute (every repo call `runWithTenant`; RLS + WITH CHECK proven; app-level cross-tenant-invisible test). Safety-critical rules `PROPOSED`-only, never auto-active (unit + e2e). No unsafe retraining έΑΦ memory touches ONLY the rx.read medicine-name relabel and never a safety flag; ACTIVE clinical rules are recorded but NOT auto-applied to alter a clinical check. All via 35 + `@Audited`. Flag-gated (`ai.suite`).

### Verification gates (all green)
- **turbo typecheck 27/27**, **lint 15/15** (0 errors; 1 pre-existing doctor-portal `no-explicit-any` warning, unrelated), **build+test 23/23**.
- **jest api 853/853** (74 suites; **+29**: new `ai-feedback-helpers` + `ai-feedback.e2e` + 2 new 36 rx.read memory tests). **jest db 173/173** (34 suites; **+6** new `ai-feedback-isolation.spec.ts`). **i18n 19/19 parity**. Prisma client regenerated.
- **Isolation (`ai-feedback-isolation`, real 01έΗΤ38 migrations in pglite, `app_user` + `app.tenant_id`):** each of `ai_feedback`/`ai_memory`/`ai_rules` tenant-scoped (T1/T2 see only own); one tenant's memory invisible to another; WITH CHECK blocks writing memory/feedback for another tenant + moving a rule cross-tenant (UPDATE); NO context έΗΤ zero rows (fail-closed).
- **Vertical smoke (e2e over the real graph JwtAuthGuard έΗΤ FeatureGuard `ai.suite` έΗΤ RolesGuard έΗΤ AuditInterceptor; 35/clinical/feedback repos faked):** no tokenέΗΤ401; no-`ai.suite`έΗΤ404 (feedback+memory+rules); feedback needs `ai.use` (RECEPTIONέΗΤ403); bare ΏθΣΞ/ΏθΣΟ recorded + audited, no learning without a correction; unknown suggestionέΗΤ404; bad rating/correctionέΗΤ400; **recurring non-safety mapping έΗΤ 1st inactive έΗΤ 2nd ACTIVE memory (listed) έΗΤ next `rx.read` relabels `augmntn 625`έΗΤ`Augmentin 625` with `mappedByMemory` and still `mustVerify:true`**; INACTIVE (0.4) mapping NOT applied; **`dosing` correction έΗΤ PROPOSED rule that stays PROPOSED (never auto-active), no memory written**; rule review needs `ai.rules.review` (SALESMANέΗΤ403); admin activates έΗΤ `ACTIVE` + `reviewedBy` + audited έΗΤ re-reviewέΗΤ409; **clinical rule review on an `ai.suite`-but-not-`ai.clinical` tenantέΗΤ403**; unknown ruleέΗΤ404; **one tenant's memory never visible to another** (app-level; RLS proven in db).

### Files
- **NEW:** `packages/shared/src/ai-feedback.ts`; `packages/db/prisma/migrations/20260705320000_ai_feedback_learning/migration.sql`; `packages/db/src/ai-feedback-isolation.spec.ts`; `apps/api/src/ai-feedback/{ai-feedback.constants,ai-feedback.dto,ai-feedback.repositories,ai-feedback.service,ai-feedback.controller,ai-feedback.module,index,__fakes__,ai-feedback-helpers.spec,ai-feedback.e2e.spec}.ts`.
- **EDITED:** `packages/shared/src/index.ts` (export ai-feedback); `packages/shared/src/permissions.ts` (`ai.rules.review` + grants); `packages/db/prisma/schema.prisma` (3 models + 2 enums); `packages/db/src/index.ts` (export `Rating`/`RuleStatus`); `apps/api/src/app.module.ts` (register `AiFeedbackModule`); `apps/api/src/clinical-ai/{clinical-ai.service,clinical-ai.module}.ts` (memory injection into rx.read); `apps/api/src/clinical-ai/clinical-ai.e2e.spec.ts` (feedback-repo override + 2 memory tests).

WORK TYPE: FEATURE (branch feat/38-ai-feedback-learning). Ended with `[CHECKPOINT]`. Controller handles the staging merge.
