## Build-step 37 έΑΦ AI Suite: Operations (Advisory) (`ai.ops`)

**Status:** έεΖ DONE/APPROVED (2026-07-05) ┬╖ **Branch:** `feat/37-ai-suite-ops` (WORK TYPE: FEATURE) ┬╖ **Spec:** `specs/37-ai-suite-ops.md` ┬╖ **Depends on:** 35 (gateway), 24 (dashboard data), 28 (stock/batches), 15 (appointments), 20 (sales velocity), 21/23 (financials). ┬╖ **CODEREF:** none matched 37 (only `37-ai-suite-ops.md`) έΑΦ proceeded on the spec alone. ┬╖ **Schema/RLS:** **NO migration έΑΦ OWNS no tables**; reuses 35's `ai_tasks`/`ai_suggestions` and READS existing appointment/sales/stock/batch/finance tables through its OWN `runWithTenant` repo (RLS is the floor; aggregates only, never raw/cross-tenant). ┬╖ **Flags:** all PRE-EXISTED έΑΦ `ai.ops` (dependsOn `ai.suite`) was added to the catalog in 35; `full`=FLAG_KEYS auto-includes it; source flags `clinic.appointments`/`pharmacy.inventory` pre-existed έΑΦ **no catalog/preset change**. ┬╖ **Permissions:** REUSED έΑΦ `ai.use` already held by TENANT_OWNER (all TENANT perms) / ADMIN / MANAGER (the owner/manager audience for ops); **no grant change**.

### Problem
Owners and managers want forward-looking, advisory help built on data they already have: who'll no-show, what to reorder, what will expire, what the numbers mean, and a natural-language way to ask έΑΦ surfaced through the dashboard (24) and the relevant modules (29 reorder, 28/15). All ADVISORY: a human acts; nothing auto-executes. Everything routes through the 35 gateway so it is logged, budgeted and per-tenant-keyed, and is surfaced only when the tenant owns both `ai.ops` and the specific insight's source module (no expiry insight without inventory).

### What changed
**Pure core `@mp/shared/ops-ai.ts`** (browser-safe, no `Date.now()` έΑΦ `asOf` is always passed in έΑΦ no provider/keys) έΑΦ the five ops task types + the deterministic ADVISORY FLOOR each returns before a real provider is wired (and the shape a provider answer is validated against later):
- `OPS_TASKS`/`OPS_TASK_TYPES`/`isOpsTask` έΑΦ the dotted task-type strings (`predict.noshow`, `predict.demand`, `predict.expiry`, `analytics.ask`, `ops.chat`); `AI_OPS_SUITE_FLAG` (re-exports the 35 `AI_OPS_FLAG`).
- `OPS_SURFACE_FLAG` + `opsSurfaceFlagFor(task)` έΑΦ the SOURCE-module flag each insight additionally rides (`predict.noshow`έΗΤ`clinic.appointments`, `predict.demand`/`predict.expiry`έΗΤ`pharmacy.inventory`; `analytics.ask`/`ops.chat`έΗΤnull, they read only what already exists).
- `predictNoShows(rows)` έΑΦ smoothed no-show probability per upcoming appointment from the patient's OWN prior attendance (Laplace prior PRIOR_SHOWS=4/PRIOR_MISSES=1 so a 1-of-1 miss έΚι certainty), HIGH/MEDIUM/LOW band, reminder/overbook suggestion, most-risky-first, `advisoryOnly:true`; `NOSHOW_SYSTEM_POLICY`/`_DISCLAIMER`.
- `predictDemand(rows, coverTargetDays=14)` έΑΦ daily velocity (`soldQty/windowDays`) έΗΤ days-of-cover έΗΤ reorder hint sized to restore the cover target (`ceil(velocity┬╖target έΙΤ onHand)`); reorders only when there's real velocity AND cover below target; lowest-cover-first, no-velocity last; `DEMAND_SYSTEM_POLICY`/`_DISCLAIMER`.
- `predictExpiryRisk(batches, asOf, horizonDays=90)` έΑΦ projects unsold-at-expiry from velocity (`atRiskQty = qty έΙΤ floor(velocity┬╖daysToExpiry)`); surfaces only batches within the horizon with real risk (already-expired OR some qty projected to survive), soonest-expiry-first, HIGH/MEDIUM/LOW band, promote/return suggestion; `EXPIRY_SYSTEM_POLICY`/`_DISCLAIMER`.
- `answerAnalytics(question, metrics)` έΑΦ **GROUNDED**: matches the question's words to the provided read-only metrics (by key+label), cites the exact figures with signed delta/`deltaPct`/direction (up/down/flat), explains the change; NEVER invents έΑΦ no match summarises what's available, no metrics says it has nothing to answer from; `grounded:true`+`readOnly:true`; `ANALYTICS_SYSTEM_POLICY`/`_DISCLAIMER`.
- `opsChatReply(question)` έΑΦ staff how-to/lookup from a small curated `OPS_HOWTO` book (refund/reorder/expiry/discount/appointment/report/stock/login) + an honest fallback pointing to a human; `advisoryOnly:true`; `OPS_CHAT_SYSTEM_POLICY`/`_DISCLAIMER`/`_FALLBACK`.
- `callCenterScaffold()` έΑΦ the ┬π2 goal 6 voice SCAFFOLD: a `CallCenterScaffold` descriptor of six DISABLED hook points (book/rescheduleέΗΤ15, reminder-confirmέΗΤ37, order-statusέΗΤ34, availabilityέΗΤ36, triage-handoffέΗΤ32, staff-how-toέΗΤ37) `deferredTo:43`, `advisoryOnly:true`; pure metadata, no AI call, no action.
- Added the 5 ops task types additively to `AI_TASK_TYPES` + `DEFAULT_TASK_TIER` in `ai-gateway.ts` (advisory, cost-aware: `predict.*`/`ops.chat`έΗΤFAST, `analytics.ask`έΗΤBALANCED).

**API `apps/api/src/ops-ai/` έΑΦ NEW `OpsAiModule` (owns no tables):**
- `ops-ai.controller.ts` έΑΦ `@Controller('ai/ops')` `@RequireFeature('ai.ops')` (FeatureGuard FIRST, 404 for a tenant without the ops sub-suite). `POST /ai/ops/{predict-noshow,predict-demand,predict-expiry,analytics-ask,ops-chat}` each `@HttpCode(200)` `@RequirePermission('ai.use')` `@Audited('ai.ops.*','ai_suggestion')`, plus read-only `GET /ai/ops/call-center/scaffold` (`ai.use`, no gateway call).
- `ops-ai.service.ts` έΑΦ per method: `requireSurface` (per-insight SOURCE flag via `opsSurfaceFlagFor` έΗΤ 404 if the source module is off) έΗΤ READ the tenant's own read-only aggregates from the repo έΗΤ compute the deterministic `@mp/shared` floor έΗΤ `run()` routes through **35 `AiGatewayService.runAiTask`** with `{ floor }` έΗΤ returns `{ id, taskType, decisionRequired:true, result:floor }`. `callCenter()` returns the pure scaffold (no gateway).
- `ops-ai.repositories.ts` έΑΦ abstract `OpsAiRepo` + `PrismaOpsAiRepo`: `noShowHistory` (upcoming WAITING appts + each patient's terminal-status/NO_SHOW counts via `groupBy`), `demandInputs` (per-medicine `SaleItem.qty` sum over the window + `Stock` on-hand + brand names), `expiryInputs` (near-expiry `Batch` rows + per-medicine velocity from the same window), `analyticsMetrics` (current-vs-prior-30-day `Sale` aggregate: sales/discount/transactions). Every method wrapped in `runWithTenant(tenantId)`.
- `ops-ai.dto.ts` έΑΦ thin parsers (prediction bodies optional `branchId`/`windowDays`/`coverTargetDays`/`horizonDays`; `analytics-ask`/`ops-chat` require a non-empty `question` έΗΤ 400). `ops-ai.constants.ts` (`AI_OPS_FEATURE`, `OPS_AI_REPO`/`OPS_AI_CLOCK` tokens, window/limit constants). `__fakes__.ts` (`FakeOpsAiRepo`, seeded per tenant). `index.ts`.
- Registered in `app.module.ts` after `ClinicalAiModule` (with a docstring paragraph); imports `FlagsModule`+`PermissionsModule`+`AiModule`.

### Verification gates (all green)
- **typecheck:** turbo 27/27 (`@mp/shared` rebuilt first έΑΦ resolves via built output). **lint:** 15/15, 0 errors, 1 warning (pre-existing `doctor-portal.repositories.ts:220` unused-disable, unrelated to 37). **build:** turbo 15/15. **turbo test:** 20/20.
- **jest api:** 824/824 (74 suites; **+28** = 15 unit `ops-ai-helpers.spec.ts` + 13 e2e `ops-ai.e2e.spec.ts`). **jest db:** 167/167 (33 suites; isolation INHERITED έΑΦ 37 owns no tables; all reads go through `runWithTenant` RLS). **i18n:** 19/19 parity (EN/UR/Roman).
- **Vertical smoke** (e2e over the REAL module graph JwtAuthGuardέΗΤFeatureGuard `ai.ops`έΗΤRolesGuard `ai.use`έΗΤAuditInterceptor, with the AI-gateway + ops repos faked and the REAL provider factory/mock provider; tenants T_FULL=full, T_NOAI=lab, T_PARTIAL=clinic+`ai.suite`/`ai.ops` overrides):
  - no tokenέΗΤ401; a tenant without `ai.ops`έΗΤ404 (suite absent).
  - **per-insight SOURCE flag** (Acceptance ┬π6): T_PARTIAL has `ai.ops` on but `pharmacy.inventory` off έΗΤ `predict-demand`/`predict-expiry`έΗΤ404, while `predict-noshow` (clinic.appointments, present)/`analytics-ask`/`ops-chat`έΗΤ200 έΑΦ "no expiry insight without inventory".
  - running an ops task needs `ai.use` έΗΤ RECEPTIONέΗΤ403.
  - `predict.noshow`: scores from history (flaky patient HIGH + first), routes through 35 (a DONE `AiTask` + a PENDING `AiSuggestion` carrying the advisory floor), audited; PENDING **not applicable** έΗΤ human APPROVES via the 35 decision surface έΗΤ applicable (advisory guard).
  - `predict.demand`: reorder hint sized 100 (10/day┬╖14 έΙΤ 40 on-hand); well-stocked item not reordered; `advisoryOnly`.
  - `predict.expiry`: slow-mover-near-expiry flagged, fast-mover-that-sells-through excluded; `advisoryOnly`.
  - `analytics.ask`: grounded answer over real aggregates, citations show profit 90 έΗΡ previous 150 direction DOWN; empty questionέΗΤ400.
  - `ops.chat`: matched how-to + PENDING suggestion; empty questionέΗΤ400.
  - call-center scaffold: `GET` returns `deferredTo:43` with every hook `enabled:false` and did NOT route through the gateway (0 tasks).

### Notes / decisions
- **Advisory-only by construction (┬π5 do-NOT-break):** every POST returns a PENDING 35 suggestion; nothing auto-acts. The predictions/answers are DETERMINISTIC `@mp/shared` composers (the safe floor the mock provider carries until a real one is wired), so the advisory guarantee is testable code, not model behaviour. The call-center piece is a metadata scaffold only (43 builds the agent).
- **`analytics.ask` grounding:** answers ONLY from the read-only aggregates the repo hands it (tenant-scoped, current-vs-prior period), cites the exact numbers, and never fabricates a figure/trend/cause έΑΦ satisfying ┬π3.3/┬π5 (no raw or cross-tenant access).
- **No new tables/flags/permissions:** the module reuses 35's persistence + the pre-existing catalog. `asOf` is injected via `OPS_AI_CLOCK` so the pure expiry math stays clock-free and deterministic in tests.

## Build-step 36 έΑΦ AI Suite: Clinical (Assist-Only) (`ai.clinical`)

**Status:** έεΖ DONE/APPROVED (2026-07-05) ┬╖ **Branch:** `feat/36-ai-suite-clinical` (WORK TYPE: FEATURE) ┬╖ **Spec:** `specs/36-ai-suite-clinical.md` ┬╖ **Depends on:** 35 (gateway), 18/20 (Rx/medicine), 19 (lab), 14 (allergies), 17/33 (consult). ┬╖ **CODEREF:** none (proceeded on the spec alone). ┬╖ **Schema/RLS:** **NO migration έΑΦ OWNS no tables**; reuses 35's `ai_tasks`/`ai_suggestions` and READS existing clinical/catalog tables through its OWN `runWithTenant` repo (RLS is the floor). ┬╖ **Flags:** all PRE-EXISTED (`ai.clinical`, `pharmacy.aiReader`, `pharmacy.pos`, `lab.results`, `clinic.consultation`; `full` preset) έΑΦ **no catalog change**. ┬╖ **Permissions:** `ai.use` GRANTED additively to PHARMACIST/SALESMAN/PATHOLOGIST/LAB_TECH (the clinical staff who run the AI); ADMIN/MANAGER/DOCTOR already held it.

### Problem
The biggest staff-capability gains are clinical (reading a script into a cart, catching interactions, explaining a report, flagging abnormals) έΑΦ AND the highest-risk. Each must be **assist-only**: AI drafts, a licensed human (pharmacist/doctor/pathologist) confirms and signs the medico-legal act. All six route through the 35 gateway so they are logged, budgeted and per-tenant-keyed, and are surfaced only when the tenant owns both `ai.clinical` and the specific module.

### What changed
**Pure core `@mp/shared/clinical-ai.ts`** (browser-safe, no `Date.now()`/provider/keys) έΑΦ the six clinical task types + the deterministic SAFETY FLOOR each returns before a real provider is wired (and the shape a provider answer is validated against later):
- `CLINICAL_TASKS`/`CLINICAL_TASK_TYPES`/`isClinicalTask` έΑΦ the dotted task-type strings (`rx.read`, `medicine.search`, `interaction.check`, `lab.explain`, `result.flag`, `note.summarize`); `AI_CLINICAL_SUITE_FLAG`.
- `CLINICAL_SURFACE_FLAG` + `surfaceFlagFor(task)` έΑΦ the MODULE flag each surface additionally rides (`rx.read`έΗΤ`pharmacy.aiReader`, `medicine.search`έΗΤ`pharmacy.pos`, `interaction.check`/`note.summarize`έΗΤ`clinic.consultation`, `lab.explain`/`result.flag`έΗΤ`lab.results`).
- `smartMedicineSearch(query, candidates)` έΑΦ brand/generic/**alternative**(same-generic)/**intent**(symptomέΗΤgeneric via `INTENT_CUES`) ranking, order-stable, `mustVerify:true`, flags Rx items; `intentGenericsFor(query)` exposed so the catalog fetch can widen to symptom-mapped generics; `MEDICINE_SEARCH_SYSTEM_POLICY`/`_DISCLAIMER`.
- `explainLabReport(values, lang)` έΑΦ plain-language line per analyte (within/above/below range) localised **EN + UR + Roman-UR**, `hasAbnormal`/`hasCritical`, `informationalOnly:true`; `LAB_EXPLAIN_SYSTEM_POLICY` + `labExplainDisclaimer(lang)`; `LabValueLite` (compatible with 19 `EvaluatedValue`).
- `flagAbnormalResults(values)` έΑΦ keeps only HIGH/LOW/CRITICAL, CRITICAL-first, neutral notes, `pathologistSigns:true` (never finalises); `RESULT_FLAG_SYSTEM_POLICY`/`_DISCLAIMER`.
- **rx.read / interaction.check / note.summarize REUSE the 33/34 composers** `composePrescriptionRead` (34), `crossCheckMedications` (33), `summarizeClinicalNote` (33) + their policies έΑΦ no duplication.
- Added the 6 clinical task types additively to `AI_TASK_TYPES` + `DEFAULT_TASK_TIER` in `ai-gateway.ts` (quality-first: `interaction.check`/`result.flag`έΗΤQUALITY; `rx.read`/`lab.explain`έΗΤBALANCED; `medicine.search`/`note.summarize`έΗΤFAST).

**35 gateway extension (backward-compatible):** `AiGatewayService.runAiTask(..., opts?: { floor })` έΑΦ when a suite passes its deterministic structured floor it is attached to the persisted suggestion as `output.result` (the free-text `output.text` stays the provider's raw output; the key is omitted entirely for plain 35 callers, so all 35 tests are unchanged). The mock provider still runs for honest token/cost/latency + budget.

**NEW `ClinicalAiModule`** (`apps/api/src/clinical-ai/`, imports FlagsModule + PermissionsModule + **AiModule**, exports the service):
- `ClinicalAiController` `@Controller('ai/clinical')` `@RequireFeature('ai.clinical')` FIRST έΗΤ 6 `POST` routes (`rx-read`, `medicine-search`, `interaction-check`, `lab-explain`, `result-flag`, `note-summarize`), each `@RequirePermission('ai.use')` + `@Audited({action:'ai.clinical.*'})`.
- `ClinicalAiService` έΑΦ per task: (1) `requireSurface` checks the MODULE flag via `FlagService` (404 if off), (2) gather real data (`interaction.check` fetches the patient's current meds 18 + allergies 14 by `patientId`; `medicine.search` does a 2-pass catalog fetch έΑΦ literal+intent terms, then widen by matched generics for alternatives), (3) compose the deterministic floor, (4) route through **35 `runAiTask`** with `{ floor }`, (5) return `{ id, taskType, decisionRequired:true, result }`. NO decision endpoint of its own έΑΦ the human decides via the 35 `POST /ai/suggestions/:id/decision` (only APPROVED/EDITED applies).
- `ClinicalAiRepo` (abstract + Prisma) έΑΦ READS `patient_allergies` (14), `prescriptions`/`prescription_items`/`medicines` (18/20) via `runWithTenant`, mirroring the 33 doctor-portal queries; OWNS no tables.
- `clinical-ai.dto.ts` έΑΦ plain-function parsers (400 on bad input) for all 6 bodies; `__fakes__.ts` `FakeClinicalAiRepo` (seeded catalog + patients); registered in `app.module.ts` after AiModule.

**No web surface** (backend suite; the existing POS 20 / lab 19 / consult 17 / doctor-portal 33 surfaces call these endpoints έΑΦ their own AI panels from 32/33/34 already exist). No new i18n keys (the composers emit EN+UR+Roman directly).

### Verification gates
- **turbo typecheck + lint 42/42** (0 errors; 1 pre-existing doctor-portal `no-explicit-any` warning έΑΦ my repo file carries no directive/warning).
- **turbo build + test 23/23.**
- **jest api 796/796** (70 suites; **+28**: `clinical-ai-helpers.spec` composers + `clinical-ai.e2e.spec` over the REAL module graph & the REAL 35 mock provider). **jest db 167/167** (unchanged έΑΦ 36 owns no tables; isolation inherited via `runWithTenant` RLS on the reused 35 + existing clinical tables). **i18n 19/19** parity.
- **Vertical smoke (e2e):** no tokenέΗΤ401; tenant without `ai.clinical`έΗΤ404 (suite absent); **per-surface module flag** έΑΦ T_PARTIAL (`ai.clinical` on, `pharmacy.aiReader`+`lab.results` off, `clinic.consultation` on) έΗΤ `rx-read`/`lab-explain`έΗΤ404 but `note-summarize`έΗΤ200; run needs `ai.use` (RECEPTIONέΗΤ403); **rx.read**έΗΤstructured `mustVerify` read + DONE `AiTask` + PENDING `AiSuggestion` carrying `output.result` + audited; PENDING not applicable έΗΤ APPROVE έΗΤ applicable (`canApply`); rx.read empty itemsέΗΤ400; **medicine.search**έΗΤbrand + same-generic alternative (2-pass widen) + intent (`fever`έΗΤparacetamol); **interaction.check**έΗΤuses the patient's REAL Warfarin + Penicillin-allergy έΗΤ DRUG_DRUG HIGH (warfarin+NSAID) + DRUG_ALLERGY (amoxicillin) + `highRisk`, `advisoryOnly:true` (never blocks), unknown patientέΗΤ404, neither patient nor medsέΗΤ400; **lab.explain**έΗΤplain-language EN/UR/Roman lines + `informationalOnly`, bad flagέΗΤ400; **result.flag**έΗΤCRITICAL-first, NORMAL excluded, `pathologistSigns:true`; **note.summarize**έΗΤ`draftOnly` summary, empty noteέΗΤ400.

### Notes / decisions
- **Assist-only is absolute (┬π5 do-NOT-break):** every task returns a PENDING suggestion; nothing mutates business data. The medico-legal act (dispense / sign the prescription / sign the lab result) stays the licensed human's, applied by the calling feature ONLY after `canApplySuggestion` passes on a human decision recorded via the 35 surface.
- **Owns no tables by design** (spec ┬πtop: "Reuses 35 AiTask/AiSuggestion (task types only)") έΑΦ the clinical task types are free-text `task_type` strings, so no enum/migration was needed. Isolation is inherited: the reused 35 tables have their pglite T1/T2 test; every clinical read goes through `runWithTenant`.
- `interaction.check`/`medicine.search` reach real 14/18/20 data through the module's OWN tenant-scoped repo (never importing the owning modules), exactly as 31/33 do.

## Build-step 35 έΑΦ AI Suite: AI Gateway (`@mp/ai`)

**Status:** έεΖ DONE/APPROVED (2026-07-05) ┬╖ **Branch:** `feat/35-ai-gateway` (WORK TYPE: FEATURE) ┬╖ **Spec:** `specs/35-ai-gateway.md` ┬╖ **Depends on:** 02 (tenancy/RLS), 04 (RBAC), 06 (audit), 10 (offline idempotency), 11, 13. ┬╖ **CODEREF:** none (proceeded on the spec alone). ┬╖ **Schema/RLS/flags:** NEW migration `έΑο310000` (4 tenant-scoped tables + 3 enums; `apply_tenant_rls`├Ω4). Feature flags + permissions all PRE-EXISTED (no catalog change).

### Problem
Many features want AI, but scattered direct provider calls would be unsafe, unauditable, uncontrollable on cost, and provider-locked. We need ONE gateway: provider-agnostic, per-tenant keys, per-task model routing, quality-first tiering, **human-in-the-loop by construction**, full logging, and budget caps έΑΦ so "assist-only" and cost control are STRUCTURAL, not per-feature hopes. Earlier AI hooks (15/16/17/18/20/32/33/34) degrade until this exists, then light up.

### What changed
**Pure core `@mp/shared/ai-gateway.ts`** (browser-safe, dependency-light, no `Date.now()`/provider/keys) έΑΦ the structural guarantees as testable code:
- Vocabulary mirroring the DB enums: `AiTier` (FAST/BALANCED/QUALITY) ┬╖ `AiTaskStatus` (QUEUED/RUNNING/DONE/FAILED) ┬╖ `SuggestionDecision` (PENDING/APPROVED/REJECTED/EDITED) + lists + guards (`isAiTier`/`isAiTaskStatus`/`isSuggestionDecision`/`isHumanDecision`).
- **`canApplySuggestion(decision)`** έΑΦ THE human-in-the-loop guard: applicable ONLY if `APPROVED`/`EDITED`; a PENDING/REJECTED/unknown/null decision is NEVER applicable (fail-safe). Every AI surface routes an application through this. Plus `isPendingDecision`/`isTerminalDecision`.
- Per-task **quality-first routing**: `AI_TASK_TYPES` + `DEFAULT_TASK_TIER` (`clinical.cds`έΗΤQUALITY, `clinical.triage`/`pharmacy.rxRead`έΗΤBALANCED, `ops.*`έΗΤFAST) + `tierForTask(taskType, overrides)` (tenant override wins; unknownέΗΤ`DEFAULT_TIER`=BALANCED).
- Cost + budget math: `DEFAULT_TIER_RATE` (placeholder per-1k-token rates), `estimateCost`/`estimateCostForTier`/`round4`, `periodKeyFor` (UTC `YYYY-MM`), `budgetRemaining`, `isOverBudget` (capέΚν0 έΘΤ no cap), `wouldExceedBudget`.
- `AI_GATEWAY_SYSTEM_POLICY` έΑΦ the master assist-only system prompt every provider call is prefixed with; `AI_SUITE_FLAG`/`AI_OPS_FLAG` constants.

**Engine `@mp/ai`** (rewrote the pre-35 scaffold, `@mp/shared` dep added; **backward-compatible**):
- `AiProvider` interface (`complete(req) έΗΤ AiResult`; the single swappable seam) + `AiCompletionRequest`/`AiResult`.
- `MockAiProvider` έΑΦ deterministic, network-free, assist-only (echoes a human-review-required suggestion; tokens έΚΙ chars/4). The safe default until a real SDK+key is wired.
- `createAiGateway(config)` EXTENDED: optional `provider`/`tierOverrides`/`models`. `isConfigured()` = provider present; `route(taskType)` = tier+model; `complete({taskType,input,taskPolicy})` prepends the master policy via `buildSystemPrompt` and runs the provider. **CRITICAL do-NOT-break preserved:** the 32/33/34 feature seams call `createAiGateway({tenantId})` (no provider) έΗΤ `isConfigured()` false έΗΤ they still fall back to their deterministic `@mp/shared` composers. `costOf`/`estimateTokens`/`defaultModelFor` helpers; `AI_ASSIST_ONLY` kept.

**API `AiModule`** (`apps/api/src/ai/`): `@RequireFeature('ai.suite')` FIRST (404 if off) έΗΤ per-route `@RequirePermission`.
- `POST /ai/tasks` (`ai.use`, `@Audited`, `@IdempotencyKey`) έΑΦ `runAiTask`: mask input (`maskAuditSummary`) έΗΤ resolve routing from the tenant's config (else quality-first default) έΗΤ **budget: block if the period cap is reached, recording a FAILED task and leaving spend untouched (403)** έΗΤ `gateway.complete()` via the injected `AiProviderFactory` έΗΤ persist `AiTask` (status DONE, model, tokensIn/out, `costEstimate`, `latencyMs`, createdBy) έΗΤ `incrementSpend` έΗΤ create a PENDING `AiSuggestion`. Rides `SyncService.runIdempotent` when an `Idempotency-Key` is present so a queued offline AI action replayed on reconnect returns the SAME suggestion without re-running the provider (offline queue, ┬π5; the 10 outbox already models an `ai` action).
- `POST /ai/suggestions/:id/decision` (`ai.use`, `@Audited`) έΑΦ `decideSuggestion`: PENDINGέΗΤAPPROVED/REJECTED/EDITED (EDIT replaces output); already-decided έΗΤ 409; unknown έΗΤ 404.
- `GET /ai/suggestions/:id`, `GET /ai/tasks`(+`/:id`) (`ai.use`) έΑΦ the logs.
- `GET /ai/budget` (`ai.use`) + `PUT /ai/budget` (`ai.budget.manage`, `@Audited`) έΑΦ period cap + spend + remaining/over view.
- `GET /ai/config` + `PUT /ai/config` (`ai.budget.manage`, `@Audited`) έΑΦ per-task routing upsert; **a body with `apiKey`/`key`/`secret` is refused (400)** έΑΦ keys are never persisted.
- Service methods `canApply`/`assertApplicable` are what the coming suites (36/37) call before applying a suggestion; `AiGatewayService` is exported so they inject it and go through `runAiTask`+`decideSuggestion` έΑΦ no direct provider calls anywhere (┬π5).

**Secret store** `AiSecretStore` / `EnvAiSecretStore` έΑΦ per-tenant keys read from env (`AI_KEY_<TENANTID>` έΗΤ `AI_PROVIDER_KEY` fallback), NEVER the DB. The `ai_provider_configs` table has NO key column. `AiProviderFactory`/`DefaultAiProviderFactory` build the per-tenant gateway (provider chosen by config; mock until a real SDK branch is added) έΑΦ swapping the provider is config-only.

**Data model (OWNS 4 tables):** `ai_provider_configs` (tenant+taskType routing, **no key**), `ai_tasks` (uniform request + cost/latency), `ai_suggestions` (output + human decision, FKέΗΤtask cascade), `ai_budgets` (per-period cap + spend, unique tenant+period). All tenant-scoped via the canonical `apply_tenant_rls` policy (02). Enums `AiTier`/`AiTaskStatus`/`SuggestionDecision` exported from `@mp/db`.

**Flags/permissions:** REUSED έΑΦ `ai.suite`/`ai.clinical`/`ai.ops` already in the 05 catalog (`full` preset has them); permissions `ai.use` + `ai.budget.manage` already granted (ADMIN both; MANAGER/DOCTOR `ai.use`). NO catalog change.

**Web:** none έΑΦ this is a backend primitive; the detailed budget/cost surface is deferred to 39. i18n untouched (parity intact).

### Verification gates (all green)
- **turbo typecheck + lint:** 42/42 (0 errors; 1 pre-existing `doctor-portal.repositories.ts` unused-eslint-disable warning, unrelated).
- **turbo build + test:** 23/23. Web builds unchanged (no new page).
- **jest api:** 768/768 (68 suites; **+37**) έΑΦ new `ai-helpers.spec.ts` (HITL guard incl. fail-safe unknown/null; routing quality-first + override; cost det. + clamp; budget cap/period math; mock provider determinism + assist-only wording + overrides + master-policy prefix), `ai-secret-store.spec.ts` (null w/o env; per-tenant over shared; factory builds configured gateway w/ no key in code), `ai.e2e.spec.ts` (full HTTP smoke below).
- **jest db:** 167/167 (33 suites; **+6** `ai-gateway-isolation`) έΑΦ real 01έΗΤ35 migrations in pglite: 4-table T1/T2 scoping, budget-spend never cross-tenant, WITH-CHECK blocks insert/UPDATE-move to another tenant, NO-context fail-closed.
- **i18n parity:** 19/19 (ENέΗΦUR identical; untouched).
- **Isolation:** configs/tasks/suggestions/budgets tenant-scoped; one tenant's keys/spend never visible to another (┬π6 proven).
- **Vertical/flag smoke (e2e over the real graph + REAL mock provider):** no tokenέΗΤ401; no-`ai.suite` tenant (lab preset)έΗΤ404 on tasks + budget; run needs `ai.use` (RECEPTIONέΗΤ403); `runAiTask` routes clinical.cdsέΗΤQUALITY (`gateway-quality`), persists tokensIn/out+cost>0+latency, returns PENDING suggestion, audited (`ai.task.run`); unknown task typeέΗΤsafe BALANCED default; no inputέΗΤ400; **HITL** (PENDING έΗΤ `canApply` false + `assertApplicable` throws έΗΤ APPROVE έΗΤ applicable + audited έΗΤ re-decideέΗΤ409); REJECTED never applicable; EDIT without outputέΗΤ400 then with output records it; decide unknownέΗΤ404 / invalid decisionέΗΤ400; **spend accumulates** (GET /ai/budget spent>0); **over-capέΗΤ403 + a FAILED task recorded, no suggestion, spend not mutated**; budget set needs `ai.budget.manage` (MANAGERέΗΤ403, ADMIN 200 remaining=cap); **same `Idempotency-Key` replays the SAME suggestion έΑΦ exactly one task + one suggestion persisted (provider ran once)**; config upsert (no key) OK + a body with `apiKey`έΗΤ400 + config read needs `ai.budget.manage` (MANAGERέΗΤ403).
- **White-label / performance:** N/A (no web surface).

### Notes / decisions
- **`@mp/ai` now depends on `@mp/shared`** (`workspace:*`) έΑΦ single source of truth for the tier/cost/routing vocab; turbo `^build` orders it. The pre-35 `createAiGateway`/`isConfigured`/`AI_ASSIST_ONLY` surface is preserved verbatim so the 32/33/34 seams keep compiling and keep falling back to their safe composers (they construct provider-less gateways).
- **Budget enforcement = block-if-already-over** (before the run), recorded as a FAILED `AiTask`; a positive cap is required to block (cap 0 έΘΤ opt-in / no cap). Cap is stored at 2dp (currency); spend at 4dp (token-level cost).
- **Offline queue** for AI is satisfied structurally: the 10 outbox already carries an `ai` action (`requiresNetwork`), and the server dedupes the replay via the idempotency seam έΑΦ no double provider call.
- Provider is the deterministic `MockAiProvider` for every provider name today; adding a real provider (Anthropic/OpenAI/έΑο) is a single new branch in `DefaultAiProviderFactory.resolveProvider` using `AiSecretStore.getKey(tenantId, name)` έΑΦ no schema/API change. 36/37 will wire `ai.clinical`/`ai.ops` surfaces to call `runAiTask`+`decideSuggestion`.

## Build-step 34 έΑΦ Phase 3: Online Pharmacy (Own Store)

**Status:** έεΖ DONE/APPROVED (2026-07-05) ┬╖ **Branch:** `feat/34-online-pharmacy` (WORK TYPE: FEATURE) ┬╖ **Spec:** `specs/34-online-pharmacy.md` ┬╖ **Depends on:** 20 (catalog/stock), 28 (batch/FEFO), 14, 18 (Rx), 21 (payment/COD), 09, 13.

### Problem
The pharmacy wants to sell online under its OWN brand with home delivery, but (a) prescription medicines must be pharmacist-validated before dispensing, (b) online stock must stay consistent with the counter so the two never oversell the same batch, and (c) delivery + COD must be tracked. It's a public-facing store, so it must hit the 90+ mobile bar. (Multi-vendor marketplace = deferred 45.)

### What changed
**Two invariants, both provable in code (not left to the runtime or the model):**
- **RX ASSIST-ONLY:** a basket with any prescription-required line parks in `RX_REVIEW`; a pharmacist approves before anything is dispensed. The AI read (`OnlineRxReadGateway`έΗΤ`@mp/ai` 36 under `RX_READ_SYSTEM_POLICY`έΗΤdeterministic `composePrescriptionRead` floor) ALWAYS returns `mustVerify: true` and NEVER approves.
- **NO-OVERSELL:** online fulfilment decrements the SAME `stock`/`batches` tables as the counter (20/28) via a GUARDED atomic decrement έΑΦ `stock.updateMany({ where: { έΑο, qty: { gte: want } }, data: { qty: { decrement: want } } })` inside one transaction; zero matched rows έΘΤ `OnlineStockError` έΘΤ rollback (all-or-nothing). FEFO per-batch decrement + a SALE `StockMovement` mirror the 20 finalize hook. Reused `allocateFefo` + `round2` from `@mp/shared`.

**API έΑΦ NEW `OnlinePharmacyModule`** (`@RequireFeature('pharmacy.online')` FIRST on every controller; THREE role-scoped controllers over ONE service):
- **Customer** `@Roles(Role.PATIENT)`: `GET /online/catalog?q=` (searchable catalog: label/price/stock/requiresRx), `POST /online/orders` (checkout έΑΦ patient resolved from principal like 31, prices from catalog never body, `initialOrderStatus` = RX_REVIEW if any `requiresRx` else PLACED, reserve at PLACED else on approval, best-effort invoice + notify), `GET /online/orders` (own), `GET /online/orders/:id` (track; strangerέΗΤindistinguishable 404).
- **Pharmacist** `@RequirePermission('pharmacy.cashier')`: `GET /online/ops/review` (RX_REVIEW queue), `GET /online/ops/orders/:id/rx-read` (assist-only read beside the image), `POST έΑο/decision` (approveέΗΤreserveέΗΤAPPROVED / rejectέΗΤCANCELLED), `POST έΑο/status` (PACKED/CANCELLED only έΑΦ delivery is rider-driven), `POST έΑο/assign` (riderέΗΤOUT_FOR_DELIVERY), `GET/POST /online/ops/riders`.
- **Rider** `@Roles(Role.RIDER)`: `GET /online/rider/assignments` (own; caller's own `Rider` resolved by `userId`), `POST έΑο/:id/status` (proof-gated DELIVERED, reason-gated FAILED, ownέΗΤ404; DELIVERED έΗΤ order DELIVERED + COD settled).
- Writes `@Audited`. Payment/COD REUSES `BillingService` (21, best-effort like home-collection: `createInvoice` source OTHER `refId=orderId` at placement; ONLINE prepaid via `pay('ONLINE')`, CASH=COD settled via `pay('CASH')` on delivery; invoice patient link via refId έΑΦ decoupled from cross-module patient ids). Per-status WhatsApp via `NotificationService` (09, best-effort). No FlagService needed in-service (all gating at the guard layer).

**Data model έΑΦ OWNS 4 tables + 1 additive column.** `online_orders`, `online_order_items` (orderέΗΤitems cascade FK), `riders`, `delivery_assignments`; additive `medicines.requires_rx BOOLEAN DEFAULT false` (the authoritative Rx-review source, same precedent as 20 adding salePrice/costPrice). Migration `20260705300000_online_pharmacy` έΑΦ `ALTER medicines`, 2 enums (`OnlineStatus`; **`RiderStatus`** έΑΦ deliberately named to AVOID colliding with the existing 09 `DeliveryStatus` message enum), 4 CREATE TABLEs + indexes + the orderέΗΤitems FK, `apply_tenant_rls`├Ω4. Enums exported from `@mp/db`. All catalog/stock/patient/branch data REUSED via the module's OWN tenant-scoped repo (31 precedent), never importing 20/28/14.

**Pure `@mp/shared/online-pharmacy`** (added to the barrel; no package.json change): `PHARMACY_ONLINE_FLAG`; `OnlineStatusLit`/`RiderStatusLit` + `ONLINE_STATUS_FLOW`/`RIDER_STATUS_FLOW` + `canTransition*`/`nextStatuses`/`orderStatusForDelivery`; `requiresPharmacistReview`/`initialOrderStatus`; `orderItemsSubtotal`/`orderTotal` (reuse 20 `round2`); `RX_READ_SYSTEM_POLICY`/`RX_READ_DISCLAIMER`/`composePrescriptionRead` (deterministic assist-only floor). Backs BOTH the API service and the web storefront so they agree by construction.

**Flags:** `pharmacy.online` (dependsOn `pharmacy.pos`) already existed in the catalog έΑΦ added it to the `pharmacy` + `clinic_pharmacy` presets in `@mp/flags`. NO new permission (role/perm-gated). Updated the one flags.service spec that used `pharmacy.online` as its "off-in-preset-but-parent-on" example έΗΤ switched to `lab.homeCollection` (still off in the lab preset with parent `lab.catalog` on).

**Web** (Next 15 app-router islands, brand-themed via 07 CSS vars, `noindex`): `/store` έΑΦ UR-first customer storefront (catalog/search, local cart, checkout with address + COD/online + Rx-image key, my orders/track; degrades to sign-in/no-access), **registered in `lighthouserc.json` `collect.url` for the 90+ mobile gate**; `/rider` έΑΦ EN-first rider PWA (own assignments, proof/reason-gated status buttons); `/rx-desk` έΑΦ EN-first pharmacist queue (assist-only read + `mustVerify` + Approve/Reject). Manifest shortcuts added for `/store` + `/rider`. i18n: `st*`/`rd*`/`rq*` keys added to BOTH en.json + ur.json (parity 19/19).

### Verification gates (all green)
- **turbo typecheck + lint 42/42** (0 errors; 1 pre-existing `no-explicit-any` unused-directive WARNING in `doctor-portal.repositories.ts`, present on HEAD έΑΦ non-fatal, not this step's file). **turbo test + build 23/23.**
- **jest api 731/731** (65 suites; +19: `online-pharmacy.e2e` + `online-pharmacy-helpers`). **jest db 161/161** (32 suites; +6: `online-pharmacy-isolation`). **i18n 19/19 parity.**
- **Web build:** `/store` 2.45 kB / 144 kB, `/rider` 1.64 kB / 143 kB, `/rx-desk` 1.58 kB / 143 kB έΑΦ all far under the 250 kB script budget.
- **Isolation (pglite, real migrations 01έΗΤ34):** 4-table T1/T2 tenant-scoping + WITH-CHECK blocks cross-tenant order/assignment + fail-closed (no context έΗΤ 0 rows), PLUS a guarded-decrement test proving the shared `stock` never goes negative (second over-quantity reserve matches 0 rows).
- **Vertical smoke (e2e over the REAL module graph + REAL Rx gateway floor, Prisma/billing faked):** no tokenέΗΤ401; no-`pharmacy.online` tenantέΗΤ404; non-PATIENT on storefrontέΗΤ403; PATIENT on opsέΗΤ403; browse catalog + place OTC order (shared stock 10έΗΤ8) + audited; unknown medicineέΗΤ400; lists ONLY my orders + stranger trackέΗΤ404; **no-oversell** (two 6-of-10 orders έΗΤ 2nd 409, stock stays 4); Rx basketέΗΤRX_REVIEW with NOTHING reserved έΗΤ assist-only read (`mustVerify`, disclaimer) έΗΤ approveέΗΤAPPROVED + reserved (5έΗΤ3); pharmacist rejectέΗΤCANCELLED (never dispensed, stock untouched); packέΗΤassign riderέΗΤOUT_FOR_DELIVERY έΗΤ rider pick έΗΤ deliver requires proof έΗΤ DELIVERED + COD payment recorded (order.paid); rider w/o profileέΗΤ404; another rider's assignmentέΗΤ404; pharmacy-preset tenant present.

### Notes / decisions
- **Public storefront = authenticated PATIENT surface.** The platform serves all tenants under ONE shared host and derives the tenant from the principal (the custom-domain path is dormant); `@RequireFeature` fail-closes to 404 without a tenant. So a truly-anonymous guest storefront can't resolve a tenant/flag today έΑΦ the customer surface is `@Roles(PATIENT)` (consistent with the "public-facing" 31 PWA, which is likewise authenticated). `online_orders.guest_phone` is reserved (nullable) for the future guest/custom-domain path.
- **No compensating restock on CANCEL** (yet): a cancelled order that had already reserved stock leaves the decrement in place (reconciled via 28) έΑΦ kept simple; the no-oversell invariant (never dispense more than on-hand) is the priority and holds.
- **Delivery enum renamed** `RiderStatus` to avoid colliding with the existing 09 `DeliveryStatus` (message-delivery) enum.

WORK TYPE: FEATURE (branch feat/34-online-pharmacy). Ended with `[CHECKPOINT]`. Controller handles the staging merge.

## Build-step 33 έΑΦ Phase 3: Doctor Portal + AI Decision Support

**Status:** έεΖ DONE/APPROVED (2026-07-05) ┬╖ **Branch:** `feat/33-doctor-portal-ai` (WORK TYPE: FEATURE) ┬╖ **Spec:** `specs/33-doctor-portal-ai.md` ┬╖ **Depends on:** 14, 15, 17, 18, 19, 22, 35 (gateway), 13.

**Schema/RLS/flags impact.** ONE new owned tenant table `cds_suggestions` + enum `CdsStatus` (migration `έΑο290000`); RLS via canonical `apply_tenant_rls` (T1/T2 + WITH-CHECK + fail-closed proven in new `doctor-portal-isolation` pglite spec over 01έΗΤ33). **Flags REUSED έΑΦ NO catalog change, NO new permission:** the whole surface is gated `clinic.doctorPortal` (pre-existed, dependsOn `clinic.consultation`) FIRST έΗΤ `@Roles(Role.DOCTOR)`; the AI panel additionally gated on `ai.clinical` (pre-existed) checked in the service. Role-gated (a DOCTOR holds ZERO RBAC permissions), like 31/32.

**Problem.** Doctors want to work outside the consultation room (review patients/history/reports, write notes + e-prescriptions, see earnings, self-schedule) AND want AI decision support έΑΦ but CDS that DECIDES is unsafe + a liability. It must ASSIST; the doctor decides and signs.

**What shipped.** The doctor's remote workspace + **assist-only CDS** (Phase 3, item 3). This module IS the "33/36" clinical gateway the 17 consultation AI-assist referenced as not-yet-wired.
- **NEW `DoctorPortalModule`** (`@RequireFeature('clinic.doctorPortal')` 404 FIRST έΗΤ `@Roles(Role.DOCTOR)` 403 for other staff). Every path resolves the caller's OWN `Doctor` (by `principal.userId έΗΤ Doctor.userId`) and scopes to it έΑΦ a doctor sees ONLY their own patients/appointments/reports/suggestions, and the `doctorId` on any write is ALWAYS the caller (never a body field έΗΤ cannot write in another doctor's name). Patient scope is HARD: a patient is reachable only if they share an appointment or a prior encounter (`assertLinked` έΗΤ indistinguishable 404 otherwise).
- **Endpoints:** `GET /doctor/me` (own profile), `/doctor/appointments`(?date/status), `/doctor/patients`, `/doctor/patients/:id` (profile + allergies + current meds + lab reports + prior encounters, scoped); `POST /doctor/encounters`(+`PATCH /:id`) writing notes/diagnoses (17 shape, forced identity); `POST /doctor/prescriptions` (18 shape, forced identity) έΑΦ mirrors the **18 allergy contract**: proposed meds cross-checked against the patient's REAL recorded allergies (14) έΗΤ an allergy conflict without `allergyOverrideReason` is REJECTED **409**, re-submit with a reason (captured); `GET /doctor/earnings` (REUSES `CommissionService.myEarnings` so the numbers **MATCH 22**); self-scheduling `GET/POST/DELETE /doctor/availability`, `GET/POST/DELETE /doctor/leave`, `GET /doctor/slots?date=` (availability έΙΤ leave έΙΤ booked via the SAME pure `buildDaySlots` 15 uses); **AI CDS** `POST /doctor/cds/suggest` (needs `ai.clinical` έΗΤ 404 if off), `POST /doctor/cds/:id/decision`, `GET /doctor/cds`(+`/:id`, own-scopedέΗΤ404).
- **CDS is ASSIST-ONLY:** the machine SUGGESTS (differentials to consider, drug-drug + drug-allergy interaction flags from the patient's REAL meds (18) + allergies (14), note summary); every suggestion is LOGGED (`cds_suggestions`, created `PENDING`); the doctor's **accept/edit/reject** is a SEPARATE, logged act (`status`+`decidedAt`+`decisionNote`). **Nothing auto-writes.** Generation routes through an injected `DoctorCdsGateway` seam via **`@mp/ai` (35)** under the exported `CDS_SYSTEM_POLICY`; until 35 wires a provider it returns the deterministic `composeCdsSuggestions` έΑΦ the guaranteed **safety FLOOR**.
- **OWNS only 1 table** (`cds_suggestions`); all clinical data REUSES the existing tables through its OWN tenant-scoped repo (patient-app precedent), never importing 14/15/17/18/19; earnings REUSE `CommissionService`.
- **Pure `@mp/shared/doctor-cds`** (`suggestDifferentials`/`crossCheckMedications`/`summarizeClinicalNote`/`composeCdsSuggestions`/`cdsDisclaimer`/`CDS_SYSTEM_POLICY`/`drugClassesOf`; `DoctorCdsKind`/`CdsSuggestionStatus`/`CdsSeverity`; `DOCTOR_PORTAL_FLAG`/`AI_CLINICAL_FLAG`) έΑΦ the assist-only guarantee lives here as testable code (class-based drug knowledge: penicillin/cephalosporin/sulfa/NSAID/anticoagulant/ACE/opioid/benzo/έΑο; known dangerous class-pairs; EN+Roman-Urdu symptom cues), never left to the language model.
- **Web** EN-first (staff surface), UR-ready `/doctor` lean client island (`mp-*` classes; tabs Today/Patients/Earnings/Schedule; patient view with history/reports; write-note + e-prescription forms with the 409έΗΤoverride flow; **AI suggestion panel** "suggestions έΑΦ you decide" with differentials/interactions/high-risk banner + Accept/Edit/Reject; earnings breakdown; availability editor + slots). StatusέΗΤstate gating off the API (`/doctor/me` probe: 200 ready / 401 signin / 403┬╖404 noaccess); the AI panel degrades to a clean "not enabled" on 404. `robots:{index:false}`.

**Gate results.** typecheck **27/27** ┬╖ lint **15/15** (0 warn) ┬╖ build **15/15** (`/doctor` 3.48 kB / 144 kB, within the `/*` Lighthouse budget) ┬╖ jest **api 712/712 (63 suites; +35)** + **db 155/155 (31 suites; +4 doctor-portal-isolation)** + i18n **19/19 parity** (EN+UR `dp*` keys) ┬╖ turbo test **20/20**.

**Vertical smoke (via the e2e over the real module graph + the REAL gateway seam).** no tokenέΗΤ401; tenant without `clinic.doctorPortal`έΗΤ404; non-DOCTORέΗΤ403; DOCTOR with no linked `Doctor`έΗΤ404; own profile returned; lists ONLY my appointments + patients (a colleague's leak blocked); patient view scoped + a stranger not in my careέΗΤ404; encounter written in the doctor's OWN name (a spoofed body `doctorId` ignored) + audited; encounter for a strangerέΗΤ404; e-prescription allergy conflictέΗΤ409 then overrideέΗΤcreated; earnings via commission (own data, matches 22); self-schedule availability + slots reflect the booked 10:00 as unavailable + delete; CDS returns assist-only differentials + a drug-allergy flag from REAL records, logged PENDING (nothing auto-written) + audited, then ACCEPTED as the doctor's act; CDS ABSENT when `ai.clinical` off (404) while the rest of the portal works; another doctor cannot read my suggestionέΗΤ404; empty CDS kindsέΗΤ400.

**Do-NOT-break honored.** Encounter/prescription/lab/commission contracts preserved (structurally-identical rows written additively via the own repo like 31; the 18 allergy-override contract mirrored; earnings reuse `CommissionService` verbatim). CDS stays assist-only (suggest έΗΤ human confirm + sign; nothing auto-writes) and goes through the 35 gateway seam. Patient-data scope is hard (own patients only). Flag-gated (portal + AI panel).

**Notes / decisions.** Chose the patient-app (31) OWN-fat-repo precedent over importing 14/15/17/18/19 services: it keeps reads+writes coherent in one store (a single fake for the e2e) and avoids split-brain module fakes, while the important invariants (allergy check before prescribing, forced doctor identity, audit) are preserved explicitly. Earnings alone REUSE `CommissionService` (one import) so the numbers match 22 exactly. The `ai.clinical` sub-gate 404s (flag-precedence: capability absent έΘΤ forbidden server-side) rather than returning a disabled-200, and the web panel degrades cleanly on that 404.

## Build-step 21 έΑΦ Phase 1: Billing & Cashier

**Status:** έεΖ DONE/APPROVED (2026-07-04) ┬╖ **Branch:** `feat/21-billing-cashier` (WORK TYPE: FEATURE) ┬╖ **Spec:** `specs/21-billing-cashier.md`

**What shipped.** ONE billing surface across OPD (17), lab (19) and pharmacy (20) έΑΦ the founding "cash is where money leaks" pain:
- **Unified invoice** built from an **enabled source** and adapting to the tenant's flags: `CONSULT` (`clinic.consultation`) / `LAB` + `PACKAGE` (`lab.results`) / `PHARMACY` (`pharmacy.pos`) / `OTHER` (manual line). A **disabled source is rejected (400)** έΑΦ a pharmacy-only tenant can't bill a lab order (Acceptance ┬π1). Lines are **auto-pulled read-only** from the source document (a pharmacy sale's items, a lab order's tests joined to catalog prices, a package's price) so 17/19/20 are never modified; `CONSULT` keys the fee as `amount` because the consult domain stores none. `computeInvoiceTotals` clamps the discount to `[0, subtotal]` and applies tax on the discounted base.
- **Payments** (cash/card/online/**credit=udhaar**): partial allowed έΗΤ `PARTIAL` + pending balance, `paid έΚξ total` έΗΤ `PAID`. A **CREDIT** payment posts a **`PatientCredit` entry (14)** via the existing `PatientService.addCredit` **and** an **AR accounting event**; a credit payment with no patient έΗΤ 400.
- **Refunds**: a **reason-code is required** (audited). Over a threshold the refund lands **`REQUESTED`** and only a **`billing.refund.approve`** holder can approve/reject before the money moves; at/under it clears at once. The **refundable amount subtracts already-claimed refunds** (APPROVED reduced `paid`; REQUESTED are pending claims) so an invoice can **never be over-refunded**, and `settleRefund` re-validates against the CURRENT `paid`. A **partial** refund reopens the balance (`PARTIAL`/`PAID`) so remaining money stays collectable; only a **full** refund έΗΤ `REFUNDED`.
- **Cashier shift**: open (float) έΗΤ collect έΗΤ **close with a denomination counter έΗΤ variance = counted έΙΤ (float + cash in έΙΤ cash out)** έΑΦ the owner's **theft tripwire** (kept exact in pure math). The refund cash-out is charged to the **requesting** cashier's shift (captured at request time), not the approver's, so the variance lands on the right person.
- **End-of-day per-person report**: collections by method, refunds and variance per cashier (`collected` excludes udhaar έΑΦ a receivable, not cash in hand).
- **Receipts**: thermal 80mm + A4 self-printing windows with the 07 letterhead.
- **Accounting events έΗΤ 23**: each settle/refund writes ONE **idempotent balanced double-entry** `AccountingEvent` (╬μdebit = ╬μcredit via `assertBalanced`) into an outbox `@@unique(tenant, source, sourceRefId)`; a re-emit is a no-op (`createMany skipDuplicates`). `pay` / `refund` / shift-`close` all ride **`SyncService.runIdempotent`** (Idempotency-Key) so an offline replay never double-charges / double-refunds / double-posts / double-credits.

**Data model.** NEW migration `20260704170000_billing_cashier` έΑΦ 7 tables: `invoices` (money breakdown + status + shift), `invoice_items` (price snapshot), `payments` (`client_action_id @unique`), `refunds` (+`shift_id` for exact drawer attribution), `cashier_shifts`, `shift_counts`, `accounting_events` (`@@unique(tenant_id, source, source_ref_id)` outbox). Enums `InvoiceSource` / `InvoiceStatus` / `PayMethod` / `RefundStatus` / `ShiftStatus` (re-exported from `@mp/db`). Every table `apply_tenant_rls` (02); T1/T2 + WITH-CHECK + fail-closed proven in `packages/db/src/billing-isolation.spec.ts` (5 tests).

**Flags/permissions.** `billing.manage` / `billing.refund.approve` perms + the billable flags already in the catalogs έΑΦ **no catalog change** (consistent with 18έΑΥ20).

**Shared math.** Pure `@mp/shared/billing` (browser-safe): enum mirrors + guards, `computeInvoiceTotals` (discount clamp + tax), `invoiceLineTotal`/`invoiceSubtotal`, `invoiceStatusFor`/`balanceDue`, `refundNeedsApproval` (+`DEFAULT_REFUND_APPROVAL_THRESHOLD`), `denominationTotal`/`shiftExpectedCash`/`shiftVariance`/`canCloseShift` (the exact tripwire), and the accounting contract `buildPaymentLines`/`buildRefundLines`/`accountingSourceFor`/`cashAccountFor`/`assertBalanced` with stable `ACCOUNT_CODES` (CASH/BANK/INCOME/AR).

**API.** `BillingModule` (imports Flags/Permissions/Patients/Brand/Sync). **Present when ANY billable flag is on** έΑΦ a single `@RequireFeature` can't express that OR, so each handler runs `assertModulePresent` (**404 FIRST**) then the permission (403) programmatically, mirroring 18. 3 controllers: `InvoicesController` (`/invoices` create/list/detail/receipt/pay[Idempotency-Key]/refund[Idempotency-Key]/refund/:refundId/decision[`billing.refund.approve`]), `ShiftsController` (`/shifts` open/close[Idempotency-Key]/current/:id/report), `BillingReportsController` (`/billing/reports/end-of-day`, `/billing/reports/refunds/pending`). Repo reads source docs read-only via `runWithTenant`.

**Web.** EN+UR `/billing` (`page.tsx` + `BillingClient.tsx`, `robots:noindex`): **Bill** (source-adaptive invoice form w/ live `computeInvoiceTotals` preview, recent list, pay, thermal+A4 receipt, refund), **Shift** (open float, **denomination counter** summing via `denominationTotal`, close έΗΤ variance), **Report** (end-of-day per-person table + pending refund approve/reject). Optional controls gated via `/flags/me`; Idempotency-Key on pay/refund/close.

**Review + fixes.** A high-effort multi-agent review of the diff surfaced money-critical refund-path bugs, all fixed before checkpoint: (1) over-refund possible (refundable now subtracts pending/approved refunds + re-validates at settle + the refund request is now idempotent via `runIdempotent`); (2) a partial refund wrongly forced `REFUNDED` and stranded the balance (now `REFUNDED` only when fully refunded, else `invoiceStatusFor`); (3) refund cash-out mis-attributed to the approver's shift (now the requesting cashier's, captured at request time); (4) end-of-day `collected` wrongly counted udhaar (now excluded). Left by design (per spec): refunds are cash-out (the spec's variance formula says "cash refunds"), and the approval threshold uses the shared default (no per-tenant threshold store exists yet έΑΦ a 41/config concern). Known limitation for 23: refunding a udhaar-paid invoice does not unwind the PatientCredit entry (refunds are method-agnostic in the spec model; AR reconciliation lands with 23).

**Gate results (all green).** typecheck 26/26 ┬╖ lint 15/15 (0 warn) ┬╖ build 15/15 (`/billing` route present) ┬╖ jest **api 387/387 [+43]** (billing helpers 17 + e2e 26) ┬╖ **db 103/103 [+5 billing-isolation]** ┬╖ i18n 19/19 parity. Vertical smoke: a lab-only tenant bills a lab order and rejects a pharmacy source (400); a tenant with no billable module έΗΤ 404 on invoices/shifts/reports. Perf έηΨ (internal cashier tool, noindex).

**Files.** shared: `packages/shared/src/billing.ts` (+ index export). db: `schema.prisma` (7 models + 5 enums), migration `20260704170000_billing_cashier/migration.sql`, `src/index.ts` (enum re-export), `src/billing-isolation.spec.ts`. api: `apps/api/src/billing/{billing.constants,billing.dto,billing.repositories,billing.service,billing.controller,billing.module,index,__fakes__,billing.e2e.spec,billing-helpers.spec}.ts`, `app.module.ts` (wire). web: `apps/web/app/billing/{page,BillingClient}.tsx`. i18n: `packages/i18n/src/messages/{en,ur}.json` (billing/bill/shift/report keys, parity kept).

**Do-NOT-break honoured.** Sale (20), LabOrder (19), Encounter (17), PatientCredit (14), audit έΑΦ all read-only from billing, untouched. The accounting-event contract is idempotent + stable by `(source, sourceRefId)`; shift variance math is exact.

## Build-step 20 έΑΦ Phase 1: Pharmacy POS (SalesmanέΗΤCashier + AI Reader)

- **Work-type:** FEATURE. **Phase 1 / item 7.** Branch `feat/20-pharmacy-pos` (stacks on `feat/19-laboratory`). Depends on 18 (Medicine model + prescription routing), 14 (patient / customer + timeline), 06 (audit), 10 (offline idempotency + compensating writes), 07 (slip letterhead), 13 (UI). AI reader έΗΤ 35/36 (degrades to a manual cart); batch/FEFO έΗΤ 28 (stock is minimal here; sales use the 10 compensating-write hook so 28 plugs in).
- **Problem:** the pharmacy counter must let inexperienced staff sell reliably from a 20έΑΥ50k medicine master: multiple salesmen build carts and **push to one cashier** who finalizes + prints an **80mm thermal slip**; stock loss must be impossible to do silently; an **AI prescription reader** turns a photo/prescription into a ready cart so untrained staff perform like experts έΑΦ but **never auto-sells** (AI fills, human confirms). Plus discounts, returns, stock-out alternatives, and per-medicine profit.
- **Design decision έΑΦ the money + lifecycle math is ONE pure module server+client share (`@mp/shared/pharmacy`):** `computeSaleTotals(lines, discount)` clamps the discount to `[0, subtotal]` (total never negative/over-discounted) and is what the cashier UI previews AND the server stores; `lineProfit`/`saleProfit`/`profitMargin` compute saleέΙΤcost; `canPush`(OPEN)/`canFinalize`(PUSHED)/`isStockOut`(qtyέΚν0) are the guards; `summarizeSale` is the timeline line. Mirrors of the DB enums (`MovementTypeLit`/`CartStatusLit`/`SaleStatusLit`) keep it browser-safe. So a previewed total can never disagree with the stored one.
- **Design decision έΑΦ finalize is the critical offline path, wrapped in the 10 idempotency seam:** `finalize` runs entirely inside `SyncService.runIdempotent(clientActionId)` (from the `Idempotency-Key` header) έΑΦ the cart fetch + `canFinalize` guard + Sale/SaleItems create + the per-line **compensating** stock decrement + the SALE `StockMovement` + the cartέΗΤFINALIZED flip are ALL inside the seam. A replayed finalize returns the SAME sale with `replayed:true` and **no second decrement / double-sell**; guards live inside so a replay of an already-FINALIZED cart is NOT a stale 400. `Sale.clientActionId` is `@unique` as a belt-and-braces guard.
- **Design decision έΑΦ stock never moves silently (06) + moves additively (10):** every decrement/return writes a signed `StockMovement` (`actorId`, `reason`, `refType/refId` έΗΤ the sale) AND applies a **compensating additive write** to `Stock.qty` (`qty += delta`, upsert) έΑΦ so two concurrent offline decrements both land and 28's FEFO/batches plug in without a rewrite. Returns require a reason (audited) έΗΤ a positive RETURN movement + `Sale.status=RETURNED`; the money-side refund approval integrates with billing (21) έΑΦ recorded now, approved there (degrades).
- **Design decision έΑΦ AI reader stays assist-only + flag-gated, degrades cleanly:** `POST /pharmacy/carts/from-prescription` is behind `pharmacy.aiReader` (dependsOn `pharmacy.pos`+`ai.suite`). With a `prescriptionId` it deterministically seeds an **OPEN DRAFT** cart from the prescription's INTERNAL-dispense medicines (18) έΑΦ `providerAvailable:false` until 35/36 wire the OCR; an image-only request degrades to an empty cart + a note. It **NEVER finalizes** έΑΦ the salesman must review + push, the cashier finalizes. With the flag OFF the route 404s and the manual cart works fully.
- **Design decision έΑΦ `/pharmacy/*` prefix avoids the existing `/medicines` surface:** 18 already owns `@Controller('medicines')` (gated `rx.write`). Rather than collide, the pharmacy medicine master lives under `/pharmacy/medicines` (fuzzy name/generic **+ exact barcode** search, extended fields, `:id/label`), keeping the module self-contained. Both modules read/write the SAME tenant-scoped `medicines` table via their own thin repos.
- **Design decision έΑΦ a SALE is a PURCHASE timeline event (light view too):** added `registerPurchase`/`collectPurchase` to the patient `TimelineRegistry` (additive) and wired `PatientService.timeline` to collect purchase contributors in BOTH the light customer view AND the full medical record (a person's purchase history is the whole point of the light view). The pharmacy registers a `SALE` contributor on boot; the existing belt-and-braces filter still keeps non-purchase kinds out of the light view.
- **Data model / migration:** NEW migration `έΑο160000_pharmacy_pos`. Extends `Medicine` additively (+`barcode`, `sale_price`, `cost_price` + a `(tenant, barcode)` index) έΑΦ 18's minimal rows keep working (its `MEDICINE_SELECT` is field-scoped). SIX new tables: `barcode_labels`, `stock` (`@@unique(tenant, branch, medicine)`), `stock_movements` (the 06 ┬π3.3 shape), `cart_handoffs` (items JSON), `sales` (`client_action_id @unique`), `sale_items`; THREE new enums `MovementType`/`CartStatus`/`SaleStatus` (re-exported from `@mp/db`). Every new table `apply_tenant_rls` (T1/T2 + WITH CHECK + fail-closed proven in `pharmacy-isolation.spec.ts`). Stock/movements/sales also carry `branch_id`.
- **Feature flags:** owns `pharmacy.pos` (module), `pharmacy.aiReader` (dependsOn `pharmacy.pos`+`ai.suite`), `pharmacy.barcodeLabels` (dependsOn `pharmacy.pos`) έΑΦ ALL already in the `@mp/shared` catalog + the `pharmacy`/`clinic_pharmacy` presets, so **no catalog change**. Permissions `pharmacy.sell`/`pharmacy.cashier`/`pharmacy.stock.adjust` already present (no change).
- **API (`PharmacyModule`, 4 controllers, `@RequireFeature('pharmacy.pos')` class-wide; nav absent for Lab/Clinic-only):** `PharmacyMedicinesController` (`pharmacy.sell`) έΑΦ `GET /pharmacy/medicines?q=` (name/generic/**barcode** + stock), `POST`/`PUT` (extended fields), `GET :id/alternatives` (same-generic in-stock), `POST :id/label` (method-flag `pharmacy.barcodeLabels`). `PharmacyCartsController` (`pharmacy.sell`) έΑΦ `POST /pharmacy/carts`, `GET`/`GET :id`, `POST :id/items` (returns cart + `stockWarning` + alternatives on stock-out), `POST :id/items/remove`, `POST :id/{push,hold,resume}`, `POST from-prescription` (method-flag `pharmacy.aiReader`; resolves the caller's `rx.viewInternal` for privacy). `PharmacyCashierController` (`pharmacy.cashier`) έΑΦ `GET /pharmacy/cashier/queue`, `POST carts/:id/finalize` (`Idempotency-Key`, compensating decrement, slip), `POST sales/:id/return` (reason-required, audited). `PharmacySalesController` (`pharmacy.cashier`) έΑΦ `GET /pharmacy/sales`, `GET :id` (profit/margin), `GET :id/slip`. All mutations `@Audited`.
- **UI (`/pharmacy`, EN+UR, `robots:noindex`):** three tabs έΑΦ **Sell** (salesman: search/scan έΗΤ add έΗΤ cart with live subtotal έΗΤ Push/Hold; "Scan prescription (AI)" seed shown only when `pharmacy.aiReader`; stock-out shows alternatives inline), **Cashier** (pushed queue έΗΤ finalize with a live-clamped discount preview via the shared `computeSaleTotals` έΗΤ **80mm thermal slip** print window; returns), **Catalog** (Pro: medicine master add + list, self-printed **barcode label** print window shown only when `pharmacy.barcodeLabels`, recent sales with **profit/margin**). Client fetches `/flags/me` to gate the optional controls (clean off-state; the server still enforces).
- **Do-NOT-break honoured:** Medicine extended (not replaced); prescription/patient/audit untouched except the additive purchase-timeline hook; finalize rides the 10 idempotency + compensating-write seams so 28 FEFO plugs in; the `StockMovement` shape kept stable for 21/23/24/28; AI stays assist-only + flag-gated.
- **Verification gates:** typecheck **26/26**; lint **15/15** (0 warnings); turbo build **15/15** (`/pharmacy` route emitted, 4.19 kB); jest **api 344/344 (37 suites; +23 έΑΦ 22 e2e wiring + 1 helpers)**, **db 98/98 (18 suites; +4 pharmacy-isolation)**, i18n **19/19** parity (EN+UR +~60 `pharm*` keys). Vertical smoke: present for `pharmacy`/`clinic_pharmacy`/`full`, absent (404) for `lab`; catalog present but `pharmacy.aiReader`/`pharmacy.barcodeLabels` 404 when off. Offline: finalize idempotent (replay = same sale, single decrement) + no-key έΗΤ 400 proven. Accountability: every sale/return writes an audited `StockMovement`. Perf έηΨ (internal POS tool, `robots:noindex`). Isolation: tenant + branch scoped; T1/T2 + WITH CHECK + fail-closed proven.

## Build-step 19 έΑΦ Phase 1: Laboratory (Orders + Smart Reports)

- **Work-type:** FEATURE. **Phase 1 / item 6.** Branch `feat/19-laboratory` (stacks on `feat/18-eprescription`). Depends on 14 (patient record + age/gender for reference ranges + timeline), 17/18 (referral/dual-prescription έΗΤ a lab order), 06 (audit), 09 (WhatsApp), 07 (report letterhead), 12 (catalog import). Manual result entry (no analyzer integration); sample is minimal here (barcode) έΑΦ 27 extends chain-of-custody, 25/26 home-collection reuse it.
- **Problem:** the lab needs a full LIS έΑΦ a catalog of tests with **prep instructions** + **packages**, **smart result templates** (params + units + **age/gender reference ranges** pre-built so the technician types only patient values and the system auto-flags high/low/critical), a lifecycle orderέΗΤsample(barcode)έΗΤresultέΗΤ**pathologist approval (sign)**έΗΤbranded report, plus **critical-value alerts**, **TAT**, **re-test**, **amend-with-reason**, patient/doctor portals and WhatsApp delivery.
- **Design decision έΑΦ the smart template evaluator is ONE pure function server+client share:** `evaluateResults(params, enteredValues, {ageYears, sex})` (in `@mp/shared/lab`) selects the applicable reference range by the patient's age + gender (a sex-specific band beats an `ANY` band), then flags each value NORMAL/HIGH/LOW/**CRITICAL** (critical wins over high/low). The technician enters values only; the API stores the SAME evaluation the web previews instantly as they type, so a stored flag can never disagree with its inputs. TAT (`computeTatHours`) and patient age (`ageYears`) are pure too.
- **Design decision έΑΦ the surface is split across the two capabilities, gated per-route:** `lab.catalog` (catalog/packages/orders/samples) and `lab.results` (result templates/entry/approval/amend/report; `dependsOn lab.catalog`). Class-level `@RequireFeature`/`@RequirePermission` set the default; result-entry & approval **override at the method** (`getAllAndOverride` έΗΤ handler wins) to the tighter `lab.results` + `lab.result.enter`/`lab.result.approve`. So a catalog-only tenant can order + collect but resulting/approval 404, and a Pharmacy/Clinic-only vertical never sees the module (vertical smoke).
- **Design decision έΑΦ approval is medico-legal & controlled:** a report is **deliverable only once signed** (`isDeliverable` έΗΤ APPROVED/DELIVERED); approval refuses unless every ordered test is resulted (pre-sign is a non-deliverable DRAFT). Amend-after-sign **requires a reason**, appends a versioned entry to the `ReportApproval.amendments` JSON, and is audited έΑΦ never a silent edit.

### Schema / migration / RLS
- **NEW migration `20260704150000_laboratory`** έΑΦ 8 tables, each tenant-scoped via canonical `apply_tenant_rls()`: `lab_tests` (`@@unique([tenant,code])`, `prep_instructions`, `template_id`, DECIMAL price), `lab_packages` (`test_ids` JSONB), `result_templates` (`params` JSONB = `[{name,unit,type,ranges:[{sex,ageMin,ageMax,low,high,criticalLow,criticalHigh}]}]`), `lab_orders` (`LabStatus` lifecycle + `reported_at` for TAT + `retest_of_id`), `lab_order_tests` (records its `package_id`), `samples` (globally-unique scannable `barcode` + collect/receive timestamps + `SampleStatus`), `results` (`values` JSONB w/ the auto-flags, one per order-test, upserted), `report_approvals` (sign + `amendments` JSONB). NEW enums `LabStatus` (ORDEREDέΗΤCOLLECTEDέΗΤRECEIVEDέΗΤRESULTEDέΗΤAPPROVEDέΗΤDELIVERED) + `SampleStatus` (PENDING/COLLECTED/RECEIVED/REJECTED), re-exported from `@mp/db`. **Permissions** `lab.order`/`lab.result.enter`/`lab.result.approve` and **flags** `lab.catalog`/`lab.results` already existed in the catalogs (LAB_TECH/PATHOLOGIST roles carry them) έΑΦ **no catalog change**. T1/T2 isolation + WITH CHECK + fail-closed proven in `packages/db/src/lab-isolation.spec.ts` (pglite, real 01έΗΤ19 migrations).

### What changed
- **Pure `@mp/shared/lab`** έΑΦ `LabStatusLit`/`SampleStatusLit` (+ arrays + guards), `isDeliverable`, `RefRange`/`ResultParam`/`RangeSex`/`ResultFlagLit`/`PatientRangeCtx`/`EvaluatedValue`, `pickRange` (age+gender selection, sex-specific preferred), `flagValue`, `evaluateResults` (έΗΤ `{values, hasCritical, hasAbnormal}`), `computeTatHours`, `ageYears`, `summarizeLabOrder`. Reused the existing additive `TEST` `TimelineKind`.
- **API `LabModule`** (registered last in `app.module`; no global guard). Four controllers under `/lab` + `/patients`: **LabCatalogController** (`lab.catalog`/`lab.order`) έΑΦ `GET/POST /lab/tests`, `PUT /lab/tests/:id`, `GET/POST /lab/packages`; **LabTemplatesController** (`lab.results`/`lab.result.enter`) έΑΦ `GET/POST /lab/result-templates`; **LabOrdersController** έΑΦ `POST /lab/orders` (validates patient 14, expands packages, best-effort prep WhatsApp), `GET /lab/orders?status=&patientId=`, `GET /lab/orders/:id`, `POST /lab/orders/:id/collect` (generates a `LAB-έΑο` barcode έΗΤ COLLECTED), `POST /lab/samples/receive` (scan έΗΤ RECEIVED), `POST /lab/orders/:id/retest` (links `retestOfId`), method-overridden `POST /lab/orders/:id/results` (evaluate vs template + patient age/gender έΗΤ auto-flag, έΗΤ RESULTED when all done, `criticalAlert`), `POST /lab/orders/:id/approve` (sign έΗΤ APPROVED + `reportedAt` + WhatsApp `lab.report.ready`, degrades), `POST /lab/orders/:id/amend` (reason required, versioned, audited), `GET /lab/orders/:id/report` (branded 07 letterhead payload, `draft` when unsigned); **PatientLabController** έΑΦ `GET /patients/:id/lab-orders` (portal list). All mutations `@Audited`. Prisma DecimalέΗΦnumber normalised at the repo seam.
- **Timeline + import wiring** έΑΦ `LabModule.onModuleInit` registers a MEDICAL `TimelineRegistry` contributor έΗΤ a `TEST` event per order (`summarizeLabOrder`, medical view only), and registers the **lab-test catalog importer** (`labTestImporter`, idempotent by `code`) with the 12 `ImportRegistry` (`GET /import/lab_test/template` etc.).
- **Web EN+UR `/lab`** έΑΦ server page frames a client island (`robots:noindex`): access probe, three tabs έΑΦ **Worklist** (orders list έΗΤ open an order έΗΤ collect/receive a barcoded sample έΗΤ per-test result entry with the params/units/ranges pre-filled and **live flags** via the shared `evaluateResults` + fetched patient age/gender έΗΤ pathologist Approve & sign έΗΤ Amend-with-reason έΗΤ **Print branded report** window (07 letterhead, per-test values + reference + flags + amendments + TAT + sign) έΗΤ Re-test), **New order** (patient/doctor ids + catalog search + selected tests έΗΤ create), **Catalog** (add a test + list). 69 new i18n keys ENέΗΦUR (parity).

### Verification gates
- **typecheck** 26/26 ┬╖ **lint** 15/15 ┬╖ **turbo build** 15/15 (web `/lab` route emitted).
- **jest api 321/321** (35 suites; **+25**: `lab-helpers.spec.ts` 11 έΑΦ vocab/deliverable, ageYears, pickRange age+gender, flagValue NORMAL/HIGH/LOW/CRITICAL, evaluateResults, TAT, summary; `lab.e2e.spec.ts` 14 έΑΦ 401, clinic-only 404 vertical smoke, catalog-only 404 on resulting, `lab.order` 403 + `lab.result.enter` 403, catalog+dup-code 409+packages, prep-at-booking, package expansion, smart-template auto-flag by age+gender + critical alert, sample collectέΗΤreceive+second-collect 409+re-test, pre-sign draft + approve gating + `lab.result.approve` 403 + TAT + report + amend-needs-reason + audit, catalog import template, portal list + timeline TEST event). **jest db 94/94** (17 suites; **+4** lab-isolation). **i18n 19/19** parity. All other package suites unaffected.
- **Isolation:** all 8 tables tenant-scoped; T1/T2 + WITH CHECK + fail-closed proven. **Vertical smoke:** module 404s for Pharmacy/Clinic-only (no `lab.catalog`); resulting 404s when `lab.results` off. **Performance έηΨ** (internal LIS tool, `robots:noindex`, no public surface).
- **Do-NOT-break honoured:** patient (14, age/gender ranges), referral (17/18), audit, notifications, 07 letterhead untouched except additively. `Sample` shape left minimal for 27 to extend + 25/26 to reuse; approval/amend kept controlled (sign-gated, reason-required, audited).

## Build-step 16 έΑΦ Phase 1: Vitals Station (Nurse)

- **Work-type:** FEATURE. **Phase 1 / item 3.** Branch `feat/16-vitals-station` (stacks on `feat/15-appointment-token`). Depends on 14 (patient record + timeline), 15 (appointment/token έΑΦ the sheet header), 10 (offline core / idempotency seam), 13 (UI/i18n). **Critical offline path.**
- **Problem:** before the doctor, a nurse records vitals on a printed A4. Two habits must BOTH be supported and neither can be forced to change: (a) type into the app then print a filled sheet, (b) print a blank header sheet and write by pen (then type it, or photoέΗΤAI read it later). AI photo-read is deferred to build-step 35; until then the photo path yields an empty draft the nurse types over.
- **Design decision έΑΦ one table, every value optional, BMI authoritative on the server:** a nurse records what the visit needs (not a fixed panel), so every measurement column is nullable. The client may send weight/height but the server ALWAYS recomputes `bmi` from them (`computeBmi`, the ONE formula shared with the web's live indicator) so a stored BMI can never disagree with its inputs. Saving rides the offline idempotency seam exactly like a token (required `Idempotency-Key` έΗΤ `SyncService.runIdempotent`, plus a P2002 backstop on the unique `client_action_id`) so a reading queued offline and replayed on reconnect returns the SAME row, never a duplicate.
- **Design decision έΑΦ a decoupled `TimelineRegistry` instead of patientsέΗΤvitals coupling:** the patient timeline (14) must show a reading, but the patients module must not import a downstream clinical module. NEW `TimelineRegistry` (mirrors the `ImportRegistry` pattern) is provided + exported by PatientsModule; VitalsModule registers a MEDICAL contributor on boot. Contributors flow IN (no cycle) and are collected ONLY when `customers.medicalRecord` is on, so the light customer view stays purchase-only automatically. This is the seam 17/19/20 reuse.

### Schema / migration / RLS
- **NEW migration `20260704120000_vitals_station`** έΑΦ 1 table `vitals`, tenant-scoped via canonical `apply_tenant_rls()` + `branch_id`: `patient_id` (+ optional `appointment_id`/`encounter_id` έΑΦ encounter reserved for 17), the reading columns (`bp_sys`/`bp_dia`/`pulse`/`spo2` INT; `temp_c`/`weight_kg`/`height_cm`/`bmi`/`blood_sugar` DECIMAL; `sugar_type` TEXT), `captured_by`/`captured_at`, `source` (`VitalsSource` enum TYPED/HANDWRITTEN_PHOTO/IMPORTED, default TYPED), and UNIQUE `client_action_id` for offline idempotency. Indexes `(tenant, patient)` + `(tenant, appointment)`. NEW enum `VitalsSource` re-exported from `@mp/db`. T1/T2 isolation + WITH CHECK + fail-closed proven in `packages/db/src/vitals-isolation.spec.ts` (pglite, real 01έΗΤ16 migrations).

### What changed
- **Pure `@mp/shared/vitals`** έΑΦ `computeBmi(weightKg, heightCm)` (έΗΤ 1 dp, null unless both positive), `summarizeVitals` (compact timeline/print line, derives BMI, never trusts input), `hasAnyVital`, `SUGAR_TYPES`/`isSugarType` (FASTING/RANDOM/PP/HBA1C), `VitalsValues`/`SugarTypeLit`/`VitalsSourceLit`. Added `VITALS` to the additive `TimelineKind` union (medical-only έΑΦ not in `PURCHASE_TIMELINE_KINDS`).
- **API `VitalsModule`** (registered after Sync/Patients/Appointments in `app.module`; no global guard). Whole controller `@RequireFeature('clinic.consultation')` (already in catalog + clinic presets έΑΦ **404s when off** = vertical smoke) + `@RequirePermission('vitals.enter')` (already in catalog; NURSE/DOCTOR carry it, RECEPTION/ADMIN do not). Endpoints: `POST /vitals` (`@Audited('vitals.record')`, required `Idempotency-Key` έΗΤ offline-idempotent, BMI recomputed); `GET /vitals?patientId=&appointmentId=` (newest first); `GET /vitals/sheet?appointmentId=&patientId=&blank=` (composes the patient/token header from PatientService + AppointmentsService έΑΦ added public `detailAppointment` + `tokenNumberForAppointment` accessors to AppointmentsService έΑΦ and pre-prints the latest reading unless `blank`); `POST /vitals/from-photo` (`@Audited`) έΗΤ a DRAFT (`aiAvailable:false`, empty until 35) the nurse confirms έΑΦ **no silent commit**. Repo converts Prisma DecimalέΗΦnumber at the seam.
- **Patient timeline wiring** έΑΦ `TimelineRegistry` provided+exported by PatientsModule; `PatientService.timeline` appends `registry.collectMedical(...)` inside the medical branch (failures isolated per contributor). VitalsModule.`onModuleInit` registers `timelineEvents` έΗΤ a `VITALS` event (`"Vitals recorded έΑΦ BP έΑο"`).
- **Web EN+UR `/vitals`** έΑΦ server page frames a client island: access probe (`GET /vitals?patientId=__probe__`), patient/appointment id inputs (prefill from `?patientId=`/`?appointmentId=`), a big number-input grid with a **live BMI** as the nurse types, Save (online έΗΤ `idempotency-key`; offline έΗΤ outbox `enqueue`, never double-saves), **Print filled / Print blank** (fetches the sheet JSON, opens a self-contained A4 print window with the patient/token header + filled values or empty write-by-pen boxes, RTL-aware), and a recent-readings history. New `.mp-vitals-*` styles; 42 new i18n keys ENέΗΦUR (parity).

### Verification gates
- **typecheck** 26/26 ┬╖ **lint** 15/15 ┬╖ **turbo build** 15/15 (web `/vitals` route emitted).
- **jest api 247/247** (29 suites; **+20**: `vitals-helpers.spec.ts` 8 + `vitals.e2e.spec.ts` 12 έΑΦ flag 404 vertical smoke, `vitals.enter` 403, BMI auto-compute + offline-idempotent replay, missing-key 400, out-of-range 400, filled + blank sheet with header/token, photoέΗΤdraft no-commit, timeline VITALS event, audit). **jest db 82/82** (14 suites; **+3** vitals-isolation). **i18n 19/19** parity. shared/ui/import/offline/consent/notifications/patients/appointments suites unaffected.
- **Isolation:** tenant-scoped; T1/T2 + WITH CHECK + fail-closed proven. **Offline:** replay returns the same row (idempotency seam + P2002 backstop). **Vertical smoke:** whole surface 404s when `clinic.consultation` off.
- **Do-NOT-break honoured:** patient/appointment/timeline/offline-idempotency/flag-gate untouched except additively (new `TimelineRegistry`, new public appointment accessors, new `VITALS` timeline kind). Vitals row shape is additive έΑΦ stable for the consultation (17) to read.

## Build-step 15 έΑΦ Phase 1: Appointment & Token (paper-first)

- **Work-type:** FEATURE. **Phase 1 / item 2.** Branch `feat/15-appointment-token` (stacks on `feat/14-patient-management`). Depends on 14 (patient), 10 (offline core / idempotency seam), 09 (notifications), 13 (UI/i18n).
- **Problem:** the clinic runs on paper; aged patients don't self-book; the compounder is often too busy to register fully; staff reconcile a paper register at day's end. A system fighting this is abandoned. Design **for** paper: one-tap offline tokens, full registration optional, end-of-day photoέΗΤ(AI later) register import with a human verify.
- **Design decision έΑΦ a Token creates a WALK_IN Appointment + a numbered Token atomically:** the queue is built from active appointments with their token numbers attached; booked appointments (source BOOKED) join the same queue; register-import commits create appointments+tokens with source REGISTER_IMPORT. Token numbering is **sequential per doctor/branch/day** via a plaintext `day_key` + a tenant-scoped unique index `(tenant, doctor, branch, day_key, number)` so numbering never collides (and co-exists across tenants έΑΦ proven in the isolation test).

### Schema / migration / RLS
- **NEW migration `20260704110000_appointment_token`** έΑΦ 6 tables, all tenant-scoped via canonical `apply_tenant_rls()` + `branch_id` where location-scoped: `doctors` (slotMinutes/comfortLevel/optional user link), `doctor_availability` (weekly dayOfWeek + minutes-of-day windows), `doctor_leave` (dated ranges), `appointments` (`ApptStatus` lifecycle + `ApptSource`), `tokens` (`number` + `day_key` + UNIQUE `client_action_id` for offline idempotency; unique `(tenant, doctor, branch, day_key, number)`), `register_imports` (`imageKeys` JSON + `RegImportStatus` UPLOADEDέΗΤPARSEDέΗΤVERIFIEDέΗΤIMPORTED + `draft` JSON). NEW enums `ApptStatus`/`ApptSource`/`RegImportStatus` re-exported from `@mp/db`. T1/T2 isolation + WITH CHECK + fail-closed + no-cross-tenant-numbering proven in `packages/db/src/appointment-isolation.spec.ts` (pglite, real 01έΗΤ15 migrations).
- **No new feature flag** έΑΦ `clinic.appointments` already in the catalog (`@mp/shared/flags`) and in the `clinic`/`clinic_pharmacy`/`full` presets. **No new permission** έΑΦ `appointments.manage` already in the catalog (granted to ADMIN/MANAGER/DOCTOR/RECEPTION/CALL_CENTER). The WHOLE controller is `@RequireFeature('clinic.appointments')` + `@RequirePermission('appointments.manage')` at the class level (flag FIRST έΗΤ 404 when off, then permission έΗΤ 403).

### What changed
- **Pure `@mp/shared/appointments`** (browser-safe, no node imports): `dayKeyOf` (UTC day bucket the server + offline client agree on), `nextTokenNumber` (max+1, gap-free), `buildDaySlots` (availability έΙΤ leave έΙΤ booked, de-duped, minuteέΘΕ`HH:MM` `minutesToLabel`/`labelToMinutes`), the appointment lifecycle state machine (`APPT_TRANSITIONS`/`canTransitionAppt`/`isTerminalAppt`), and the register-import draft contract (`RegisterDraftRow`/`isCommittableDraftRow`/`committableRows`).
- **API `AppointmentsModule`** (imports `SyncModule`): `POST /appointments/tokens` έΑΦ one-tap walk-in, **CRITICAL OFFLINE PATH** riding `SyncService.runIdempotent(clientActionId)` (required `Idempotency-Key` header) so a replayed token returns the SAME number without double-issuing (a P2002 backstop on the unique index catches the save-race). Doctor CRUD; availability/leave CRUD; `GET /appointments/doctors/:id/slots?date=` (availability έΙΤ leave έΙΤ booked); `POST /appointments` (book, source BOOKED) + `PATCH /appointments/:id` (reschedule/cancel/status/no-show, state-machine-validated έΗΤ 400 on illegal transition); `GET /appointments/queue` + `GET /appointments/display` (per-doctor now-serving + up-next). Register import: `POST /register-imports` (photosέΗΤUPLOADED) έΗΤ `POST /:id/parse` (empty draft until AI 35; PARSED) έΗΤ `PATCH /:id/draft` (human-verified rows; VERIFIED) έΗΤ `POST /:id/import` (commit; **must be VERIFIED first**, incomplete rows skipped not guessed έΗΤ 400 before verify; never auto-commits). All mutations `@Audited`. Injectable `APPT_CLOCK` for deterministic `day_key`/slots in tests.
- **Web EN+UR `/appointments`** έΑΦ flag/permission-aware island (404/403 έΗΤ clean no-access): offline badge (from `useSyncStatus`), compounder giant one-tap **New Token** (online έΗΤ token #; network-down έΗΤ outbox `enqueue` so it syncs, never double-issues), live **Queue** with Start/Done/No-show taps, **Doctors** tab (add doctor + per-doctor availability/leave via time inputs), full-screen-ish **Display** board, and the human-gated **Register import** wizard (upload keys έΗΤ parse έΗΤ verify rows έΗΤ import). New `mp-appt-*` CSS.
- **i18n:** ~60 new `appt*` keys in EN+UR (`@mp/i18n` catalogs), parity gate green.

### Verification gates (all green)
- typecheck **26/26**, lint **15/15**, turbo build **15/15** (`/appointments` route compiled).
- jest: **api 227/227** (27 suites; **+21** έΑΦ 13 appointment e2e over the real guard graph [flag-off 404 vertical smoke, permission 403, idempotent replay, sequential/per-doctor numbering, slots=availέΙΤleaveέΙΤbooked, lifecycle + illegal-transition 400, queue+display, register-import human-gate + skip-incomplete + audited] + 8 pure-helper unit) ┬╖ **db 79/79** (13 suites; **+6** `appointment-isolation`: per-tenant doctors/appointments/tokens, no-cross-tenant numbering collision, WITH CHECK ├Ω2, fail-closed) ┬╖ i18n **19/19** incl. ENέΗΦUR parity ┬╖ ui/import/offline/consent/notifications/patients unaffected.
- **Flag / vertical smoke:** `clinic.appointments` OFF (pharmacy/lab-only) έΗΤ every route 404s, module absent from nav (proven in e2e). **Offline self-check:** token idempotency proven (replayed clientActionId έΗΤ same number, exactly one token for three POSTs).

### Notes / manual-run caveats
- Register-import AI parse returns an EMPTY draft until the AI gateway (35) lands (staff fill rows manually); today `imageKeys` are client-provided photo keys έΑΦ multipart upload + R2 object store = `[DECIDE AT BUILD]`.
- Token creation rides `SyncService.runIdempotent` (durable dedup via `sync_idempotency`) AND stores `client_action_id` on the token (unique) as a domain backstop; the web outbox path mints its own key on true network failure only (fetch never reached the server), so it cannot double with a partially-succeeded online POST.
- `prisma migrate deploy` / full `deploy.sh` need a live Postgres 16 + server; not runnable in this sandbox. Migration validated under pglite (isolation test runs the real 01έΗΤ15 SQL) and `prisma generate` έεΥ.
