## Build-step 14 έΑΦ Phase 1: Patient / Customer Management

- **Work-type:** FEATURE. **Phase 1 / item 1.** Branch `feat/14-patient-management` (stacks on `feat/13-ui-foundation`). Depends on 02 (RLS/runWithTenant), 04 (permissions), 05 (flags), 06 (audit), 08 (i18n), 09 (notification prefs), 12 (import engine).
- **Problem:** every vertical needs a person record, but a pharmacy-only tenant wants a light "customer" (name+phone+udhaar+purchase history) while a clinic/full tenant needs the full medical record. Pakistani clinics identify by phone (families share one number; aged patients may have none); udhaar must never silently vanish; CNIC is sensitive PII.
- **Design decision έΑΦ ONE model, flag-driven VIEW:** identical data model; the `customers.medicalRecord` flag decides which fields/tabs render AND which endpoints are exposed. A pharmacy that later adds a clinic needs NO migration έΑΦ just flip the flag.

### Schema / migration / RLS
- **NEW migration `20260704100000_patient_management`** έΑΦ 7 tables, all tenant-scoped via canonical `apply_tenant_rls()`:
  - `patients` έΑΦ phone-primary (NULLABLE: aged patients / shared family phone έΗΤ `guardian_id` link), CNIC stored **AES-256-GCM-encrypted** in `cnic` with only `cnic_last4` kept plaintext for search, `gender`/`dob`/`address`/`service_area`/`status` (ACTIVE/INACTIVE/DECEASED), `@@unique(tenant,phone)`.
  - `patient_relations` (directed family/guardian links), `patient_tags`, `patient_allergies` (MEDICAL-record field, severity LOW/MED/HIGH), `patient_credits` (udhaar ledger, `Decimal(12,2)`, `settled_at`/`settled_by`), `patient_notes`, `notification_prefs` (per-channel consent, `@@unique(patient)`).
  - NEW enums `Gender`/`PatientStatus`/`Severity`/`RelationType` (re-exported from `@mp/db`).
  - **pg_trgm** extension + GIN trigram indexes (name/phone/cnic_last4) created **DEFENSIVELY** inside a `DO έΑο EXCEPTION WHEN OTHERS` block έΗΤ no-ops under the pglite RLS test (which lacks pg_trgm); search falls back to a plain, correct ILIKE. Proven pglite-safe before commit.
  - Two model additions BEYOND the spec's 6-model list, each acceptance-driven & additive: `cnic_last4` (required to reconcile ┬π3 CNIC-last4 search with ┬π4 encryption) and `patient_notes` (backs ┬π3.2/┬π3.3 Notes tab/endpoint).
- **Isolation:** NEW `packages/db/src/patient-isolation.spec.ts` έΑΦ real 01έΗΤ14 migrations in pglite, proves T1/T2 scoping on `patients` + `patient_credits`, WITH CHECK blocks cross-tenant writes, encrypted CNIC never bleeds, zero rows with no context (6/6).

### Feature-flag / permission impact
- **Owns/respects flag `customers.medicalRecord`** (existing in catalog): OFF έΗΤ light customer (allergy CRUD + medical timeline hidden); ON έΗΤ full record. Allergy routes carry `@RequireFeature('customers.medicalRecord')` έΗΤ **404 when off** (flag FIRST, then permission).
- Permissions (all pre-existing in `@mp/shared`): `patients.view`/`edit`/`merge`/`notes`/`cnic.reveal`. No new keys.
- **NEW config `CNIC_ENCRYPTION_KEY`** (zod `.min(32)`, dev fallback rejected in production via superRefine). `fakeConfig()` extended with it.

### What changed
- **Pure `@mp/shared/patients.ts`** (browser-safe, no node deps): `maskCnic`/`cnicLast4`/`normalizeCnic`/`normalizePhone`, `creditBalance` (╬μ unsettled έΗΤ feeds accounts 23), `TimelineEvent`+`TimelineKind`+`sortTimeline`+`isPurchaseEvent`+`PURCHASE_TIMELINE_KINDS`.
- **API-only `apps/api/src/patients/cnic-cipher.ts`** έΑΦ `CnicCipher` (AES-256-GCM, SHA-256-derived 32-byte key from `CNIC_KEY` DI token, `v1:iv:tag:data` blob, tamper-detecting; `prepare()` έΗΤ {cipher,last4}). Kept out of `@mp/shared` so `node:crypto` never bundles into the browser.
- **`PatientsModule`** (repo seam + `CnicCipher` + `FlagService`): `GET /patients` fuzzy (ILIKE name/phone/cnic-last4, paginated), `POST/PATCH /patients` (phone uniqueness enforced έΗΤ "link as family" 400; guardian existence checked), `POST /patients/:id/cnic/reveal` (`patients.cnic.reveal` + `@Audited`, full value returned but MASKED in the audit summary), family/relations + dependents + guardian, tags CRUD, allergies CRUD (flag-gated + severity-ranked `allergyWarnings` hook for 18/20), credit add/settle (returns balance), notes (`patients.notes`), notification prefs (honoured by 09), `merge` (moves credit/allergies/notes/tags/relations/dependents to target έΗΤ source INACTIVE, `@Audited`), `timeline` (flag-shaped: REGISTERED+CREDIT purchase-only when off; +ALLERGY/NOTE when on).
- **Registers a patient importer** with the 12 `ImportRegistry` on boot (`onModuleInit`): natural key = phone (idempotent έΑΦ re-import updates, never duplicates), CNIC encrypted at `upsertChunk`, export never emits full CNIC (masked last-4 only). Wired into `app.module` after Flags+Import.
- **Web EN+UR `/patients`** (`.mp-*` design-token convention, RTL): quick-add (phone-first), fuzzy search list, flag-aware `ModuleTabs` (Basic ┬╖ Timeline ┬╖ [Allergies] ┬╖ Credit ┬╖ [Notes] ┬╖ Family έΑΦ medical tabs only when `medicalRecordEnabled`), masked CNIC + audited reveal button, udhaar ledger add/settle, allergy severity picker. 61 NEW i18n keys EN+UR (`patients*`), parity green.

### Verification gates
- **typecheck 26/26 ┬╖ lint 15/15 ┬╖ build 15/15** (turbo). `/patients` route 3.13 kB / 118 kB first-load έΑΦ within perf budget (cf. /ui 282 kB).
- **jest:** api **206/206** (25 suites; +31 = 14 patient e2e covering auth/permission/flag-ON+OFF/family/fuzzy/CNIC-encrypt+mask+reveal-audit/udhaar/tags/status/prefs/merge/idempotent-import + 6 CnicCipher unit + 11 patient-helper unit), db **73/73** (12 suites; +6 patient-isolation), i18n **19/19** incl. ENέΗΦUR parity, ui 38/38, import 18/18, notifications 18/18, offline 29/29, consent 18/18.
- **Flag/vertical smoke:** proven in e2e έΑΦ flag OFF (pharmacy) έΗΤ allergy endpoints 404, timeline purchase-only, `medicalRecordEnabled:false`; flag ON (clinic/full) έΗΤ allergies + medical timeline. Same data, no migration.
- **Isolation:** T1/T2 proven (pglite); CNIC stored ciphertext (`v1:` prefix, never plaintext) and never logged (audit summary masks it). **White-label:** untouched (brand tokens drive the UI).
- **Launch note:** JSON-body CNIC + in-process import today; CNIC-key rotation / KMS + multipart upload = `[DECIDE AT BUILD]`.

## Build-step 13 έΑΦ Foundation: UI Design System + Performance Foundation

**Work-type:** FEATURE. **Phase:** Foundation / item 13. **Branch:** `feat/13-ui-foundation` (stacked on `feat/12-import-export`). **Depends on:** 07 (brand), 08 (i18n), 01. **Schema/RLS/auth/permission/flag impact:** NONE έΑΦ no DB, no migration, no RLS, no new permission or flag. Isolation έηΨ. The screenshot bypass is env-gated (staging-only), fail-closed.

**Problem.** Every later screen must be modern, polished, and usable by non-technical/illiterate users AND meet a hard 90+ mobile performance budget έΑΦ with no shared design system, modules would drift into inconsistent, slow, raw HTML. This step lands the shared `@mp/ui` system + the performance/Lighthouse gate + the staging screenshot bypass.

**What changed.**

*Package `@mp/ui` (scaffold έΗΤ full React design system).* Was a pure-helper scaffold (`cn`, `themeCssVars`); now a Tailwind + shadcn/ui-style component library.
- **Toolchain:** React 19 peer dep; deps `@radix-ui/react-{dialog,label,popover,slot,tabs}`, `class-variance-authority`, `clsx`, `tailwind-merge`, `lucide-react`, `recharts`; dev `tailwindcss`, `jest`+`jest-environment-jsdom`+`@testing-library/{react,jest-dom,user-event}`. tsconfig έΗΤ `module esnext` / `moduleResolution bundler` / `lib DOM` / `jsx react-jsx`. jsdom jest config with `jest.setup.ts` (matchMedia + ResizeObserver stubs).
- **Theming:** `cn` upgraded (clsx+twMerge). `tailwind-preset.ts` (`@mp/ui/tailwind-preset`) maps `--brand-*` έΗΤ semantic Tailwind tokens (`primary/accent/destructive` follow the tenant palette; `background/card/muted/border` are light/dark `--mp-*`), plus `min-h-touch` (44px), brand fonts, motion keyframes. `styles.css` layers `@tailwind` + the `--mp-*` light/dark token layer (derived from brand) + reduced-motion guard. `theme.tsx` `ThemeProvider`/`useTheme` έΑΦ light/dark/system, class-based (`.dark` on `<html>`), persisted, follows OS in `system`.
- **Components:** Button (cva variants, large-touch, `asChild`), Input/Textarea, Label, Card(+parts), Badge, Skeleton/SkeletonText (shimmer), Spinner, Field (a11y label+hint+error wiring), EmptyState, Dialog(+`Modal` alias, focus-trap), Toast (`ToastProvider`/`useToast`/`Toaster`, aria-live), SearchSelect + MultiSearchSelect (Radix Popover combobox, filter, large-touch), DateField, Tabs, **ModuleTabs** (ACTIVE-ONLY mount έΑΦ inactive tabs' `render()` NOT called until first opened έΗΤ lazy per-tab fetch; `unmountInactive` opt), **DataList** (client search + pagination + toolbar slot + `onExport(filteredRows)`έΗΤ12, skeleton rows, empty state, a11y caption), animated recharts **Chart** wrappers (Line/Area/Bar/Donut, brand-ramp colours, dynamic-import friendly), **AppShell** (brand header + sidebar; `visibleNav` filters by injected `hasFlag`/`can` predicates so a disabled module/absent permission έΗΤ NO nav entry; slots for language/theme/account), Feature (prop-driven flag wrapper), ShortcutScope (`mod+k`/sequence combos, suppressed in inputs unless opted in, `eventToToken`), VoiceInput/`useVoiceInput` (Web Speech, locale-aware, self-hides when unsupported).
- **Pure testable seams:** `screenshotBypassEnabled`/`screenshotTokenValid`/`grantsScreenshotAccess` (+ `SCREENSHOT_TOKEN_PARAM`), exposed on the lean **`@mp/ui/screenshot`** subpath so the edge middleware imports the logic WITHOUT dragging React/Radix in. `evaluateBudgets`/`withinBudget`/`DEFAULT_BUDGETS` perf-budget model (longest-prefix route match, JS+total ceilings).

*Web app wiring.* `tailwind.config.ts` spreads the `@mp/ui` preset + scans app & `packages/ui/src`; `postcss.config.mjs` (tailwind+autoprefixer); `globals.css` gains the `@tailwind` layers + `--mp-*` tokens at the TOP (legacy `.mp-*` styles kept below, authoritative on conflict); `ThemeProvider` added to `layout.tsx` (`defaultMode="system"`); added dep `lucide-react`. **`/ui` showcase** (server shell + `UiShowcase` client) built ENTIRELY from @mp/ui, framed in AppShell (nav proves Pharmacy-POS flag OFF έΗΤ hidden, Lab ON έΗΤ shown), dynamic-imported chart (`DemoChart` via `next/dynamic ssr:false`), all copy from new `ui.*` i18n keys έΗΤ polished light/dark, RTL in Urdu, brand-token driven. **`middleware.ts`** screenshot token (matcher excludes static assets). **`/lh-bloated`** intentional canary (`import * as` lucide + eager chart έΗΤ 431 kB first-load vs `/ui` 279 kB).

*Perf / Lighthouse gate.* `lighthouserc.json` (LHCI: `next start`, public routes `/ /login /ui`, mobile emulation, assert perf/a11y/best-practices `minScore 0.9`, `budgetsPath`) + `budgets.json` (script 250 KB / total 700 KB / timing budgets). `.github/workflows/ci.yml`: the Lighthouse **stub replaced** with a real job (build web + deps έΗΤ `lhci autorun`) + a NEGATIVE step that fails if `/lh-bloated` scores έΚξ90 (proves the gate bites). Root `lighthouse` script. The internal "fast-&-smooth" budget check is the unit-tested `evaluateBudgets` seam (a 900-KiB route fails).

**i18n keys.** New nested `ui.*` block (58 keys) added to EN + UR catalogs (parity preserved) covering the showcase, nav labels, theme-toggle labels, and the demo tag.

**Runtime verification (driven via `next start`).**
- Screenshot token έΑΦ Case A (NODE_ENV=production, APP_ENV unset): `/ui` 200; `/ui?screenshot_token=<secret>` **200 with NO `x-mp-screenshot` header** (bypass OFF regardless, param ignored, fail-closed). Case B (APP_ENV=staging): correct token έΗΤ **200 + `x-mp-screenshot: read-only`**; wrong token έΗΤ **403**.
- `/ui` SSR HTML contains design-system utilities (`min-h-touch`, `bg-primary`/`text-brand`), a compiled `/_next/static/css/*` stylesheet, the showcase heading, and the AppShell nav with Lab shown + Pharmacy-POS hidden (flag-gated).

**Do-NOT-break honoured.** 07 brand `--brand-*` contract + 08 i18n unchanged; @mp/ui component APIs are additive/stable; Lighthouse gate + budgets now permanent in CI; screenshot bypass fail-closed & staging-only.

**Verification gates (all green).** typecheck **26/26**; lint **15/15**; turbo build **15/15** (web build: `/ui` 279 kB / `/lh-bloated` 431 kB first-load, middleware 34.5 kB); jest **19 tasks** έΑΦ NEW `@mp/ui` **38/38** (8 suites: cn, screenshot, perf-budget, button, data-list, module-tabs, app-shell, misc[theme/feature/shortcut/toast/search-select]) + api 175/175 + import 18/18 + db 67/67 + notifications 18/18 + offline 29/29 + consent 18/18 + **i18n 19/19 incl. ENέΗΦUR parity**. White-label: brand-token driven (verified); RTL verified. Performance: Lighthouse job wired in CI (not run in-sandbox έΑΦ no Chrome); budget logic unit-proven.

**Notes / caveats.**
- Lighthouse itself is CI-only (needs headless Chrome, not available in this sandbox); the config + budgets + negative canary are committed and the budget-evaluation logic is unit-tested here.
- `MODULE_TYPELESS_PACKAGE_JSON` warning on `dist/tailwind-preset.js` when Next loads the config is cosmetic; `@mp/ui` is NOT marked `type:module` on purpose (its CJS `jest.config.js`/`jest.setup.ts` would break).
- Urdu font strategy stays the 08 local-font stack; a self-hosted subset woff2 (same `unicode-range`+`font-display:swap` contract) is `[DECIDE AT BUILD]` if local fonts prove insufficient.

## Build-step 12 έΑΦ Foundation: Import / Export Engine

- **Work-type:** FEATURE. **Phase:** Foundation / item 12. **Branch:** `feat/12-import-export` (stacked on `feat/11-consent-terms`). **Depends on:** 02 (tenancy/RLS), 04 (RBAC permission), 06 (audit). **Reused by:** 14 patients, 19 lab catalog, 20/28 pharmacy, 29 suppliers έΑΦ generic engine.
- **Schema/migration/RLS/permission impact:** NEW migration `20260704090000_import_export` έΑΦ two tenant-scoped tables + one enum (`CREATE TYPE "ImportStatus"`). Both tables call the canonical `apply_tenant_rls()` (02) έΗΤ `tenant_isolation` policy (visible/writable only under own `app.tenant_id` GUC; WITH CHECK blocks cross-tenant writes; no-context έΗΤ zero rows, fail-closed). NO new permission έΑΦ the sample importer reuses the existing `purchase.manage` (suppliers). NO new global guard (routes ride the JwtAuthGuard; per-entity permission checked programmatically). No auth-contract change; no feature flag (import/export is always-on infra).

**Problem.** A tenant onboards by loading 20kέΑΥ50k medicines, a test catalog, patients and suppliers from Excel/CSV, and must export anything it can see. Hand entry is impossible; a bad import is dangerous. Need validated, previewable, resumable bulk import + universal filtered export, idempotent by natural key (no duplicates on re-import).

**What changed.**
- **NEW pure package `@mp/import`** (framework-free, side-effect-free, deterministic έΑΦ reused by API + web + every consuming module):
  - the `Importer<Parsed>` contract each module declares: `entity`, `permission`, `columns` (`ColumnSpec{key,header,type,required,example}`), `upsertKey` (natural key), `validateRow(coerced,rowNumber)`, `transformRow(coerced)`;
  - an **RFC-4180 CSV/TSV codec**: `parseDelimited`/`parseCsv` (quoted fields, `""` escapes, embedded commas/newlines, CRLF or LF, unquoted-cell trim, blank-line skip, case-insensitive header match) + `serializeDelimited`/`serializeCsv` (quote only where required, stringify non-string/null);
  - `buildTemplate` (header + one example row); `dryRun` (structural required/type coercion έΗΤ then importer `validateRow` only on clean rows έΗΤ valid/invalid split + transformed `validRows` + `errors[]` + `missingHeaders`, NOTHING persisted); `buildErrorReportCsv` (row/field/message); `planUpsert` (collapse by natural key, last-wins, trimmed+case-insensitive key έΗΤ no duplicates) + `chunk`; `ImportStatus`/`IMPORT_STATUSES` vocabulary.
- **DB:** `ImportJob` (`status ImportStatus` default VALIDATED, `total`/`valid`/`invalid`/`applied` progress counters, `payload Json?` = staged transformed valid rows for apply, `errorReport String?` = inline CSV, `errorReportKey String?` RESERVED for future R2 object key, `createdBy`, `@@index([tenantId,entity])`) + `ImportStatus` enum (`UPLOADED|VALIDATED|APPLYING|DONE|FAILED`) + demo target `ImportDemoSupplier` (`name`/`phone`/`city`, `@@unique([tenantId,phone])`). `ImportStatus` re-exported from `@mp/db`. Isolation proven in `packages/db/src/import-isolation.spec.ts` (real 01έΗΤ12 migrations in pglite; T1/T2 see only own jobs+rows, WITH CHECK blocks cross-tenant insert, no-context έΗΤ 0 rows).
- **API `ImportModule`:** `ImportRegistry` (maps entityέΗΤ`EntityImporter` = pure spec + `upsertChunk(tenantId,rows)` + `exportColumns` + `exportRows(tenantId,filters)`; ships sample `demoSupplierImporter` bound to the demo target, natural key `phone`, `validateRow` enforces 7έΑΥ15 digit phone). `ImportService`: `upload` (parse έΗΤ dryRun έΗΤ create VALIDATED job staging validRows + errorReport; returns preview counts + first 100 errors + errorCount, writes NOTHING to target) ┬╖ `apply` (planUpsert dedupe έΗΤ APPLYING έΗΤ chunked (`APPLY_CHUNK_SIZE=500`) idempotent `upsertChunk`, `setApplied` per chunk for progress, resume from `applied` offset, on error έΗΤ FAILED keeping progress, else έΗΤ DONE; re-applying a DONE job is a no-op) ┬╖ `getTemplate` ┬╖ `getJob`/`listJobs` ┬╖ `getErrorReport` ┬╖ `exportCsv` (importer `exportRows` honours filters, serialized to CSV). Repo seam `ImportRepo` + `PrismaImportRepo` (Prisma `upsert` by compound unique `tenantId_phone`) + `FakeImportRepo`. Controller (`@Controller()`): `GET /import/:entity/template`, `POST /import/:entity/upload` (`@Audited import.upload`), `POST /import/:entity/:jobId/apply` (`@Audited import.apply`), `GET /import/:entity/jobs`, `GET /import/:entity/:jobId`, `GET /import/:entity/:jobId/errors`, `GET /export/:listKey?filters` έΑΦ each resolves the entity's importer (404 if unknown) and checks its DYNAMIC permission via `PermissionService.roleHasPermission` (403 if missing); CSV endpoints set `Content-Type: text/csv`. `ImportModule` imports `PermissionsModule`, exports `ImportRegistry`+`ImportService`; registered last in `AppModule` (no global guard έΗΤ order immaterial).
- **Web (EN+UR):** `/admin/import` server shell + `ImportWizard` client island έΑΦ entity picker (demo_supplier), step 1 download template, step 2 paste/upload CSV έΗΤ Validate έΗΤ PREVIEW (total/valid/invalid chips, missing-header warning, row-error table + "έΑοN more" + error-report download), step 3 confirm apply (disabled when 0 valid) έΗΤ applied summary / failed-retry hint, plus a filtered Export (city filter) button. Access probed on mount (401έΗΤsign-in, 403έΗΤno-access). CSV downloads via fetch+Blob. New `mp-import-*` styles in `globals.css`; 34 EN+UR i18n keys (parity green).
- **Launch notes ([DECIDE AT BUILD]):** upload takes CSV/TSV text as a JSON field today (multipart/streamed upload via a FileInterceptor deferred); `payload` staged as an inline JSON blob + apply runs in-process chunked (object/blob store for large payloads + Redis/worker background dispatch deferred; `errorReportKey` reserved for R2 offload); the engine is codec-agnostic έΑΦ Excel/xlsx (SheetJS) parse/serialize is a swappable codec deferred (CSV/TSV shipped).
- **Verification gates (all green):** typecheck **26/26**, lint **15/15**, turbo build **15/15**; jest έΑΦ `@mp/import` **18/18** (codec/template/dryRun/error-report/planUpsert/chunk), `@mp/db` **67/67** (11 suites; +6 import-isolation), `@mp/api` **175/175** (22 suites; +11 import e2e incl. 401/403/404 gating, dry-run-writes-nothing, apply-idempotent-no-duplicate, audited, error-report, filtered export, 20k-row background apply with progress, FAILED-job resume), `@mp/i18n` **19/19** (incl. ENέΗΦUR parity), unchanged: notifications 18/18, offline 29/29, consent 18/18. Isolation: import jobs + imported rows tenant-scoped (T1/T2 pglite proof). No feature-flag/vertical/performance/white-label surface at this step.

## Build-step 11 έΑΦ Foundation: Terms & Consent Gate

- **Work-type:** FEATURE. **Phase:** Foundation / item 11. **Branch:** `feat/11-consent-terms` (stacked on `feat/10-offline-core`). **Depends on:** 02 (tenancy/RLS), 03 (auth principal), 06 (audit).
- **Schema/migration/RLS/permission impact:** NEW migration `20260703180000_consent_terms` έΑΦ two tenant-scoped tables + three enums. Both tables call the canonical `apply_tenant_rls()` (02) έΗΤ `tenant_isolation` policy (visible/writable only under own `app.tenant_id` GUC; WITH CHECK blocks cross-tenant writes; no-context έΗΤ zero rows, fail-closed). NEW tenant permission `consent.manage` (added to `PERMISSIONS` + `ADMIN` role defaults in `@mp/shared`). NEW global `ConsentGuard` registered by `ConsentModule` (acts only on `@RequiresConsent` routes; runs after `JwtAuthGuard`). No auth-contract change; no feature flag (consent is always-on infra).

**Problem.** Liability protection needs explicit, VERSIONED, logged consent έΑΦ staff (system use), patients (treatment, data use, AI disclaimer), tenants (service terms). The AI assistant must capture a disclaimer before first use. Wording changes after a Pakistani-lawyer review έΗΤ it must be DATA, not code, and a new version must re-prompt.

**What changed.**
- **NEW pure package `@mp/consent`** (framework-free, side-effect-free, deterministic έΑΦ caller passes `nowMs`; reused by web + API + unit tests):
  - Vocabulary: `ConsentAudience` (STAFF/PATIENT/TENANT), `ConsentType` (SYSTEM_USE/TREATMENT/DATA_USE/AI_ASSISTANT_DISCLAIMER/SERVICE_TERMS), `ConsentSubjectType` (USER/PATIENT), `ConsentLang` (EN/UR); ordered `CONSENT_*` arrays; `AUDIENCE_SUBJECT` map.
  - `REQUIRED_CONSENTS` έΑΦ the blanket onboarding gate per audience (STAFFέΗΤ[SYSTEM_USE], PATIENTέΗΤ[TREATMENT,DATA_USE], TENANTέΗΤ[SERVICE_TERMS]). `AI_ASSISTANT_DISCLAIMER` deliberately NOT blanket έΑΦ it is an ACTION gate via `@RequiresConsent`.
  - `effectiveDocument` / `effectiveDocumentsByType` έΑΦ the CURRENT version = newest whose `effectiveFrom` has passed (future-dated publish does not prompt yet), language-preferred.
  - `isConsentSatisfied` / `outstandingConsents` / `gateFor` έΑΦ the gate: a subject satisfies a type iff it holds a record at version έΚξ current; a NEW (higher) version re-opens the gate; older records stay valid history. A required type with no in-force document is omitted (enforceable the moment one is published, no code change).
  - `sanitizeConsentContext` + `maskIp` έΑΦ whitelist only safe keys (`ip`/`userAgent`/`source`/`lang`), mask the IP (v4 last octetέΗΤ`x`, v6 keep 2 hextets), clamp lengths, drop unknown keys, return `undefined` when nothing safe remains (┬π5 έΑΦ no raw sensitive data ever stored).
  - 18 unit tests (`consent.spec.ts`).
- **DB (`@mp/db`):** `ConsentDocument` (id, tenantId, audience, type, lang, version, title, body=SWAPPABLE legal text, effectiveFrom, supersedesId, updatedBy, createdAt; `@@unique([tenantId,audience,type,lang,version])`, `@@index([tenantId,audience,type])`) + `ConsentRecord` (id, tenantId, subjectType, subjectId, documentId, type, version, context Json?, acceptedAt; `@@index([tenantId,subjectType,subjectId])`, `@@index([tenantId,documentId])`) + enums `Audience`/`ConsentType`/`SubjectType`. NEW `consent-isolation.spec.ts` (pglite, real 01έΑΥ11 migrations): T1 sees only its own docs/records, wording never bleeds, WITH CHECK blocks cross-tenant publish + accept, no-context έΗΤ zero rows.
- **API (`ConsentModule`):** `ConsentService` over a `ConsentRepo` seam (`PrismaConsentRepo` via `runWithTenant`; `FakeConsentRepo` for e2e) + injectable `CONSENT_CLOCK`. `publishDocument()` (auto-increment version, link `supersedesId`, default effective=now έΑΦ editing wording = new version = re-open gate, no redeploy), `required()` (outstanding docs for an audience), `accept()` (idempotent per subject+type+version; masked context), `isTypeSatisfied()` (fail-closed; backs the guard). Global `ConsentGuard` + `@RequiresConsent(type)` decorator έΗΤ 403 `{ error:'consent_required', type, document, message }` until current version accepted έΑΦ the STABLE contract AI steps (32/36έΑΥ39) reuse. Endpoints `/consent`: `GET documents` + `PUT documents` (gated by `consent.manage`, `@Audited consent.document.publish`), `GET required?audience=&lang=` + `POST accept` (any-authed, tenant-scoped, `@Audited consent.accept`, context masked from req ip/user-agent), `GET demo/ai` (`@RequiresConsent('AI_ASSISTANT_DISCLAIMER')` έΑΦ proves the gate). 10 e2e tests (`consent.e2e.spec.ts`).
- **Web:** EN+UR `/admin/consent` (`ConsentManager` island) έΑΦ publish a versioned doc per audience/type/lang with live direction-aware (UR RTL) preview, optional effective date, and the published-versions list; server enforces `consent.manage`. EN+UR `/consent` (`ConsentGate` island) έΑΦ the outstanding STAFF documents, each readable + scrollable, an EN/UR document-language toggle that re-fetches, scroll-to-end-then-explicit-"I agree" recording the exact version. 37 NEW i18n keys added to BOTH catalogs (parity kept). Consent-specific CSS in `globals.css`.
- **Enum labels:** consent types/audiences rendered via `consentType*`/`consentAudience*` catalog keys (no raw codes).

**Launch note / `[DECIDE AT BUILD]`:** final legal wording is a Pakistani lawyer's call έΑΦ the model keeps it swappable as `ConsentDocument.body` via an admin edit, no code change. Patient/tenant subject wiring (14/31) plugs the patient subject through `ConsentService` directly; the `@RequiresConsent` + `AI_ASSISTANT_DISCLAIMER` contract is stable.

**Fixes during integration (pre-commit, uncommitted WIP was mid-flight):** (1) e2e `OTP_TRANSPORT` override used `{ deliver }` έΑΦ corrected to the real `OtpTransport.send` interface (09 swapped the transport). (2) the AI-demo e2e asserted `body.message.error`/`.type`; NestJS serializes a `ForbiddenException(object)` payload as the body verbatim, so corrected to `body.error`/`body.type` (matches the guard's deliberate structured payload).

**Verification gates (all green):** typecheck 24/24 ┬╖ lint 14/14 ┬╖ turbo build 14/14 (both `/admin/consent` + `/consent` routes emitted) ┬╖ jest: `@mp/db` 61/61 (10 suites, incl. consent-isolation T1/T2), `@mp/api` 164/164 (21 suites, incl. 10 consent e2e), `@mp/i18n` 19/19 (incl. ENέΗΦUR parity, +37 keys), `@mp/consent` 18/18, `@mp/notifications` 18/18, `@mp/offline` 29/29 ┬╖ i18n parity: EQUAL ┬╖ isolation: T1/T2 proven (documents + records + WITH CHECK + fail-closed).
- **Files:** NEW `packages/consent/**` (pkg + `src/index.ts` + `src/consent.spec.ts` + configs), `packages/db/prisma/migrations/20260703180000_consent_terms/migration.sql`, `packages/db/src/consent-isolation.spec.ts`, `apps/api/src/consent/**` (module, service, controller, guard, repositories, dto, constants, __fakes__, index, e2e), `apps/web/app/admin/consent/{page.tsx,ConsentManager.tsx}`, `apps/web/app/consent/{page.tsx,ConsentGate.tsx}`. MODIFIED `packages/db/prisma/schema.prisma` (2 models + 3 enums), `packages/shared/src/permissions.ts` (`consent.manage`), `apps/api/src/app.module.ts` (import `ConsentModule`), `apps/api/package.json` + `pnpm-lock.yaml` (`@mp/consent` dep), `packages/i18n/src/messages/{en,ur}.json` (+37 keys), `apps/web/app/globals.css` (consent styles).

## Build-step 10 έΑΦ Foundation: Offline-First Core

- **Work-type:** FEATURE (cross-cutting offline-first sync seam; always-on infra, never a flag). **Phase:** Foundation (item 10 of 39). **Branch:** `feat/10-offline-core` (stacked on `feat/09-notifications-engine`; controller merges to `staging` at checkpoint). **Date:** 2026-07-03.
- **Depends on:** 01 (monorepo + SW shell), 03 (auth/tenant principal). **Load-bearing for the critical-path modules** έΑΦ 15 token, 16 vitals, 18 capture, 20 POS build their offline behaviour on this step's `enqueue`/idempotency/conflict hooks. Stock-affecting modules (20/28/29/30) MUST follow the compensating-write strategy documented here.
- **Problem:** clinics lose internet; token/vitals/POS/rx-capture must keep working offline and reconcile on reconnect with NO double-posting and a sane conflict policy, while AI features (which need the network) queue. This lands the always-on local-first store + outbox + idempotent-sync + conflict-policy seam and proves it end-to-end with a demo entity, before the real entities exist.
- **NEW package `@mp/offline`** (pure, framework-free, reused by BOTH web client + API έΑΦ same "engine package" pattern as `@mp/notifications`; no Prisma/React/timer/`Date.now` dependency, deterministic): the action/outbox model (`OfflineAction` = `clientActionId` + entity/op/payload/`baseRev`/`requiresNetwork`/createdAt) + queue helpers (`enqueue` idempotent, `dedupeActions`, `drainableActions`, `pendingNetworkActions`, `removeAction`, `canRunWhileOffline`); the idempotency contract (`SYNC_IDEMPOTENCY_HEADER='idempotency-key'`, `isValidClientActionId`); reconnect `syncBackoffMs` (exp, capped); the pull cursor (`SyncCursor`, `ZERO_CURSOR`, `advanceCursor`, `parseCursor`); `deriveSyncStatus` (offlineέΗΤerrorέΗΤsyncingέΗΤsynced); and the **conflict policy** έΑΦ `detectConflict` (stale base = baseRev<serverRev), `resolveServerLww` (DEFAULT server-authoritative LWW, server wins + logs on conflict), `applyCompensatingDelta`/`resolveCompensatingDelta` (additive stock write, order/concurrency-independent, never clobbered by LWW), and a per-entity override registry `ConflictPolicy`/`defaultConflictPolicy(stockEntities)`. Own jest suite (29 unit tests).
- **Schema/migration:** NEW migration `20260703170000_offline_core`. Three tables: `SyncIdempotency` (id, tenant_id, user_id, client_action_id UNIQUE, result JSON, created_at) έΑΦ the dedupe ledger; `SyncDemoEntity` (id, tenant_id, name, stock_qty, `rev` = tenant-monotonic revision that BOTH orders the change feed AND is the optimistic-lock token, updated_by, updated_at; indexed `(tenant_id,rev)`) έΑΦ demo critical-path entity proving the whole flow; `SyncConflict` (id, tenant_id, entity, entity_id, client_action_id, base_rev, server_rev, resolution, created_at; indexed `(tenant_id,created_at)`) έΑΦ the append-only conflict log. No new enums.
- **RLS:** ALL THREE tables tenant-scoped via the canonical `apply_tenant_rls()` policy (02) έΑΦ a device reads/writes only its own tenant's idempotency keys, entities and conflicts; WITH CHECK blocks cross-tenant writes; no-context = zero rows (fail-closed). NEW `packages/db/src/offline-isolation.spec.ts` proves T1/T2 isolation + WITH-CHECK block (idempotency + entity) + fail-closed (all three) on the REAL 01έΗΤ10 migration chain in pglite (7 tests).
- **Feature-flags:** έηΨ none exposed έΑΦ offline core is always-on infra.
- **API `SyncModule`:** `SyncService` with three load-bearing seams έΑΦ `runIdempotent(tenantId,userId,clientActionId,fn)` (at-most-once: stored result returned on replay, `fn` never re-runs έΗΤ no double-post); `getChanges(tenantId,since)` (tenant deltas where rev>since + advanced cursor); conflict reconciliation. Demo methods exercise every rule: `upsertDemo` (create always applies; update detects stale `baseRev` έΗΤ server-authoritative LWW, logs a `SyncConflict`, server value wins; clean base έΗΤ apply + bump rev); `applyStockDelta` (compensating additive write, deduped). Holds a `ConflictPolicy` (default server-lww; stock entities register compensating). Repo seam (`SyncRepo`) + Prisma impl (all via `runWithTenant`; `nextRev` = `max(rev)+1` per tenant) + in-memory fake. NEW `@IdempotencyKey()` param decorator reads the `Idempotency-Key` header (the reusable seam every critical-path mutation rides).
- **Endpoints (`/sync`, all authed):** `GET changes?since=` (core pull, any authed user, tenant-scoped έΑΦ RLS scopes it, cursor advances); `POST demo/upsert` + `POST demo/stock` (require `Idempotency-Key` header else 400; gated by NEW `sync.inspect`; `@Audited`); `GET conflicts` (conflict log, gated). Demo routes prove acceptance before real modules exist.
- **Permission:** NEW `T('sync.inspect', έΑο)` in `@mp/shared` PERMISSIONS (additive; TENANT scope); granted to ADMIN + MANAGER defaults (TENANT_OWNER via `permissionKeysByScope('TENANT')`; SUPER_ADMIN via full reconcile).
- **Web (offline client + `/admin/sync`, EN+UR):** NEW `lib/offline-db.ts` (IndexedDB outbox έΑΦ durable, keyed by clientActionId, graceful no-op where storage is unavailable) + `lib/offline.tsx` `OfflineProvider`/`useSyncStatus` (local-first `enqueue`, online/offline events, outbox processor draining on reconnect with the pure backoff; network-only/AI actions queue + surface a "will run when online" hint) wired into `layout.tsx` around all pages; NEW `OfflineIndicator` (fixed offline/syncing/synced badge, RTL-aware, always visible). NEW `/admin/sync` inspector (`page.tsx` + `SyncDemo.tsx`) έΑΦ create a demo item offline (queues έΗΤ syncs on reconnect), sell stock (compensating write), queue an AI action (network-only), watch synced items + the conflict log. 22 NEW flat i18n keys `sync*`/`noSyncAccess` in EN+UR (parity gate green). NEW `.mp-sync*` styles in `globals.css`. `@mp/offline` added to web + api deps. No ESLint i18n-guard violations.
- **Acceptance (all met):** ┬π1 a critical-path action records locally + queues offline and syncs on reconnect, indicator shows offlineέΗΤsyncingέΗΤsynced; ┬π2 replaying the same `clientActionId` does not double-post (idempotency proven, incl. stock replay applied once); ┬π3 `GET /sync/changes?since=` returns only this tenant's deltas since the cursor + cursor advances (other tenant sees nothing); ┬π4 a simulated stale-base conflict is detected, reconciled server-first, and logged; ┬π5 the compensating-write hook is exercised by a stock delta (two decrements both land έΑΦ proves stock not clobbered by LWW); ┬π6 an AI-flagged action queues with `requiresNetwork` and runs only once online; ┬π7 gates green + T1/T2 isolation proven.
- **Conflict-policy default + hooks (per ┬π3.3):** default = server-authoritative LWW + `SyncConflict` log; per-entity override registry (`ConflictPolicy`) delivered so 20/28/29/30 register `compensating-delta` for their stock entities; the compensating (additive) write is documented + unit-proven here. Per-module conflict specifics remain `[DECIDE AT BUILD]`.
- **`[DECIDE AT BUILD]` recorded (launch notes):** the engine dispatches the outbox in-process from the web client today (fetch on reconnect); a Redis/BullMQ worker-backed server dispatch + a richer per-device delta feed (currently the demo entity's `rev`-ordered rows) land when the worker/real entities are built. Per-module conflict rules for token/vitals/POS confirmed at each module's build.
- **Do-NOT-break upheld:** auth/tenant context untouched; `enqueue`/idempotency contract is the stable seam 15/16/18/20 consume; stock uses compensating writes (never LWW); offline core is always-on (no flag).
- **Verification gates:** typecheck **22/22**; lint **13/13**; turbo build **13/13**; jest έΑΦ `@mp/db` **55/55** (9 suites; +7 offline-isolation), `@mp/api` **154/154** (20 suites; +10 sync e2e), `@mp/i18n` **19/19** (incl. parity), `@mp/notifications` **18/18**, `@mp/offline` **29/29** (NEW). i18n parity έεΦ. RLS isolation (all three offline tables, real 01έΗΤ10 chain, pglite) έεΦ. `prisma validate` έεΦ. Full pre-existing suite green (no regressions).

## Build-step 09 έΑΦ Foundation: Notifications Engine (provider-agnostic messaging)

- **Work-type:** FEATURE (always-on provider-agnostic messaging engine; never a flag). **Phase:** Foundation (item 9 of 39). **Branch:** `feat/09-notifications-engine` (stacked on `feat/08-i18n-base`; controller merges to `staging` at checkpoint). **Date:** 2026-07-03.
- **Depends on:** 02 (tenant RLS + `runWithTenant`), 06 (`@Audited` + AuditInterceptor), 07 (BrandingProfile sender identity), 08 (`Lang` enum + i18n catalogs). **Replaces the 03 OTP stub transport WITHOUT changing 03's API.** Consumed in-process by every later messaging module (reminders 16/17, report-ready 19, follow-ups, rx-send 18) via `NotificationService.notify()`.
- **Problem:** many modules message patients/staff; without one engine each reinvents delivery/templates/status and the per-tenant white-label sender identity leaks everywhere. This lands the single load-bearing engine.
- **NEW package `@mp/notifications`** (pure, framework-free, reused by API + web preview έΑΦ mirrors the `@mp/brand`/`@mp/flags` "engine package" pattern; string-union enums mirror the Prisma enums so it carries no Prisma dependency): `NotificationProvider` contract (`{channel; send(msg): ProviderResult}`) + `OutboundMessage`/`ProviderResult`; `renderTemplate`/`extractVariables`/`missingVariables` (`{var}` interpolation, same grammar as `@mp/i18n`); `resolveChannelChain` (WhatsAppέΗΤSMS fallback, config-toggled); `RetryPolicy`/`shouldRetry`/`retryBackoffMs` (default 3 attempts, exp backoff); `webhookNextStatus` (guarded transitions έΑΦ QUEUEDέΗΤSENTέΗΤDELIVERED/FAILED, DELIVERED terminal, idempotent/out-of-order events ignored); `requiresApproval` (WhatsApp only); built-in **system templates** (`SYSTEM_TEMPLATES`, `auth.otp` EN+UR bodies with `{app}`/`{code}`) so system messages send before a tenant authors anything. Own jest suite (18 unit tests).
- **Schema/migration:** NEW migration `20260703160000_notifications_engine`. `NotificationTemplate` (id, tenant_id, key, channel, lang, body, variables JSON, status DRAFT/APPROVED; `@@unique([tenantId,key,channel,lang])`) + `NotificationLog` (id, tenant_id, to_ref, channel, template_key, status QUEUED/SENT/DELIVERED/FAILED, provider_msg_id, attempts, error; indexed on `(tenant_id,created_at)` + `(tenant_id,provider_msg_id)`). NEW enums `Channel {WHATSAPP SMS INAPP}`, `TemplateStatus {DRAFT APPROVED}`, `DeliveryStatus {QUEUED SENT DELIVERED FAILED}` (exported from `@mp/db`).
- **RLS:** BOTH tables tenant-scoped via the canonical `apply_tenant_rls()` policy (02) έΑΦ a tenant's templates + delivery logs are visible/writable only under its own `app.tenant_id` GUC; WITH CHECK blocks cross-tenant writes; no-context = zero rows (fail-closed). NEW `packages/db/src/notifications-isolation.spec.ts` proves T1/T2 isolation + WITH-CHECK block (both tables) + fail-closed on the REAL 01έΗΤ09 migration chain in pglite (6 tests).
- **Feature-flags:** έηΨ none exposed έΑΦ the engine is always-on infra (load-bearing for all later modules). Sits under the flag engine; providers configured via env/secrets, never a flag.
- **API `NotificationsModule`:** `NotificationService.notify({tenantId,to,channel?,templateKey,vars?,lang?,bypassConsent?})` έΑΦ consent hook έΗΤ per-tenant sender identity (07 `brand.identity.notificationSender`, also feeds `{app}`) έΗΤ template resolve (tenant row wins; regulated-channel rows must be APPROVED else 400; else built-in system default) + render έΗΤ create QUEUED log έΗΤ walk channel-fallback chain with a **fresh per-channel retry counter** έΗΤ on success update log SENT+providerMsgId, on total failure FAILED (returns `{logId,status,channel,providerMsgId}`; consent-blocked returns `{logId:null,status:'BLOCKED'}` with no log). `sendOtp()` (bypasses consent, WhatsAppέΗΤSMS, `auth.otp` template). `handleWebhook()` (guarded status advance by providerMsgId). Template mgmt: `listTemplates`/`upsertTemplate` (variables auto-derived from body; edit resets to DRAFT)/`approveTemplate`/`listLogs`. Repo seam (`NotificationRepo`) + Prisma impl (all via `runWithTenant`) + in-memory fake. Providers: `buildProviderRegistry(config)` binds per channel; **2 config-swappable mock WhatsApp providers** (`mock-cloud`/`mock-bsp` via `NOTIF_WHATSAPP_PROVIDER`, no secret in repo) + `MockSmsProvider`/`MockInAppProvider`; `FAILING_RECIPIENT` sentinel for tests. `ConsentProvider` seam + `AllowAllConsentProvider` default (14 swaps real patient consent through the same seam). `NOTIFICATION_OPTIONS` (fallbackEnabled + retry policy) built from config.
- **Endpoints (`/notifications`, all authed; management gated by NEW `notifications.manage`):** `GET templates` (list + channel/lang vocab + system keys), `PUT templates` (upsert, `@Audited`), `POST templates/:id/approve` (`@Audited`), `POST templates/preview` (pure render, no send), `GET logs` (status/channel filters, recipients masked to last-3), `POST demo/send` (gated engine exercise, `@Audited`), `POST webhook` (simulated provider status advance, tenant-scoped). Wire types use `@mp/notifications` string unions (portable έΑΦ avoids TS2742 on Prisma deep types).
- **Permission:** NEW `T('notifications.manage', έΑο)` in `@mp/shared` PERMISSIONS (additive; TENANT scope); granted to ADMIN + MANAGER defaults (TENANT_OWNER gets it via `permissionKeysByScope('TENANT')`; SUPER_ADMIN via full reconcile). Boot reconcile syncs it.
- **03 OTP swap (do-NOT-break):** `apps/api/src/auth/notification-otp-transport.ts` `NotificationOtpTransport implements OtpTransport` (injects `NotificationService`, routes `send()`έΗΤ`sendOtp()`); AuthModule now `imports: [JwtModule, AuditModule, NotificationsModule]` and binds `OTP_TRANSPORT`έΗΤ`NotificationOtpTransport` (was `StubOtpTransport`, retained as reference). **Auth request/verify API unchanged.** No DI cycle (NotificationsModule imports BrandModule, not AuthModule); NotificationsModule re-declares `APP_CONFIG` with the same `loadConfig` factory (single test override covers both). Global guard order (JwtέΗΤFeatureέΗΤRolesέΗΤAuditInterceptor) preserved έΑΦ NotificationsModule adds no global guard.
- **Config (`@mp/config`):** NEW `NOTIF_WHATSAPP_PROVIDER` (`mock-cloud`|`mock-bsp`, default mock-cloud), `NOTIF_CHANNEL_FALLBACK` (bool, default true), `NOTIF_MAX_ATTEMPTS` (default 3). Fake config in auth `__fakes__` extended to match.
- **Web (`/admin/notifications`, EN+UR):** server `page.tsx` + client `NotificationManager.tsx` έΑΦ template editor (key/channel/lang/body) with **LIVE preview via the shared pure `renderTemplate`** (UR body rendered RTL-correct via its own `dir`, variable chips from `extractVariables`), approve action, and a status-filtered delivery-log table (masked recipients). 30 NEW flat i18n keys `notif*`/`noNotifAccess` in EN+UR (parity gate green). NEW `.mp-notif*` styles in `globals.css`. `@mp/notifications` added to web deps (proves the pure core is shared with the browser). No ESLint i18n-guard violations.
- **Acceptance (all met):** ┬π1 send via mockέΗΤlogέΗΤsimulated webhook QUEUEDέΗΤSENTέΗΤDELIVERED + failure recorded & retried; ┬π2 03 OTP flows through engine (transport swapped, API unchanged); ┬π3 templates per tenant/channel/language, UR RTL, variables substitute; ┬π4 per-tenant sender identity applied + WhatsAppέΗΤSMS fallback; ┬π5 provider swappable by config (2 mocks, no secret in repo); ┬π6 consent hook honored (default allow, blocked recipient not messaged); ┬π7 gates green + i18n parity + T1/T2 isolation proven.
- **`[DECIDE AT BUILD]` recorded (launch notes):** concrete WhatsApp provider = Meta Cloud API direct candidate; per-tenant verified WhatsApp number + template-approval/sending-limits to confirm before launch. Real signed public provider webhook + Redis/BullMQ worker-backed dispatch land when the worker is built out έΑΦ the engine dispatches in-process synchronously today (with the retry policy applied) behind a provider/dispatch seam.
- **Verification gates:** typecheck **20/20**; lint **12/12**; turbo build **12/12**; jest έΑΦ `@mp/db` **48/48** (8 suites; +6 notifications-isolation), `@mp/api` **144/144** (19 suites; +13 notifications e2e), `@mp/i18n` **19/19** (incl. parity), `@mp/notifications` **18/18** (NEW). i18n parity έεΦ. RLS isolation (both notification tables, real 01έΗΤ09 chain, pglite) έεΦ. Full pre-existing suite green (no regressions from the OTP-transport swap).
- **Files (high-level):** NEW `packages/notifications/**` (package.json, tsconfig(.build), jest.config, src/index.ts, src/engine.spec.ts); `packages/db/prisma/migrations/20260703160000_notifications_engine/migration.sql`, `packages/db/src/notifications-isolation.spec.ts`; `apps/api/src/notifications/**` (constants, repositories, providers, consent, service, dto, controller, module, __fakes__, index, e2e spec); `apps/api/src/auth/notification-otp-transport.ts`; `apps/web/app/admin/notifications/{page,NotificationManager}.tsx`. EDITED `packages/db/prisma/schema.prisma` + `src/index.ts`; `packages/shared/src/permissions.ts`; `packages/config/src/index.ts`; `packages/i18n/src/messages/{en,ur}.json`; `apps/api/src/auth/{auth.module,__fakes__}.ts`; `apps/api/src/app.module.ts`; `apps/api/package.json`, `apps/web/package.json`, `apps/web/app/globals.css`.

## Build-step 08 έΑΦ Foundation: i18n Base (EN+UR UI, EN+UR+Roman AI)

- **Work-type:** FEATURE (cross-cutting internationalisation; always-on framework, never a flag). **Phase:** Foundation (item 8 of 39). **Branch:** `feat/08-i18n-base` (stacked on `feat/07-branding-whitelabel`; controller merges to `staging` at checkpoint). **Date:** 2026-07-03.
- **Depends on:** 01 (web app + monorepo). Consumed heavily by 13 (`@mp/ui`), 32 + 35έΑΥ39 (AI surfaces via the `AiLang` contract), and 09 (notification drafting language). Two-tier rule per ARCHITECTURE.md ┬π2.11 / ┬π12.5: UI = EN+UR; AI = EN+UR+Roman-UR.
- **Schema/migration:** NEW migration `20260703150000_i18n_language`. `enum Lang { EN UR }` (`CREATE TYPE`); `users` gains nullable `language "Lang"` (`ALTER TABLE ... ADD COLUMN`). NULL = not-yet-chosen (app resolves a role default). No new table.
- **RLS:** έηΨ no new isolation work έΑΦ the preference is a column on the already tenant-scoped `users` table, so it inherits the canonical `tenant_isolation` policy (02): visible/writable only under the row's own `app.tenant_id` GUC. Preference is therefore tenant-scoped by construction; the framework itself (catalogs/utilities) holds no tenant data. Proven in-CI: the existing `auth-isolation`/all 7 db isolation specs still pass on the real 01έΗΤ08 migration chain via pglite.
- **Feature-flags:** έηΨ none exposed έΑΦ i18n is always-on infra (the UI is bilingual by construction; the AI-language contract is load-bearing). Sits under the flag engine.
- **Do-NOT-break honored:** all UI copy now flows through the `@mp/i18n` catalog (enforced by the new lint rule). The `AiLang` contract (`@mp/shared`) is frozen and load-bearing for every AI surface. The parity gate is now a standing pipeline gate for all later steps. Existing pages untouched: `lib/auth-i18n.ts` re-based as a thin adapter over `@mp/i18n` keeping its `Lang`/`dir`/`resolveLang`/`tr`/`MsgKey` API stable. Global guard order (JwtέΗΤFeatureέΗΤRolesέΗΤAuditInterceptor) preserved έΑΦ `PreferencesModule` adds no global guard (authed + self-scoped).
- **Problem:** UI must serve English + Urdu at parity (a hard gate) and AI surfaces must additionally handle Roman Urdu. Without a framework + parity gate + no-hardcoded-string rule from the foundation, screens drift half-translated, RTL breaks, and Urdu fonts can wreck the perf budget.
- **What changed έΑΦ NEW package `@mp/i18n`:** the single source of truth for UI copy (framework-agnostic; web + API import it). `src/messages/en.json` + `ur.json` (migrated ALL prior UI copy from `auth-i18n.ts`, organised flat + `home`/`settings`/`i18n`/`enum` groups). `Locale='en'|'ur'`, `LOCALES`, `DEFAULT_LOCALE`, `isLocale`, `dir` (urέΗΤrtl), `resolveLocale`, `getMessages`, `translate(messages, dotPathOrFlatKey, vars?)` (`{var}` interpolation; returns the key on a miss so gaps are loud), `formatLabel(messages, domain, value)` (έΗΤ `enum.<domain>.<value>`, falls back to the raw value έΑΦ never crashes on a new enum member). `src/parity.ts` έΑΦ `flattenKeys`/`parityDiff` (two-way key-set diff). Jest (ts-jest): `parity.spec` (ENέΗΦUR identical key sets + missing-key detection BOTH directions), `format-label.spec` (labels EN+UR, dot-path/flat lookup, interpolation, safe fallback), `ai-lang.spec` (the AI classifier test set). Separate `tsconfig.build.json` keeps specs out of `dist`; imported JSON emits to `dist/messages`.
- **What changed έΑΦ `@mp/shared` (AI-language contract):** `ai-lang.ts` έΑΦ `AiLang='en'|'ur'|'roman-ur'`, `AI_LANGS`, `detectAiLang(input)` (Urdu/Arabic script blocks via `\u` escapes έΗΤ `ur`; else a distinctive Roman-Urdu cue lexicon incl. health terms έΗΤ `roman-ur`; else `en`; empty έΗΤ `en`), `normalizeForAi(input)` έΗΤ `{lang, text}` (trim + collapse whitespace). Exported from the `@mp/shared` index; every AI surface routes input through it so output mirrors the user's language across all three.
- **What changed έΑΦ API (`apps/api/src/preferences/`):** `PreferencesModule` (always-on, self-scoped). `PreferencesService` έΑΦ `getLanguage(principal)` έΗΤ stored `Lang` else `defaultLocaleForRole` (patientέΗΤ`ur`, staffέΗΤ`en`), returns `{language, explicit}`; `setLanguage(principal, locale)` persists; `Lang`έΘΕ`Locale` mapping. Repo seam `PreferencesRepo` (`getLanguage`/`setLanguage` via `runWithTenant`, updateMany pins tenant_id+id) + `PrismaPreferencesRepo` + `FakePreferencesRepo`. `parseSetLanguage` dto (wire contract = lowercase locale; 400 on anything else). `PreferencesController` έΑΦ `GET /me/preferences` (effective language), `PUT /me/preferences` (`@Audited({action:'preferences.language.update', entityType:'preferences'})`). Wired into AppModule; `Lang` re-exported from `@mp/db`; `@mp/i18n` added to `apps/api` deps.
- **What changed έΑΦ web (EN+UR):** `lib/i18n.tsx` έΑΦ `I18nProvider` (client; initial locale from the server-read cookie so SSR + first render agree; `setLocale` writes cookie `mp.locale` + localStorage + applies `<html lang/dir>` + best-effort `PUT /me/preferences` when signed in; on mount a signed-in user's stored choice is pulled back for cross-device sync), `useI18n`, `useT`. `lib/locale.ts` (neutral constants: `LOCALE_COOKIE`, storage key, max-age, `Locale`/`dir` re-exports). `lib/server-i18n.ts` έΑΦ `serverLocale(fallback)` reads the cookie via `next/headers` for `<html lang/dir>` (no flash). `components/LanguageSwitcher.tsx` (EN/UR toggle). `/settings` page + `SettingsClient` (switch persists live + `formatLabel` role-label demo, never raw codes). `layout.tsx` now async: reads `serverLocale()` έΗΤ `<html lang/dir>`, wraps in `I18nProvider`. `auth-i18n.ts` re-based as an adapter over `@mp/i18n` (`tr` gained an optional vars arg). All 7 server page shells (login ├Ω3, admin ├Ω4) resolve `?lang` έΗΤ cookie έΗΤ default via `serverLocale`. Home copy migrated to the catalog; patient phone placeholder + brand contrast-detail line moved into keys.
- **Urdu font strategy (┬π3.5, coordinated with 13):** `globals.css` `@font-face 'MP Urdu'` with `font-display: swap`, `unicode-range` restricted to the Arabic/Urdu blocks (CSS-level subset έΑΦ face only fetched when Urdu glyphs paint), and `src: local(...)` only (Nastaliq/Naskh/system fallback; no remote file έΗΤ zero extra network cost, offline-first). `:root[lang='ur'], [dir='rtl']` gets the Urdu stack + roomier line-height; a nested LTR island (phone field) is unaffected. 13 may add a self-hosted subset woff2 under the same swap + unicode-range contract.
- **No-hardcoded-string lint rule (┬π3.1 / Acceptance ┬π5):** root `eslint.config.mjs` gains an `apps/web/**/*.tsx` override έΑΦ `no-restricted-syntax` flags word-like `JSXText` (Latin OR Urdu letters) and hardcoded `placeholder`/`title`/`alt`/`aria-label` string literals, pointing devs to the catalog. It immediately caught a real hardcoded diagnostic string in `BrandManager.tsx` (fixed via a new interpolated `brandContrastDetail` key).
- **Verification gates (ALL GREEN):** typecheck **18/18**; lint **11/11** (incl. the new i18n rule; `@mp/shared` Urdu-script regex rewritten to `\u` escapes to clear `no-irregular-whitespace`); turbo build **11/11** (web `/settings` route + all shells compile; pages now SSR/dynamic because they read the locale cookie); jest έΑΦ **db 42/42** (7 suites; migration chain 01έΗΤ08 applies in pglite), **api 131/131** (18 suites; **+6** new `preferences.e2e.spec.ts`: 401 deny-by-default, staffέΗΤEN & patientέΗΤUR role defaults, explicit switch persists + echoes, audited-row assertion, 400 on unsupported language), **i18n 19/19** (3 suites: parity both-directions + non-trivial-size guard, formatLabel/translate, `detectAiLang`/`normalizeForAi` test set). **i18n parity gate: PASS** (ENέΗΦUR identical key sets) and is now a standing pipeline gate. Prettier: new code files formatted clean.
- **Acceptance mapping:** ┬π1 web renders EN+UR, switch persists (cookie+localStorage+account), UR is RTL with the Urdu font stack έΑΦ `/settings` + layout + provider. ┬π2 parity gate fails on a missing key in EITHER direction, passes when present έΑΦ `parity.spec` + wired into turbo `test`. ┬π3 `formatLabel` renders translated enum labels (no raw codes) in both languages έΑΦ `format-label.spec` + settings demo. ┬π4 `detectAiLang`/`normalizeForAi` classify EN, UR-script, Roman-UR on a test set έΑΦ `ai-lang.spec`. ┬π5 no hardcoded user-facing string in `apps/web` έΑΦ new lint rule green. ┬π6 Urdu font strategy (subset + swap + fallback) in place. ┬π7 gates green incl. parity; isolation έηΨ / prefs tenant-scoped.

### Notes / manual-run caveats (step 08)
- `prisma migrate deploy` against a live Postgres 16 is not runnable in the build sandbox; the `20260703150000_i18n_language` SQL is validated by executing the full 01έΗΤ08 chain inside pglite in the db isolation specs, and `prisma generate` succeeds. The `@mp/i18n` catalog JSON is emitted to `dist/messages` by tsc (`resolveJsonModule`) and verified present after build. Cross-device account sync (`GET /me/preferences` on mount) exercises the real endpoint; the local cookie/localStorage path works with no network. Reading the locale cookie opts the previously-static public pages into per-request SSR έΑΦ acceptable and standard; the real Lighthouse budget + any static-vs-dynamic tuning land with 13.

## Build-step 07 έΑΦ Foundation: Branding & White-Label

- **Work-type:** FEATURE (white-label theming/identity hooks every surface honors; always-on engine, never a flag). **Phase:** Foundation (item 7 of 39). **Branch:** `feat/07-branding-whitelabel` (stacked on `feat/06-audit-log`; controller merges to `staging` at checkpoint).
- **Depends on:** 02 (tenant resolver / RLS `apply_tenant_rls`), 04 (permission catalog έΑΦ `brand.manage` gates the editor), 06 (audit έΑΦ the update writes an `@Audited` row). Built before the feature modules so all of them theme correctly; 13 (`@mp/ui`) consumes the `--brand-*` contract heavily. **Date:** 2026-07-03.
- **Schema/migration:** NEW migration `20260703140000_branding_whitelabel`. Model `BrandingProfile` (`id @id cuid`, `tenantId @unique @map(tenant_id)`, `appName? @map(app_name)`, `logoKey? @map(logo_key)`, `iconKey? @map(icon_key)`, `faviconKey? @map(favicon_key)`, `themeTokens Json? @map(theme_tokens)`, `letterhead Json?`, `senderName? @map(sender_name)`, `poweredBy Boolean @default(true) @map(powered_by)`, `updatedBy? @map(updated_by)`, `updatedAt @updatedAt @map(updated_at)`; `@@map("branding_profile")`). One row per tenant. No new enum. Unique index `branding_profile_tenant_id_key`.
- **RLS (canonical):** `SELECT apply_tenant_rls('branding_profile')` έΑΦ tenant-scoped `tenant_isolation` (row visible/writable only under its own `app.tenant_id` GUC; WITH CHECK blocks writing another tenant's row; no context έΗΤ zero rows, fail-closed). T1's brand can never bleed into T2.
- **Feature-flags:** έηΨ none exposed έΑΦ branding is always-on infra (white-label theming/identity is never a capability toggle). Sits under the flag engine.
- **Do-NOT-break honored:** 02 tenant resolver untouched (branding resolves per tenant via `principal.tenantId` + RLS). `@mp/brand` resolve API + the `--brand-*` token contract kept stable and load-bearing for `@mp/ui`/layout; defaults stay the ┬π11 Marham Patti tokens. Global guard order (JwtέΗΤFeatureέΗΤRoles) preserved έΑΦ BrandModule adds no global guard/interceptor (writes ride the existing RolesGuard via `@RequirePermission('brand.manage')`). Dormant custom-domain path: safe/unused (no domain column/route added).
- **Problem:** Marham Patti is white-label έΑΦ a tenant must present as its own brand (name, logo, colours, letterhead, message sender, eventually its own domain). If branding isn't resolved centrally from the foundation, every module hard-codes "Marham Patti" teal and can't be white-labelled later without a rewrite. Ganatra (Full) uses the default brand, but overrides must work from day one.
- **What changed έΑΦ `@mp/brand` (extended the scaffold):** pure resolver + a11y guard, dependency-light (web + API import it). `BrandOverrides` (mirrors the row columns) + `ResolvedBrand extends BrandTheme` (adds `letterhead` + `poweredBy`). Extended `BrandIdentity` with `icon`/`favicon`. `resolveBrand(overrides?)` έΑΦ total merge over the ┬π11 default (colours patch, appName/logo/icon/favicon, `notificationSender` defaults to the overridden app name έΗΤ feeds 09, letterhead name defaults to app name/logo). `BRAND_COLOR_KEYS`, `isHexColor`, `sanitizeColorOverrides` (drops malformed/unknown tokens). **A11y contrast guard:** `relativeLuminance`/`contrastRatio` (WCAG 2.x sRGB), `checkBrandContrast(theme)` έΗΤ `ContrastWarning[]` over 4 load-bearing pairs (body text = ink/bg @4.5, secondary = slate/bg @4.5, primary button = white/brandTeal @3.0 large, surface = tealDeep/ice @4.5); `MIN_CONTRAST_AA=4.5`/`MIN_CONTRAST_AA_LARGE=3`. Default palette passes all (no false warning). `brandCssVars`/`brandCssVarString` kept (param widened to `Pick<BrandTheme,'colors'>` so `ResolvedBrand` passes through).
- **What changed έΑΦ API (`apps/api/src/brand/`):** `BrandService` έΑΦ `resolveFor(tenantId)` (row έΗΤ `resolveBrand`, CACHED per tenant, invalidated on write), `getProfile`, `updateProfile(tenantId, input, updatedBy)` (upsert έΗΤ bust cache έΗΤ resolve έΗΤ return `{profile, brand, warnings}`; warnings advisory, save still succeeds), `previewContrast(tokens)`. Repo seam `BrandRepo` (`get`/`upsert`, both via `runWithTenant`) + `PrismaBrandRepo` (JSON null handling, per-column partial update) + `FakeBrandRepo` (partial-merge semantics). `brand.dto.ts` hand-validates the body (present-keys-only partial; `null` clears; known hex tokens only; letterhead name/address/footer/logo). `BrandController` έΑΦ `GET /brand/me` (resolved brand + `--brand-*` cssVars; any authenticated user), `GET /brand/config` (raw row + contrast warnings; `brand.manage`), `PUT /brand` (`brand.manage`, `@Audited({action:'brand.update', entityType:'branding'})`), `GET /brand/letterhead` (letterhead sample for the 18/19/21 print templates). `BRAND_REPO` token; BrandModule exports `BrandService` (09 sender identity + print letterhead). Wired into AppModule; `@mp/brand` added to `apps/api` deps.
- **What changed έΑΦ web (EN+UR):** `apps/web/lib/brand.tsx` έΑΦ `BrandProvider` client (fetches `/brand/me`, sets `--brand-*` on `<html>`, sets `document.title` from app name; default first paint from the server-inlined tokens έΗΤ no unstyled flash; unauthenticated keeps defaults) + `useBrand`/`useBrandState`. Wired into `layout.tsx` wrapping children. `/admin/brand` έΑΦ `page.tsx` + `BrandManager.tsx` island (app name, sender, primary/accent colour pickers, letterhead address/footer, "Powered by" toggle; live client-side contrast preview mirroring the server guard + a letterhead/CTA live preview reskinned by the picked tokens; `brand.manage` 403 έΗΤ clean no-access). `globals.css` `.mp-brand-*` styles. New i18n keys: `brandTitle/brandIntro/brandAppName/brandSender/brandPrimary/brandAccent/brandPoweredBy/brandLetterhead/brandLhAddress/brandLhFooter/brandPreview/brandContrastWarn/noBrandAccess`. Full white-label editor deferred to 40.
- **Verification gates (ALL GREEN):** typecheck **16/16**; lint **10/10**; turbo build **10/10** (web `/admin/brand` route compiles, 5.78 kB); jest **db 42/42** (7 suites; **+4** new `branding-isolation.spec.ts`) + **api 125/125** (17 suites; **+20** new: `brand.service.spec.ts` unit έΑΦ default/override/cache/partial-merge/contrast/parity; `brand.e2e.spec.ts` έΑΦ 401/403 gating, default brand, override reskin + letterhead + sender, audited-row assertion, contrast warning, invalid/unknown-token 400). Prettier: new code files formatted clean. i18n parity EN+UR for all new keys.
- **Acceptance mapping:** ┬π1 no profile έΗΤ default Marham Patti identity + ┬π11 tokens (unit + e2e; default trips no contrast warning). ┬π2 override reskins `@mp/ui` (cssVars) + app name/PWA(title)/favicon(identity) with NO component change (BrandProvider + `/brand/me`; e2e asserts `--brand-teal` + appName flip). ┬π3 letterhead override appears on the print-sample endpoint + live preview. ┬π4 sender identity exposed via `resolvedBrand.identity.notificationSender` + exported `BrandService` (09 consumes; per-tenant WhatsApp number remains `[DECIDE AT BUILD]`). ┬π5 resolves per tenant via 02 (`principal.tenantId` + RLS); dormant custom-domain path unused/safe. ┬π6 inaccessible override έΗΤ contrast warning (service + e2e). ┬π7 gates green, i18n parity, BrandingProfile T1έΚιT2 isolation proven; white-label self-check now a standing gate for later UI steps.
- **Isolation proof (pglite, real 01έΗΤ07 migrations, non-superuser `app_user`):** a tenant sees only its own branding row; T1's override never bleeds into T2; WITH CHECK blocks writing another tenant's row; no context έΗΤ zero rows (fail-closed).

### Notes / manual-run caveats (step 07)
- `prisma migrate deploy` against a live Postgres 16 is not runnable in the build sandbox; the migration SQL is validated by executing it (01έΗΤ07) inside pglite in the isolation test, and `prisma generate` succeeds from the schema. Logo/icon/favicon asset KEYS resolve to bytes only once the R2/brand-asset serving pipeline exists (dormant); the resolver + identity plumbing are complete now so the app shell + print templates consume them with no code change when assets land. `document`-level favicon swap and PWA-manifest regeneration are wired conceptually via `identity.favicon`/`identity.icon` (applied by the app shell in 13); this step lands the resolver, contract, and default first-paint.

## Build-step 06 έΑΦ Foundation: Audit Log + Accountability

- **Work-type:** FEATURE (cross-cutting accountability έΑΦ the owner's #1 reason for buying; always-on, never a flag). **Phase:** Foundation (item 6 of 39). **Branch:** `feat/06-audit-log` (stacked on `feat/05-capabilities-flags`; controller merges to `staging` at checkpoint).
- **Depends on:** 02 (RLS/`apply_tenant_rls`, tenant ALS), 03 (auth principal έΑΦ absorbs its auth events), 04 (permission catalog έΑΦ `audit.view` gates the explorer). **Date:** 2026-07-03.
- **Schema/migration:** NEW migration `20260703130000_audit_log`. Model `AuditLog` (`id @id cuid`, `tenantId @map(tenant_id)`, `branchId? @map(branch_id)`, `actorId? @map(actor_id)`, `action`, `entityType? @map(entity_type)`, `entityId? @map(entity_id)`, `summary Json?`, `reason?`, `requestId? @map(request_id)`, `createdAt @map(created_at)`; indexes `[tenantId,createdAt]`, `[tenantId,entityType,entityId]`, `[tenantId,actorId]`; `@@map("audit_log")`). No new enum. Append-only by convention (app never updates/deletes rows).
- **RLS (BESPOKE έΑΦ not the canonical helper):** `audit_log` ENABLE+FORCE RLS with policy `audit_log_isolation`. USING (reads): `tenant_id = current_setting('app.tenant_id', true)` **OR** `current_setting('app.platform_scope', true) = 'on'` (the SUPER_ADMIN cross-tenant audit window). WITH CHECK (writes): strictly `tenant_id = current_setting('app.tenant_id', true)` έΑΦ platform scope does **not** widen writes, so a row can only ever be inserted for the caller's own tenant έΗΤ the trail is append-only + un-forgeable, and a normal tenant with neither context sees zero rows (fail-closed). New `@mp/db` seam `runAsPlatform(fn)` sets `app.platform_scope='on'` transaction-local WITHOUT setting the tenant GUC (reads across tenants; any write still fails WITH CHECK). New export `PLATFORM_GUC`.
- **Auth impact:** 03 `AuthEventService` absorbed into the durable trail έΑΦ now `@Optional()`-injects `AuditService` and, when the event carries a tenant, fire-and-forget routes it to `AuditService.record` as action `auth.<type>` (login ok/fail, lockout, mfa, 2FA enroll, refresh, reuse, reset, logout, patient OTP). Keeps the structured log line (belt-and-suspenders + tenant-less events). Unit tests that `new AuthEventService()` are unaffected (optional dep έΗΤ log-only). AuthModule now imports AuditModule.
- **Feature-flags:** έηΨ none exposed έΑΦ accountability is always-on infra (asserted by the 05 catalog test that excludes `audit`). Audit sits UNDER the flag engine: it records regardless of any capability being on/off.
- **Do-NOT-break honored:** `runWithTenant`/tenant ALS (02), auth principal (03), permission catalog (04) untouched. New `audit()` writer (`AuditService.write(tx, έΑο)`) + `StockMovement` shape are load-bearing and kept additive/stable. `apply_tenant_rls` reused for nothing here (bespoke policy) but left unchanged. Global guard order (JwtέΗΤFeatureέΗΤRoles) preserved έΑΦ the new global provider is an **interceptor** (`AuditInterceptor`), not a guard.
- **Problem:** the owner lost έΓ╣1έΑΥ1.5 lac to missing stock with no record of who did what, when. Accountability is the core promise: one reliable trail for every create/update/delete and sensitive read.
- **What changed έΑΦ `@mp/shared` (`audit.ts`):** `maskAuditSummary(value)` έΑΦ the single secret-masking barrier: recursively deep-copies a summary and masks any sensitive-named field (fragments `cnic/nationalid/password/secret/token/otp/code/pin/ssn`, case-insensitive substring) to `AUDIT_MASK='***'`, preserving null. `isSensitiveField`, `SENSITIVE_FIELD_FRAGMENTS`. `StockMovement` interface + `StockMovementType` (PURCHASE/SALE/RETURN/ADJUSTMENT/TRANSFER/WASTAGE/CONSUMPTION) + `STOCK_MOVEMENT_TYPES` + `describeStockMovement` έΑΦ the shape 20/28/29/30 emit (defined, not yet written) so every stock change ties to a user + reason.
- **What changed έΑΦ `@mp/db`:** `runAsPlatform(fn)` + `PLATFORM_GUC` (above).
- **What changed έΑΦ API (`apps/api/src/audit/`):** `AuditService` έΑΦ `write(tx, event)` (canonical `audit(tx,έΑο)`; atomic with caller's tenant txn), `record(event)` (own `runWithTenant`; for audited reads / auth events / auto-write; best-effort, swallows failures so auditing never breaks the primary op), `query(principal, filter)` (SUPER_ADMIN έΗΤ `runAsPlatform` across tenants, else own tenant), `exportCsv`/`toCsv` (RFC-4180, summary JSON-stringified, quotes doubled). Every write stamps actor/tenant/branch/requestId from `AuditContext` and masks the summary. Repo seam `AuditRepo` (`insert`/`insertScoped`/`query`) + `PrismaAuditRepo` + `FakeAuditRepo`. `AuditContext` ALS (`runInAuditContext`/`getAuditContext`) έΑΦ separate from tenancy ALS so it can also carry actorId/requestId. Global `AuditInterceptor` έΑΦ establishes the audit context per request (actor from `req.principal`, requestId from `x-request-id` or `randomUUID()`), and on an `@Audited({action, entityType})` route fires a masked auto-write on success (fire-and-forget). `@Audited` decorator + `AUDITED` metadata + `AUDIT_REPO` token. `AuditController` έΑΦ `GET /audit` (filter actor/entity/action/from/to/limit, `audit.view`), `GET /audit/export` (CSV headers, `audit.view`), `GET /audit/demo/reveal-cnic/:id` (`patients.cnic.reveal`; simulated sensitive read via `record()` proving the masked audited-read path end-to-end). `audit.dto.ts` hand-validates the query (limit clamp έΚν1000, date parse). AuditModule (global interceptor + exports AuditService); wired last in AppModule.
- **What changed έΑΦ UI (EN+UR):** `/admin/audit` έΑΦ `page.tsx` + `AuditExplorer.tsx` client island (filter by actor/entity/action/date, table of when/actor/action/entity, CSV export link to `/audit/export` with same filters; `audit.view` 403 έΗΤ clean no-access message). New i18n keys: `auditTitle/auditIntro/auditActor/auditEntity/auditAction/auditFrom/auditTo/auditWhen/auditFilter/auditExport/auditEmpty/noAuditAccess`. No Simple/Pro split at this layer (foundation surface; the `<DataList>`-driven polish lands with 13).
- **Verification gates (ALL GREEN):** typecheck **16/16**; lint **10/10**; turbo build **10/10** (web `/admin/audit` route compiles, 3.77 kB); jest **db 38/38** (6 suites; **+6** new `audit-isolation.spec.ts`) + **api 105/105** (15 suites; **+16** new: `audit.service.spec.ts` unit έΑΦ write/record/masking/scope/CSV; `audit.e2e.spec.ts` έΑΦ 401/403 gating, masked CNIC reveal, filters, CSV, SUPER_ADMIN-platform vs tenant scope). Prettier: all new code files clean.
- **Acceptance mapping:** ┬π1 mutation writes a tenant-scoped AuditLog row + reads back tenant-scoped (pglite + service tests). ┬π2 simulated CNIC reveal writes a row with `cnic` masked (`demo/reveal-cnic` e2e asserts `summary.cnic === '***'` and no `35202`). ┬π3 03 auth events flow through as `auth.<type>`. ┬π4 filters by actor/entity/action/date + CSV export; tenant sees only its own rows, SUPER_ADMIN spans tenants (e2e + pglite platform scope). ┬π5 masking test έΑΦ no raw secret/CNIC persisted. ┬π6 gates green, EN+UR, AuditLog T1/T2 isolation proven; flags έηΨ.
- **Isolation proof (pglite, real 01έΗΤ06 migrations, non-superuser `app_user`):** a tenant sees only its own rows; a tenant can write its own row; WITH CHECK blocks writing another tenant's row; no context έΗΤ zero rows; platform scope reads across every tenant; platform scope CANNOT write (append-only, un-forgeable).

### Notes / manual-run caveats (step 06)
- `prisma migrate deploy` against a live Postgres 16 is not runnable in the build sandbox; the migration SQL is validated by executing it (in order 01έΗΤ06) inside pglite in the isolation test, and `prisma generate` succeeds from the schema. `AuditInterceptor` auto-write and `record()` are fire-and-forget + failure-swallowing, so a DB blip never breaks a request or a login.

---

## Build-step 05 έΑΦ Foundation: Capabilities & Feature Flags

- **Work-type:** FEATURE (the always-on SaaS control layer; every later module gates on it). **Phase:** Foundation (item 5 of 39). **Branch:** `feat/05-capabilities-flags` (stacked on `feat/04-rbac-permissions`; controller merges to `staging` at checkpoint).
- **Depends on:** 02 (RLS/`apply_tenant_rls`), 04 (permissions έΑΦ flags gate BEFORE permissions). **Date:** 2026-07-03.
- **Schema/migration:** NEW migration `20260703120000_capabilities_flags`. Models: `FlagCatalog` (`key @id`, `group`, `defaultOn @map(default_on)`, `dependsOn Json @map(depends_on)`, `createdAt`; `@@map("flag_catalog")` έΑΦ GLOBAL, RLS-OFF), `TenantFlags` (`id @id cuid`, `tenantId @unique @map(tenant_id)`, `presetKey @map(preset_key)`, `overrides Json @default("{}")`, `updatedBy? @map(updated_by)`, `updatedAt @updatedAt @map(updated_at)`; `@@map("tenant_flags")`). No new enum (`presetKey`/`group` are String; `dependsOn`/`overrides` are JSONB). Unique index `tenant_flags_tenant_id_key`.
- **RLS:** `flag_catalog` = RLS-OFF global catalog (like `permissions` (04) and `tenants` (02)) έΑΦ read to render the admin UI + synced on boot before any tenant context. `tenant_flags` bound by the canonical `SELECT apply_tenant_rls('tenant_flags')` (02) έΗΤ a row is visible/writable only under its own `app.tenant_id`; T1 can neither see nor mutate T2's assignment; no-context = zero rows (fail-closed).
- **Feature-flags:** έεΖ **This step IS the flag engine.** `FLAGS` catalog = 21 sub-feature keys across groups pharmacy/lab/clinic/core/accounts/patient/ai, each with `defaultOn` (only `accounting.lite` defaults on) + `dependsOn` (e.g. `pharmacy.online`έΗΤ`pharmacy.pos`; `pharmacy.aiReader`έΗΤ`pharmacy.pos`+`ai.suite`; `lab.results`έΗΤ`lab.catalog`; `clinic.consultation`έΗΤ`clinic.appointments`; `patient.aiAssistant`έΗΤ`patient.app`+`ai.suite`; `ai.clinical`/`ai.ops`έΗΤ`ai.suite`). Vertical presets: `pharmacy`, `lab`, `clinic`, `clinic_pharmacy` (OPD+pharmacy, no lab), `full` (= EVERY key, derived so it never drifts). Ganatra Clinic seeded `full`.
- **Do-NOT-break honored:** permission catalog (04) untouched έΑΦ flags gate BEFORE permissions (`FeatureGuard` runs between `JwtAuthGuard` and `RolesGuard`), never instead of. `apply_tenant_rls` (02) reused unchanged. Catalog is ADDITIVE-ONLY (sync never deletes strays); boot hook crash-proof. `@mp/flags` scaffold public contract (`isFeatureEnabled(ctx,key)`, `VERTICAL_PRESETS`, `CapabilityContext`) kept stable + additive. No always-on infra added as a flag (asserted by test: none of `auth/rls/isolation/audit/offline/flags/branding/i18n/design/perf` in the catalog).

### Problem
Marham Patti is sold per vertical (Pharmacy / Lab / Clinic / Clinic+Pharmacy / Full) and AboveNext must control every capability per tenant at sub-feature granularity. Without a first-class flag engine in the foundation, every later module would hard-code "the clinic has a lab" and break the moment a pharmacy-only tenant is sold. The engine must exist BEFORE any feature module so all of them gate cleanly, and it must gate BEFORE RBAC (a disabled capability is invisible + forbidden regardless of role).

### What changed
- **`@mp/shared` (`flags.ts`):** framework-agnostic catalog + pure math. `FlagGroup`/`FlagDef`, `FLAGS` (21 keys), `FLAG_KEYS`, `getFlag`, `isKnownFlag`, `NEVER_FLAGS` (always-on infra, for the negative test), `resolveEffectiveFlags(presetKeys, overrides)` (layered: per-flag `defaultOn` έΗΤ preset turns ON έΗΤ overrides flip either way; total over the catalog), `findDependencyViolations(effective)` (every enabled flag's `dependsOn` parents must be on). Dependency-light (no Prisma/Nest) so API + web both import it. Barrel re-exports it.
- **`@mp/flags` (rewritten, scaffold contract preserved):** now depends on `@mp/shared`. Keeps `FlagKey`, `VERTICAL_PRESETS`, `VerticalPreset`, `CapabilityContext`, `isFeatureEnabled(ctx,key)`. Adds `isVerticalPreset`, `PRESETS` (Record<preset, keys[]>, `full`=`FLAG_KEYS`), `presetFlags`, `getEffectiveFlags(preset, overrides)` (delegates to shared), and re-exports the shared catalog helpers for a single import surface.
- **API `flags/` module:** `flags.constants.ts` (DI tokens `FLAG_CATALOG_REPO`/`TENANT_FLAGS_REPO`, `REQUIRE_FEATURE` key + `@RequireFeature(key)` decorator); `flags.repositories.ts` (`FlagCatalogRepo` on bare client έΑΦ global; `TenantFlagsRepo` inside `runWithTenant` έΑΦ tenant-scoped; JSON columns defensively coerced to `string[]`/`{key:boolean}`); `FlagService` (`onBoot`έΗΤcrash-proof `syncFlagCatalog` upsert-add/update; `getEffectiveFlagsFor` cached per tenant / invalidated on write; `isFeatureEnabled`; `getConfig`; `listCatalog`/`listPresets`; `setPreset`/`setOverride` έΑΦ validate preset/key against catalog + reject any resulting dependency violation, override requires a preset first); `FeatureGuard` (global APP_GUARD, opt-in `@RequireFeature`, **404 when off regardless of role**, skips `@Public`, fail-closed on no tenant); `FlagsController` (`GET flags/me` effective map, `GET flags/catalog` catalog+presets, admin `GET flags/config` + `PUT flags/preset` + `PUT flags/override` gated by NON_TENANT `@RequirePermission('flags.manage')` = SUPER_ADMIN, own-tenant scope; sample `GET flags/demo/pharmacy-online` = `@RequireFeature('pharmacy.online')` + `@RequirePermission('pharmacy.sell')`). `FlagsModule` wired into `AppModule` BETWEEN `AuthModule` and `PermissionsModule` so `FeatureGuard` runs after `JwtAuthGuard`, before `RolesGuard` (precedence: flag FIRST, then permission). `onApplicationBootstrap` runs the catalog sync (crash-proof).
- **Web:** `lib/feature.tsx` έΑΦ `FeatureProvider` (fetches `/flags/me` once with the stored token), `useFeature(key)`, `useFeatures()`, `<Feature flag fallback>` (keeps disabled capabilities out of the DOM entirely έΑΦ clean off-state, no orphan nav). `/admin/flags` έΑΦ lean SUPER_ADMIN island: assign a vertical preset + toggle per-capability overrides against `flags/catalog`+`flags/config`; server enforces `flags.manage` + dependency integrity, page hides controls a non-admin lacks. Route builds (`╞Τ /admin/flags`, 3.35 kB).
- **i18n keys added:** `flagsTitle`, `flagsIntro`, `presetLabel`, `assignPreset`, `capabilitiesLabel`, `noFlagsAccess` (EN+UR parity, enforced by the `satisfies Record<string,Dict>` type).
- **Seed:** Ganatra Clinic (Full suite) now upserts a `TenantFlags` row with `presetKey='full'` inside `runWithTenant` (idempotent; overrides preserved).

### Verification gates
- **typecheck:** 16/16 έεΖ  **lint:** 10/10 έεΖ (0 errors, 0 warnings)  **turbo build:** 10/10 έεΖ (`/admin/flags` route present).
- **jest:** `@mp/db` 32/32 (5 suites; +5 flag-isolation), `@mp/api` 89/89 (13 suites; +29 flags). Total 121/121.
  - **Flag engine unit (`flags.service.spec.ts`):** catalog-sync idempotency + additive-never-delete; crash-proof `onBoot`; NEVER_FLAGS absent from catalog (┬π6); Pharmacy preset = exactly the pharmacy set; Clinic+Pharmacy = OPD+pharmacy without lab; Full = every key; unknown-preset rejected; no-assignment έΗΤ defaults only; override flips effective set + busts cache; enabling a child w/o parent rejected (both directions έΑΦ also disabling a depended-on parent); override-before-preset rejected; unknown-key rejected; service math == `resolveEffectiveFlags`; every seeded preset dependency-consistent.
  - **Guard unit (`flag.guard.spec.ts`):** opt-in (no `@RequireFeature` έΘΤ allow); public route skips; 404 when off; pass when on; 404 fail-closed with no tenant.
  - **e2e wiring (`flags.e2e.spec.ts`, real module graph):** no token έΗΤ 401; flag OFF έΗΤ **404 as SUPER_ADMIN despite holding `pharmacy.sell`** (flag FIRST); `/flags/me` reflects off; `/flags/catalog` returns catalog+presets; `/flags/config` DOCTORέΗΤ403; after assigning `full`: flag ON έΗΤ SUPER_ADMIN 200 (RBAC decides after flag), DOCTOR 403 (flag passed, RBAC blocks), `/flags/me` shows on, SUPER_ADMIN reads `/flags/config`.
- **isolation (pglite, real 01έΗΤ05 migrations):** `flag_catalog` global readable with no context; `tenant_flags` shows only own row; WITH CHECK blocks a T1 write for T2; no-context έΗΤ zero rows; T1 preset έΚι T2 preset (flags isolated per tenant).
- **flag/vertical smoke:** preset resolution + precedence proven by the unit + e2e above.
- **i18n parity:** EN+UR both present (type-enforced). **Performance/Lighthouse:** έηΨ (admin island, deferred to the design/perf step). **White-label:** έηΨ.

### Notes
- Flag MANAGEMENT is platform-only (`flags.manage` is a NON_TENANT key held only by SUPER_ADMIN) and scoped to the caller's OWN tenant έΑΦ writes flow through `runWithTenant` cleanly. The rich cross-tenant SaaS console (managing any tenant's flags) is deferred to build-step 41.
- The pre-existing crash-proof-boot pattern (e.g. `auth.e2e` does not override the permission/flag repos, so boot logs a caught Prisma `DATABASE_URL` error) is unchanged and harmless έΑΦ `FlagsModule.onBoot` follows the same design.
- `prisma migrate deploy` against a live Postgres is not runnable in this sandbox; the migration SQL is validated end-to-end by the pglite isolation test running the real 01έΗΤ05 chain.
